# GitDelta Implementation Plan\n\n> **For agentic workers:** REQUIRED SUB-SKILL: Use superpowers:subagent-driven-development (recommended) or superpowers:executing-plans to implement this plan task-by-task. Steps use checkbox (`- [ ]`) syntax for tracking.\n\n**Goal:** Build GitDelta — a lightweight, native Windows 11, read-only Git diff/commit viewer with three compare modes (working tree vs HEAD, single commit vs parent, any two commits) and a CLI+GUI launch model.\n\n**Architecture:** Pure WPF / .NET 10 (org template flavor). `GitDelta.Core` (WPF-free classlib) wraps the git CLI behind `IGitReader` and computes intra-line diffs with DiffPlex; `GitDelta.UI` (`gitdelta.exe`) is a WPF-UI FluentWindow app with a 3-pane history-driven workspace and an AvalonEdit + TextMateSharp diff control. CommunityToolkit.Mvvm + Autofac/IHost throughout. Distributed as a framework-dependent single-file WinExe via a per-user Inno Setup installer that puts `gitdelta` on PATH.\n\n**Tech Stack:** .NET 10 · C# 14 · WPF-UI (lepoco) · CommunityToolkit.Mvvm · Autofac + Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting · AvalonEdit · DiffPlex · TextMateSharp · xUnit v3 + NSubstitute + Shouldly · git CLI · Inno Setup.\n\n**Source spec:** `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-05-29-gitdelta-design.md`\n\n**Phases:** 1 Scaffolding · 2 Core models/parsers · 3 Core git reader/diff · 4 Core CLI routing · 5 UI bootstrap/shell/theme · 6 ViewModels · 7 Diff control · 8 Syntax highlighting · 9 Workspace wiring/settings · 10 CLI console dual-mode · 11 Packaging.\n\n---\n## Phase 1: Solution Scaffolding & Build Config\n\nThis phase produces a compiling, warning-free, four-project .NET 10 solution that matches the GitDelta contract backbone: `GitDelta.Core` (WPF-free classlib), `GitDelta.UI` (the `gitdelta.exe` WPF app), and two xUnit v3 test projects. It also lays down the shared build config (`Directory.Build.props`, `Directory.Packages.props` with central, pinned versions), `.editorconfig`, `version.json`, `CLAUDE.md`, and a minimal-but-real WPF-UI `App` + `FluentWindow` shell so the engineer can run `dotnet build` and get zero warnings. The git repository already exists at `C:/code/projects/GitDelta` (with `.gitignore`); no `git init` is needed. The installed SDK is .NET 10 (`10.0.108`).\n\n> **No unit tests in this phase.** Everything here is scaffolding, MSBuild config, XAML, and App bootstrap — none of it is unit-testable logic. Each task therefore uses the "implementation + build verification + commit" form. TDD begins in the later Core-logic phases.\n\n### Task 1.1: Root build configuration files\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Build.props`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/.editorconfig`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/version.json`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Confirm prerequisites and the existing repo.** Run the following and confirm the .NET 10 SDK is listed and that the folder is already a git repo (it was created during spec setup).\n\n```powershell\ndotnet --list-sdks\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta status\n```\n\nExpected: `dotnet --list-sdks` includes a line beginning `10.0` (e.g. `10.0.108 [C:\Program Files\dotnet\sdk]`). `git status` reports `On branch ...` with `docs/`, `.gitignore`, etc. — confirming git is already initialized. If `dotnet --list-sdks` shows no `10.0.x` entry, stop and install the .NET 10 SDK before continuing.\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Write `Directory.Build.props`.** This centralizes the build flags for every project. `UseWPF` is deliberately NOT here — it belongs only in `GitDelta.UI.csproj` (and the UI unit-test project). `TargetFramework` is also NOT global, because Core targets `net10.0` (no WPF) while UI targets `net10.0-windows...`; each csproj sets its own. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Build.props`:\n\n```xml\n<Project>\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <Nullable>enable</Nullable>\n    <ImplicitUsings>enable</ImplicitUsings>\n    <LangVersion>14</LangVersion>\n    <TreatWarningsAsErrors>true</TreatWarningsAsErrors>\n    <EnableNETAnalyzers>true</EnableNETAnalyzers>\n    <AnalysisLevel>latest</AnalysisLevel>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Verify the latest stable package versions before pinning.** The backbone requires pinned versions. Before writing `Directory.Packages.props`, query the live feed for the latest stable of each "latest" package so the pins are real numbers, not guesses. Run:\n\n```powershell\n$pkgs = @(\n  'Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting','Autofac','Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection',\n  'CommunityToolkit.Mvvm','WPF-UI','WPF-UI.DependencyInjection','AvalonEdit','DiffPlex',\n  'TextMateSharp','TextMateSharp.Grammars','xunit.v3','xunit.runner.visualstudio',\n  'Microsoft.NET.Test.Sdk','NSubstitute','Shouldly','coverlet.collector'\n)\nforeach ($p in $pkgs) {\n  $u = "https://api.nuget.org/v3-flatcontainer/$($p.ToLower())/index.json"\n  try {\n    $v = (Invoke-RestMethod $u).versions | Where-Object { $_ -notmatch '-' } | Select-Object -Last 1\n    "{0,-42} {1}" -f $p, $v\n  } catch { "{0,-42} (lookup failed: {1})" -f $p, $_.Exception.Message }\n}\n```\n\nExpected: one line per package with its newest stable version, e.g. `Autofac   8.x.x`, `WPF-UI   4.x.x`, `xunit.v3   3.x.x`. Record these. **Pin the exact versions you observe** for the "latest" packages in the next step. For the spec-fixed packages, keep these exact pins regardless of newer releases: `AvalonEdit` = `6.3.1.120`, `DiffPlex` = `1.9.x` (use the newest `1.9.*` stable from the lookup, e.g. `1.9.0`), `TextMateSharp` and `TextMateSharp.Grammars` = `2.0.3`. If a lookup line says `(lookup failed: ...)`, you are offline — fall back to the versions written in the template below and revisit before the final build.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Write `Directory.Packages.props` with central package management.** Replace each version below with the exact stable version observed in Step 3 where it differs (the spec-fixed pins for AvalonEdit/DiffPlex/TextMateSharp must stay as shown). Central management requires `ManagePackageVersionsCentrally=true`; csproj files will reference packages with NO `Version=` attribute. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`:\n\n```xml\n<Project>\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <ManagePackageVersionsCentrally>true</ManagePackageVersionsCentrally>\n    <CentralPackageTransitivePinningEnabled>true</CentralPackageTransitivePinningEnabled>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n\n  <!-- MVVM / DI / Hosting -->\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageVersion Include="CommunityToolkit.Mvvm" Version="8.4.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="Autofac" Version="8.4.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection" Version="10.0.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting" Version="10.0.0" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <!-- UI / Fluent -->\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageVersion Include="WPF-UI" Version="4.2.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="WPF-UI.DependencyInjection" Version="4.2.0" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <!-- Diff / editor / syntax -->\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageVersion Include="AvalonEdit" Version="6.3.1.120" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="DiffPlex" Version="1.9.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="TextMateSharp" Version="2.0.3" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="TextMateSharp.Grammars" Version="2.0.3" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <!-- Testing -->\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageVersion Include="Microsoft.NET.Test.Sdk" Version="17.14.1" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="xunit.v3" Version="3.0.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="xunit.runner.visualstudio" Version="3.1.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="NSubstitute" Version="5.3.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="Shouldly" Version="4.3.0" />\n    <PackageVersion Include="coverlet.collector" Version="6.0.4" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Write `.editorconfig`.** This is the org-standard style file (file-scoped namespaces, 4-space C#, 2-space XAML, CRLF). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/.editorconfig`:\n\n```ini\n# .editorconfig\nroot = true\n\n[*]\nindent_style = space\nindent_size = 4\nend_of_line = crlf\ncharset = utf-8-bom\ntrim_trailing_whitespace = true\ninsert_final_newline = true\n\n[*.{xml,xaml,csproj,props,targets}]\nindent_size = 2\n\n[*.cs]\n# File-scoped namespaces\ncsharp_style_namespace_declarations = file_scoped:warning\n\n# var preferences\ncsharp_style_var_for_built_in_types = false:suggestion\ncsharp_style_var_when_type_is_apparent = true:suggestion\ncsharp_style_var_elsewhere = false:suggestion\n\n# Expression-bodied members\ncsharp_style_expression_bodied_methods = when_on_single_line:suggestion\ncsharp_style_expression_bodied_constructors = false:suggestion\ncsharp_style_expression_bodied_properties = true:suggestion\ncsharp_style_expression_bodied_accessors = true:suggestion\ncsharp_style_expression_bodied_lambdas = true:suggestion\n\n# Pattern matching\ncsharp_style_prefer_switch_expression = true:suggestion\ncsharp_style_prefer_pattern_matching = true:suggestion\n\n# Null checking\ncsharp_style_prefer_null_check_over_type_check = true:suggestion\ndotnet_style_coalesce_expression = true:suggestion\ndotnet_style_null_propagation = true:suggestion\n\n# Naming: PascalCase for public members\ndotnet_naming_rule.public_members_must_be_pascal_case.symbols = public_symbols\ndotnet_naming_rule.public_members_must_be_pascal_case.style = pascal_case_style\ndotnet_naming_rule.public_members_must_be_pascal_case.severity = warning\ndotnet_naming_symbols.public_symbols.applicable_kinds = property,method,event\ndotnet_naming_symbols.public_symbols.applicable_accessibilities = public\ndotnet_naming_style.pascal_case_style.capitalization = pascal_case\n\n# Naming: _camelCase for private fields\ndotnet_naming_rule.private_fields_must_be_underscore_camel.symbols = private_fields\ndotnet_naming_rule.private_fields_must_be_underscore_camel.style = underscore_camel_style\ndotnet_naming_rule.private_fields_must_be_underscore_camel.severity = warning\ndotnet_naming_symbols.private_fields.applicable_kinds = field\ndotnet_naming_symbols.private_fields.applicable_accessibilities = private\ndotnet_naming_style.underscore_camel_style.capitalization = camel_case\ndotnet_naming_style.underscore_camel_style.required_prefix = _\n\n# Using directives\ndotnet_sort_system_directives_first = true\ncsharp_using_directive_placement = outside_namespace:warning\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Write `version.json`.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/version.json`:\n\n```json\n{\n  "major": 0,\n  "minor": 1,\n  "patch": 0\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Commit the root build config.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add Directory.Build.props Directory.Packages.props .editorconfig version.json\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nchore: add root build configuration (Directory.Build.props, central package versions, editorconfig, version.json)\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\nExpected: one commit recorded with four files changed.\n\n---\n\n### Task 1.2: Create the four projects and the solution\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Scaffold the four projects and the solution with the .NET CLI.** This creates default csproj/sln files that the next steps overwrite or adjust. Using the CLI guarantees valid project GUIDs and correct solution wiring. Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet new sln -n GitDelta -o C:/code/projects/GitDelta\ndotnet new classlib -n GitDelta.Core      -o C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core      --framework net10.0\ndotnet new wpf       -n GitDelta.UI        -o C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI        --framework net10.0\ndotnet new classlib  -n GitDelta.Core.Tests   -o C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests   --framework net10.0\ndotnet new classlib  -n GitDelta.UI.UnitTests -o C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests --framework net10.0\n```\n\nExpected: each command prints `The template "..." was created successfully.` The `dotnet new wpf` command also generates `App.xaml`, `App.xaml.cs`, `MainWindow.xaml`, `MainWindow.xaml.cs`, and `AssemblyInfo.cs` under `src/GitDelta.UI/` — these defaults will be replaced in Tasks 1.5–1.6.\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Delete the default `Class1.cs` files the templates created.** They are placeholders that would otherwise clutter the projects. Run:\n\n```powershell\nRemove-Item C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Class1.cs -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue\nRemove-Item C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Class1.cs -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue\nRemove-Item C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Class1.cs -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue\n```\n\nExpected: no output (files removed or already absent).\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Overwrite `GitDelta.Core.csproj`.** Core is a WPF-free classlib targeting `net10.0`. It pulls in CommunityToolkit.Mvvm (used for `ObservableObject` only where shared) plus DiffPlex; per the backbone, MVVM ViewModels live in UI, but DiffPlex (`DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer`) lives in Core. The build flags come from `Directory.Build.props`; versions come from `Directory.Packages.props`. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj`:\n\n```xml\n<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk">\n\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <TargetFramework>net10.0</TargetFramework>\n    <RootNamespace>GitDelta.Core</RootNamespace>\n    <AssemblyName>GitDelta.Core</AssemblyName>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageReference Include="DiffPlex" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Overwrite `GitDelta.UI.csproj`.** The UI project is the `gitdelta.exe` entry point: `WinExe`, WPF on, Windows TFM, output assembly named `gitdelta` (lowercase, per backbone), root namespace `GitDelta.UI`. It references Core and the UI packages. Single-file publish settings live here but only affect `dotnet publish` (a later phase); they are harmless for `dotnet build`. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`:\n\n```xml\n<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk">\n\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <OutputType>WinExe</OutputType>\n    <TargetFramework>net10.0-windows10.0.26100.0</TargetFramework>\n    <UseWPF>true</UseWPF>\n    <RootNamespace>GitDelta.UI</RootNamespace>\n    <AssemblyName>gitdelta</AssemblyName>\n    <ApplicationManifest>app.manifest</ApplicationManifest>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageReference Include="WPF-UI" />\n    <PackageReference Include="WPF-UI.DependencyInjection" />\n    <PackageReference Include="CommunityToolkit.Mvvm" />\n    <PackageReference Include="Autofac" />\n    <PackageReference Include="Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection" />\n    <PackageReference Include="Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting" />\n    <PackageReference Include="AvalonEdit" />\n    <PackageReference Include="TextMateSharp" />\n    <PackageReference Include="TextMateSharp.Grammars" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <ProjectReference Include="..\GitDelta.Core\GitDelta.Core.csproj" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Overwrite `GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj`.** xUnit v3 test project referencing Core, targeting `net10.0`. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj`:\n\n```xml\n<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk">\n\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <TargetFramework>net10.0</TargetFramework>\n    <IsPackable>false</IsPackable>\n    <IsTestProject>true</IsTestProject>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageReference Include="Microsoft.NET.Test.Sdk" />\n    <PackageReference Include="xunit.v3" />\n    <PackageReference Include="xunit.runner.visualstudio" />\n    <PackageReference Include="NSubstitute" />\n    <PackageReference Include="Shouldly" />\n    <PackageReference Include="coverlet.collector" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <ProjectReference Include="..\..\src\GitDelta.Core\GitDelta.Core.csproj" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Overwrite `GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj`.** Tests for ViewModels reference the UI project; because the UI project uses WPF types, the test project must set `UseWPF` and the Windows TFM. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj`:\n\n```xml\n<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk">\n\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <TargetFramework>net10.0-windows10.0.26100.0</TargetFramework>\n    <UseWPF>true</UseWPF>\n    <IsPackable>false</IsPackable>\n    <IsTestProject>true</IsTestProject>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <PackageReference Include="Microsoft.NET.Test.Sdk" />\n    <PackageReference Include="xunit.v3" />\n    <PackageReference Include="xunit.runner.visualstudio" />\n    <PackageReference Include="NSubstitute" />\n    <PackageReference Include="Shouldly" />\n    <PackageReference Include="coverlet.collector" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n  <ItemGroup>\n    <ProjectReference Include="..\..\src\GitDelta.UI\GitDelta.UI.csproj" />\n  </ItemGroup>\n\n</Project>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Add all four projects to the solution under `src/` and `tests/` solution folders.** The `--solution-folder` flag groups them the way the template prescribes. Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet sln C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln add C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj --solution-folder src\ndotnet sln C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln add C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj --solution-folder src\ndotnet sln C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln add C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --solution-folder tests\ndotnet sln C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln add C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --solution-folder tests\n```\n\nExpected: four `Project ... added to the solution.` messages.\n\n- [x] **Step 8: Restore packages to confirm the central-version pins resolve.** This validates `Directory.Packages.props`. Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet restore C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln\n```\n\nExpected: `Restored ...` for all four projects with no `NU1605`/`NU1101`/`NU1008` errors. If you see `NU1008` ("Projects that use central package version management should not define the version on the PackageReference"), a csproj still has a stray `Version=` attribute — remove it. If you see `NU1102` ("Unable to find package ... with version ..."), the pinned version in `Directory.Packages.props` does not exist on the feed — correct it to a real version from Task 1.1 Step 3.\n\n- [x] **Step 9: Commit the projects and solution.** Note this will not yet build (the UI still has default `dotnet new wpf` files referencing the wrong namespace and lacking WPF-UI wiring — fixed in Tasks 1.4–1.6). Committing the structure first keeps history granular. Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src tests GitDelta.sln\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nchore: scaffold solution with Core, UI, and two xUnit v3 test projects\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\nExpected: one commit with the csproj files, solution, and the default WPF source files added.\n\n---\n\n### Task 1.3: Project documentation (CLAUDE.md)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/CLAUDE.md`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write `CLAUDE.md` from the Pure-WPF block of the org claude-md-template.** Fill in every placeholder for GitDelta and keep the Pure-WPF architecture bullets (drop the Hybrid bullets). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/CLAUDE.md`:\n\n```markdown\n# CLAUDE.md\n\n## Project Overview\n\nGitDelta is a lightweight, native Windows 11, read-only Git diff and commit viewer (Pure WPF, .NET 10). It shows working-tree-vs-HEAD, single-commit-vs-parent, and any-two-commit diffs with a modern Fluent UI. It is NOT a Git client: no staging, committing, or any write operation. Architecture: **Pure WPF**.\n\n## Build & Run\n\n```shell\ndotnet build GitDelta.sln\ndotnet test tests/\ndotnet run --project src/GitDelta.UI/\n```\n\nThe published executable is named `gitdelta.exe` (AssemblyName `gitdelta` in `GitDelta.UI.csproj`).\n\n## Architecture\n\n**Type:** Pure WPF\n\n- `src/GitDelta.Core` — WPF-free classlib (`net10.0`): `IGitReader`/`CliGitReader`, git output parsers, `IIntraLineDiffer` (DiffPlex), repo discovery, CLI arg routing, settings persistence, domain models.\n- `src/GitDelta.UI` — WPF exe (`net10.0-windows10.0.26100.0`, `gitdelta.exe`): App bootstrap + CLI arg routing + global exception handlers, FluentWindow shell with a 3-pane workspace, start screen, ViewModels, and the AvalonEdit-based DiffView control.\n- MVVM with CommunityToolkit.Mvvm source generators\n- Autofac DI with Module pattern (one module per layer)\n- IHost bootstrapping with AutofacServiceProviderFactory\n- WPF-UI FluentWindow with Mica/Acrylic backdrop\n\n**Layering:** `UI -> Core`; Core never references UI. Services are `SingleInstance`; ViewModels are `InstancePerDependency`. Constructor injection only.\n\n**Reference template:** `C:/code/template-projects/desktop-development-template/wpf-development-template.md`\n\n## Git access\n\nGitDelta shells out to the `git` CLI (no LibGit2Sharp) via `IGitProcessRunner`. Requires Git for Windows >= 2.30 on PATH. All path-bearing git output uses `-z` (NUL-framed) with `-c core.quotepath=false` and `--no-optional-locks`.\n\n## Key Conventions\n\n- File-scoped namespaces\n- Private fields: `_camelCase`, public members: PascalCase\n- Test naming: `MethodName_Scenario_ExpectedResult`\n- No logic in View code-behind — all in ViewModels\n- Constructor injection only — no service locator\n- `ConfigureAwait(false)` in Core/library code; never `.Result`/`.Wait()` on the UI thread\n- No `async void` except event handlers\n- `DynamicResource` for all theme colors (never StaticResource or hardcoded hex)\n- 4 spaces C#, 2 spaces XAML/XML/csproj, CRLF line endings\n\n## Testing\n\n- xUnit v3 + NSubstitute + Shouldly\n- Run: `dotnet test tests/`\n- Core: parsers, diff enrichment, repo discovery, CLI arg routing (canned git output).\n- UI: ViewModel behavior with `IGitReader` mocked. No tests against live AvalonEdit.\n\n## Environment\n\n- .NET 10 SDK\n- Windows 11 SDK (10.0.26100)\n- Git for Windows >= 2.30 on PATH (runtime dependency)\n\n## Build Gate\n\n`dotnet build` must produce zero warnings (`TreatWarningsAsErrors=true`), and `dotnet test tests/` must pass before every commit.\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Commit the documentation.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add CLAUDE.md\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\ndocs: add CLAUDE.md project guidance\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\nExpected: one commit with `CLAUDE.md`.\n\n---\n\n### Task 1.4: Application manifest and assembly info\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/app.manifest`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/AssemblyInfo.cs`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Add an application manifest declaring Windows 11 / per-monitor-v2 DPI awareness.** WPF-UI Mica and crisp rendering on high-DPI displays require this. `GitDelta.UI.csproj` already points `<ApplicationManifest>` at `app.manifest` (Task 1.2 Step 4). Verification is a build, then a manual run in Task 1.7.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Overwrite `App.xaml`.** Remove the default `StartupUri` (the host will create the window in later phases; for this scaffold App.xaml.cs shows the window directly). Merge the WPF-UI `ThemesDictionary` and `ControlsDictionary` so Fluent controls and theme brushes resolve. Wire `DispatcherUnhandledException` to a handler. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`:\n\n```xml\n<Application\n    x:Class="GitDelta.UI.App"\n    xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"\n    xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"\n    xmlns:ui="http://schemas.lepo.co/wpfui/2022/xaml"\n    DispatcherUnhandledException="OnDispatcherUnhandledException">\n\n    <Application.Resources>\n        <ResourceDictionary>\n            <ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>\n                <ui:ThemesDictionary Theme="Dark" />\n                <ui:ControlsDictionary />\n            </ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>\n        </ResourceDictionary>\n    </Application.Resources>\n\n</Application>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Overwrite `App.xaml.cs` with a minimal, real bootstrap.** This scaffold version directly constructs and shows `MainWindow` so the app runs end-to-end; it also wires the three global exception handlers the spec mandates (`DispatcherUnhandledException` in XAML, plus `AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException` and `TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException` here). The full IHost/Autofac/CLI-routing bootstrap is layered in during a later phase; the `using` for `Wpf.Ui.Appearance` lets us follow the system theme. Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Windows;\nusing System.Windows.Threading;\nusing GitDelta.UI.Views;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI;\n\npublic partial class App : Application\n{\n    protected override void OnStartup(StartupEventArgs e)\n    {\n        AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += OnDomainUnhandledException;\n        TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException += OnUnobservedTaskException;\n\n        base.OnStartup(e);\n\n        var mainWindow = new MainWindow();\n        mainWindow.Show();\n    }\n\n    private static void OnDomainUnhandledException(object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)\n    {\n        if (e.ExceptionObject is Exception ex)\n        {\n            MessageBox.Show(\n                $"An unexpected error occurred: {ex.Message}",\n                "GitDelta",\n                MessageBoxButton.OK,\n                MessageBoxImage.Error);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static void OnUnobservedTaskException(object? sender, UnobservedTaskExceptionEventArgs e)\n    {\n        e.SetObserved();\n    }\n\n    private void OnDispatcherUnhandledException(object sender, DispatcherUnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)\n    {\n        MessageBox.Show(\n            $"An unexpected error occurred: {e.Exception.Message}",\n            "GitDelta",\n            MessageBoxButton.OK,\n            MessageBoxImage.Error);\n\n        e.Handled = true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Commit the App bootstrap.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): minimal App bootstrap with WPF-UI theme dictionaries and global exception handlers\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\nExpected: one commit with the two files.\n\n---\n\n### Task 1.6: Placeholder FluentWindow shell (MainWindow)\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/MainWindow.xaml`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/MainWindow.xaml.cs`\n\n> Not unit-testable (XAML view + window code-behind). `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Models/ModelDefaultsTests.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Models;\n\npublic class ModelDefaultsTests\n{\n    [Fact]\n    public void CommitInfo_TwoParents_IsMergeTrue_IsRootFalse()\n    {\n        var commit = new CommitInfo(\n            Sha: "abc123def456",\n            ShortSha: "abc123d",\n            Parents: ["p1", "p2"],\n            AuthorName: "Ann",\n            AuthorEmail: "ann@example.com",\n            AuthorDate: DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch,\n            CommitterName: "Ann",\n            CommitterEmail: "ann@example.com",\n            CommitDate: DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch,\n            Subject: "Merge",\n            Body: "");\n\n        commit.IsMerge.ShouldBeTrue();\n        commit.IsRoot.ShouldBeFalse();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void CommitInfo_NoParents_IsRootTrue_IsMergeFalse()\n    {\n        var commit = new CommitInfo(\n            Sha: "root",\n            ShortSha: "root",\n            Parents: [],\n            AuthorName: "Ann",\n            AuthorEmail: "ann@example.com",\n            AuthorDate: DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch,\n            CommitterName: "Ann",\n            CommitterEmail: "ann@example.com",\n            CommitDate: DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch,\n            Subject: "Initial",\n            Body: "");\n\n        commit.IsRoot.ShouldBeTrue();\n        commit.IsMerge.ShouldBeFalse();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void ChangedFile_Rename_CarriesOldPath()\n    {\n        var file = new ChangedFile(\n            Path: "new/name.cs",\n            OldPath: "old/name.cs",\n            Kind: ChangeKind.Renamed,\n            AddedLines: 2,\n            DeletedLines: 1,\n            IsBinary: false);\n\n        file.OldPath.ShouldBe("old/name.cs");\n        file.Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Renamed);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void DiffLine_DefaultsCanCarryEmptyIntraSpans()\n    {\n        var line = new DiffLine(\n            Kind: DiffLineKind.Context,\n            OldLineNumber: 1,\n            NewLineNumber: 1,\n            Text: "unchanged",\n            IntraSpans: []);\n\n        line.IntraSpans.ShouldBeEmpty();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void AppSettings_Defaults_MatchSpec()\n    {\n        var settings = new AppSettings();\n\n        settings.Theme.ShouldBe(AppTheme.System);\n        settings.DefaultDiffView.ShouldBe(DiffViewMode.SideBySide);\n        settings.ContextLines.ShouldBe(3);\n        settings.TabSize.ShouldBe(4);\n        settings.SyntaxHighlighting.ShouldBeTrue();\n        settings.ExternalEditorCommand.ShouldBeNull();\n        settings.WindowWidth.ShouldBe(1100);\n        settings.WindowHeight.ShouldBe(720);\n        settings.HistoryPaneWidth.ShouldBe(280);\n        settings.FilesPaneWidth.ShouldBe(260);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void AppSettings_WithExpression_OverridesSingleProperty()\n    {\n        var settings = new AppSettings { Theme = AppTheme.Dark };\n\n        settings.Theme.ShouldBe(AppTheme.Dark);\n        settings.TabSize.ShouldBe(4);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the test; expect a compile failure (no models yet).** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test OldPath,\n    ChangeKind Kind,\n    int? AddedLines,\n    int? DeletedLines,\n    bool IsBinary);\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Create the diff model records and enums.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Models/DiffModels.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\npublic enum DiffLineKind\n{\n    Context,\n    Added,\n    Deleted\n}\n\npublic enum IntraSpanKind\n{\n    Added,\n    Deleted\n}\n\npublic sealed record IntraSpan(int Start, int Length, IntraSpanKind Kind);\n\npublic sealed record DiffLine(\n    DiffLineKind Kind,\n    int? For a root commit, the empty tree is the base.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static IReadOnlyList<string> ToDiffArgs(DiffSpec spec, bool isRootCommit) => spec switch\n    {\n        DiffSpec.WorkingTreeVsHead => ["HEAD"],\n        DiffSpec.CommitVsParent c when isRootCommit => [GitConstants.EmptyTreeSha, c.Sha],\n        DiffSpec.CommitVsParent c => [c.Sha + "^", c.Sha],\n        DiffSpec.TwoCommits t => [t.BaseSha, t.TargetSha],\n        _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(spec), spec, "Unknown DiffSpec variant.")\n    };\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; `DiffSpecArgsTests` (5) and `GitResultTests` (2) all pass alongside Task 2.1's tests.\n\n- [x] **Step 8: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add GitConstants, GitResult, DiffSpec and DiffSpecArgs\n\nAdd the empty-tree SHA constant, the process-result record, the\nDiffSpec discriminated union (working-tree/commit-vs-parent/two-commits)\nand the DiffSpecArgs ref-mapping helper, with tests for each variant\nincluding the root-commit empty-tree case.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.3: `IGitProcessRunner` and the real `GitProcessRunner`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/IGitProcessRunner.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/GitProcessRunner.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/GitProcessRunnerTests.cs`\n\n`GitProcessRunner` actually launches `git`, so it is an integration-style test. We cannot unit-test it with a mock (it *is* the thing that touches the process). We test it against a real, freshly-created temp repo so the asserts are deterministic. Git is required on the build/test machine (the spec already mandates this).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests against a real temp repo.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/GitProcessRunnerTests.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Git;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git;\n\npublic sealed class GitProcessRunnerTests : IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly string _repoDir;\n\n    public GitProcessRunnerTests()\n    {\n        _repoDir = Path.Combine(Path.GetTempPath(), "gitdelta-runner-" + Guid.NewGuid().ToString("N"));\n        Directory.CreateDirectory(_repoDir);\n        RunGitDirect("init -q");\n        RunGitDirect("config user.email test@example.com");\n        RunGitDirect("config user.name Test");\n    }\n\n    public void Dispose()\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            // .git holds read-only pack files on Windows; clear the bit before deleting.\n            foreach (var file in Directory.EnumerateFiles(_repoDir, "*", SearchOption.AllDirectories))\n            {\n                File.SetAttributes(file, FileAttributes.Normal);\n            }\n            Directory.Delete(_repoDir, recursive: true);\n        }\n        catch\n        {\n            // Best-effort cleanup; a leaked temp dir must not fail the suite.\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void RunGitDirect(string args)\n    {\n        var psi = new ProcessStartInfo("git", args)\n        {\n            WorkingDirectory = _repoDir,\n            RedirectStandardOutput = true,\n            RedirectStandardError = true,\n            UseShellExecute = false\n        };\n        using var process = Process.Start(psi)!;\n        process.WaitForExit();\n        process.ExitCode.ShouldBe(0, $"git {args} failed: {process.StandardError.ReadToEnd()}");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task RunAsync_Version_ReturnsSuccessAndVersionText()\n    {\n        var runner = new GitProcessRunner();\n\n        var result = await runner.RunAsync(_repoDir, ["--version"], TestContext.Current.CancellationToken);\n\n        result.Success.ShouldBeTrue();\n        Encoding.UTF8.GetString(result.StdOut).ShouldStartWith("git version");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task RunAsync_StdOut_IsRawBytes_PreservingNulFraming()\n    {\n        File.WriteAllText(Path.Combine(_repoDir, "a.txt"), "hi\n");\n        RunGitDirect("add a.txt");\n        RunGitDirect("commit -q -m first");\n        var runner = new GitProcessRunner();\n\n        // -z makes git emit NUL-terminated records; raw bytes must keep the 0x00.\n        var result = await runner.RunAsync(\n            _repoDir, ["log", "--pretty=format:%H", "-z"], TestContext.Current.CancellationToken);\n\n        result.Success.ShouldBeTrue();\n        result.StdOut.ShouldContain((byte)0x00);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task RunAsync_FailedCommand_ReturnsNonZeroExitAndStdErr()\n    {\n        var runner = new GitProcessRunner();\n\n        var result = await runner.RunAsync(\n            _repoDir, ["cat-file", "-p", "doesnotexist"], TestContext.Current.CancellationToken);\n\n        result.Success.ShouldBeFalse();\n        result.ExitCode.ShouldNotBe(0);\n        result.StdErr.ShouldNotBeEmpty();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task RunAsync_AlreadyCancelledToken_ThrowsOperationCanceled()\n    {\n        var runner = new GitProcessRunner();\n        using var cts = new CancellationTokenSource();\n        await cts.CancelAsync();\n\n        await Should.ThrowAsync<OperationCanceledException>(\n            async () => await runner.RunAsync(_repoDir, ["--version"], cts.Token));\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the tests; expect compile failure.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: build FAILS with `CS0246` for `GitProcessRunner` / `IGitProcessRunner`. Red state.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the interface.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/IGitProcessRunner.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git;\n\npublic interface IGitProcessRunner\n{\n    Task<GitResult> RunAsync(string workingDirectory, IReadOnlyList<string> args, CancellationToken ct);\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Create the real implementation.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/GitProcessRunner.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.Text;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Runs the git CLI as a child process. stdout is captured as raw bytes (so NUL/0x1f\n/// framing and non-UTF-8 paths survive), stderr is decoded as UTF-8. Every invocation\n/// is prefixed with read-only/quoting flags. Cancellation kills the process tree.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class GitProcessRunner : IGitProcessRunner\n{\n    public async Task<GitResult> RunAsync(string workingDirectory, IReadOnlyList<string> args, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n        var psi = new ProcessStartInfo("git")\n        {\n            WorkingDirectory = workingDirectory,\n            RedirectStandardOutput = true,\n            RedirectStandardError = true,\n            UseShellExecute = false,\n            CreateNoWindow = true,\n            StandardErrorEncoding = Encoding.UTF8\n        };\n\n        // Read-only safety + stable path quoting, prepended before the caller's args.\n        psi.ArgumentList.Add("-c");\n        psi.ArgumentList.Add("core.quotepath=false");\n        psi.ArgumentList.Add("--no-optional-locks");\n        foreach (var arg in args)\n        {\n            psi.ArgumentList.Add(arg);\n        }\n\n        using var process = new Process { StartInfo = psi };\n        process.Start();\n\n        using var stdOutBuffer = new MemoryStream();\n\n        // Drain stdout as raw bytes and stderr as UTF-8 text concurrently to avoid\n        // pipe-buffer deadlock on large outputs.\n        var stdOutTask = process.StandardOutput.BaseStream.CopyToAsync(stdOutBuffer, ct);\n        var stdErrTask = process.StandardError.ReadToEndAsync(ct);\n\n        try\n        {\n            await Task.WhenAll(stdOutTask, stdErrTask).ConfigureAwait(false);\n            await process.WaitForExitAsync(ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n        catch (OperationCanceledException)\n        {\n            TryKill(process);\n            throw;\n        }\n\n        var stdErr = await stdErrTask.ConfigureAwait(false);\n        return new GitResult(process.ExitCode, stdOutBuffer.ToArray(), stdErr);\n    }\n\n    private static void TryKill(Process process)\n    {\n        try\n        {\n            if (!process.HasExited)\n            {\n                process.Kill(entireProcessTree: true);\n            }\n        }\n        catch\n        {\n            // Process may have already exited between the check and the kill.\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; the 4 `GitProcessRunnerTests` pass. (These shell out to real git; the temp repo is created and cleaned per test class.)\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/IGitProcessRunner.cs src/GitDelta.Core/Git/GitProcessRunner.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/GitProcessRunnerTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add IGitProcessRunner and real GitProcessRunner\n\nShell out to git with raw-byte stdout, UTF-8 stderr, prepended\n-c core.quotepath=false and --no-optional-locks, deadlock-free\nconcurrent stream draining, and cancellation that kills the process\ntree. Covered by integration tests against a real temp repo.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.4: `GitLogParser`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/GitLogParser.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/GitLogParserTests.cs`\n\nThe log format is `--pretty=format:%H%x1f%P%x1f%an%x1f%ae%x1f%aI%x1f%cn%x1f%ce%x1f%cI%x1f%s%x1f%b -z`: 10 fields separated by byte `0x1f`, records terminated by byte `0x00`. `%P` is space-separated parents (empty for a root commit).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests with exact framed bytes.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/GitLogParserTests.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git.Parsing;\n\npublic class GitLogParserTests\n{\n    private const char US = '\u001f'; // 0x1f field separator (%x1f)\n    private const char NUL = '\u0000'; // 0x00 record terminator (-z)\n\n    private static byte[] Bytes(string s) => Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(s);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Builds one log record: 10 %x1f-separated fields. Caller appends NUL between records.\n    /// </summary>\n    private static string Record(\n        string sha, string parents, string an, string ae, string aDate,\n        string cn, string ce, string cDate, string subject, string body)\n        => string.Join(US, sha, parents, an, ae, aDate, cn, ce, cDate, subject, body);\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_NormalCommit_MapsAllFields()\n    {\n        var record = Record(\n            "1111111111111111111111111111111111111111",\n            "2222222222222222222222222222222222222222",\n            "Alice", "alice@example.com", "2026-05-29T10:00:00+02:00",\n            "Bob", "bob@example.com", "2026-05-29T11:30:00+02:00",\n            "Add feature", "Detailed body line.");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        var c = commits[0];\n        c.Sha.ShouldBe("1111111111111111111111111111111111111111");\n        c.ShortSha.ShouldBe("1111111");\n        c.Parents.ShouldBe(["2222222222222222222222222222222222222222"]);\n        c.AuthorName.ShouldBe("Alice");\n        c.AuthorEmail.ShouldBe("alice@example.com");\n        c.AuthorDate.ShouldBe(DateTimeOffset.Parse("2026-05-29T10:00:00+02:00"));\n        c.CommitterName.ShouldBe("Bob");\n        c.CommitterEmail.ShouldBe("bob@example.com");\n        c.CommitDate.ShouldBe(DateTimeOffset.Parse("2026-05-29T11:30:00+02:00"));\n        c.Subject.ShouldBe("Add feature");\n        c.Body.ShouldBe("Detailed body line.");\n        c.IsMerge.ShouldBeFalse();\n        c.IsRoot.ShouldBeFalse();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_MultipleRecords_ReturnsInOrder()\n    {\n        var r1 = Record("aaaaaaa1", "", "A", "a@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z",\n            "A", "a@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z", "first", "");\n        var r2 = Record("bbbbbbb2", "aaaaaaa1", "B", "b@x", "2026-01-02T00:00:00Z",\n            "B", "b@x", "2026-01-02T00:00:00Z", "second", "");\n        var stdout = Bytes(r1 + NUL + r2 + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits.Count.ShouldBe(2);\n        commits[0].Subject.ShouldBe("first");\n        commits[1].Subject.ShouldBe("second");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_MergeCommit_HasMultipleParents()\n    {\n        var record = Record("merge123", "p1aaaaa p2bbbbb", "M", "m@x", "2026-05-01T00:00:00Z",\n            "M", "m@x", "2026-05-01T00:00:00Z", "Merge branch", "");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits[0].Parents.ShouldBe(["p1aaaaa", "p2bbbbb"]);\n        commits[0].IsMerge.ShouldBeTrue();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_OctopusMerge_HasThreeParents()\n    {\n        var record = Record("octo123", "p1 p2 p3", "M", "m@x", "2026-05-01T00:00:00Z",\n            "M", "m@x", "2026-05-01T00:00:00Z", "Octopus", "");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits[0].Parents.ShouldBe(["p1", "p2", "p3"]);\n        commits[0].IsMerge.ShouldBeTrue();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_RootCommit_HasNoParents()\n    {\n        var record = Record("root999", "", "R", "r@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z",\n            "R", "r@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z", "Initial commit", "");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits[0].Parents.ShouldBeEmpty();\n        commits[0].IsRoot.ShouldBeTrue();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_MultiLineBodyWithUnicode_PreservedDecodedAsUtf8()\n    {\n        var record = Record("u8sha12", "parent1", "Renée", "renee@example.com", "2026-05-29T10:00:00Z",\n            "Renée", "renee@example.com", "2026-05-29T10:00:00Z",\n            "Fix café crash", "Line one\nLine two — em dash\nLine three");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        var commits = GitLogParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        commits[0].AuthorName.ShouldBe("Renée");\n        commits[0].Subject.ShouldBe("Fix café crash");\n        commits[0].Body.ShouldBe("Line one\nLine two — em dash\nLine three");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_EmptyOutput_ReturnsEmptyList()\n    {\n        GitLogParser.Parse([]).ShouldBeEmpty();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_TrailingTerminatorOnly_ProducesNoPhantomRecord()\n    {\n        var record = Record("only111", "", "A", "a@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z",\n            "A", "a@x", "2026-01-01T00:00:00Z", "only", "");\n        var stdout = Bytes(record + NUL);\n\n        GitLogParser.Parse(stdout).Count.ShouldBe(1);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the tests; expect compile failure.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: build FAILS with `CS0246: GitLogParser`. System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Parses the output of\n/// 'git log --pretty=format:%H%x1f%P%x1f%an%x1f%ae%x1f%aI%x1f%cn%x1f%ce%x1f%cI%x1f%s%x1f%b -z'.\n/// Records are terminated by NUL (0x00); the 10 fields within each record are\n/// separated by the unit separator byte 0x1f. %P is a space-separated parent list.\n/// </summary>\npublic static class GitLogParser\n{\n    private const char FieldSeparator = '\u001f';\n    private const char RecordTerminator = '\u0000';\n    private const int FieldCount = 10;\n\n    public static IReadOnlyList<CommitInfo> Parse(byte[] stdout)\n    {\n        if (stdout.Length == 0)\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        var text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(stdout);\n        var commits = new List<CommitInfo>();\n\n        foreach (var record in text.Split(RecordTerminator))\n        {\n            if (record.Length == 0)\n            {\n                // Trailing terminator produces a final empty segment — skip it.\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var fields = record.Split(FieldSeparator);\n            if (fields.Length < FieldCount)\n            {\n                // Defensive: malformed record (e.g. missing body) — skip rather than throw.\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var sha = fields[0];\n            var parents = ParseParents(fields[1]);\n\n            commits.Add(new CommitInfo(\n                Sha: sha,\n                ShortSha: ShortSha(sha),\n                Parents: parents,\n                AuthorName: fields[2],\n                AuthorEmail: fields[3],\n                AuthorDate: ParseDate(fields[4]),\n                CommitterName: fields[5],\n                CommitterEmail: fields[6],\n                CommitDate: ParseDate(fields[7]),\n                Subject: fields[8],\n                Body: fields[9]));\n        }\n\n        return commits;\n    }\n\n    private static IReadOnlyList<string> ParseParents(string field)\n    {\n        if (field.Length == 0)\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        return field.Split(' ', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n    }\n\n    private static string ShortSha(string sha) => sha.Length <= 7 ? sha : sha[..7];\n\n    private static DateTimeOffset ParseDate(string value)\n        => DateTimeOffset.Parse(value, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture, DateTimeStyles.RoundtripKind);\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 8 `GitLogParserTests` pass.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/GitLogParser.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/GitLogParserTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add GitLogParser for NUL/0x1f-framed log records\n\nParse the 10-field %x1f-separated, -z NUL-terminated git log format\ninto CommitInfo, handling root/merge/octopus parents, ISO-8601 dates,\nmulti-line bodies and UTF-8 decoding. Covered with exact byte fixtures.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.5: `NumstatParser`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NumstatEntry.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NumstatParser.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/NumstatParserTests.cs`\n\n`git diff --numstat -z` emits, per file: `<added>\t<deleted>\t` followed by either one NUL-terminated path (normal) **or** — for renames/copies — `<added>\t<deleted>\t` then `\0<oldpath>\0<newpath>\0`. Binary files emit `-\t-\t<path>\0`. Concretely, a normal record is `added "\t" deleted "\t" path NUL`; a rename record is `added "\t" deleted "\t" NUL oldpath NUL newpath NUL`.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests with exact Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git.Parsing;\n\npublic class NumstatParserTests\n{\n    private const string TAB = "\t";\n    private const string NUL = "\u0000";\n\n    private static byte[] Bytes(string s) => Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(s);\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_NormalTextFile_ReadsAddedDeletedAndPath()\n    {\n        // entries[0].OldPath.ShouldBe("old/name.cs");\n        entries[0].Path.ShouldBe("new/name.cs");\n        entries[0].IsBinary.ShouldBeFalse();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void +\n            "1" + TAB + "1" + TAB + NUL + "a/old.cs" + NUL + "b/new.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var entries = NumstatParser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        entries.Count.ShouldBe(3);\n        entries[0].Path.ShouldBe("added.txt");\n        entries[0].Added.ShouldBe(10);\n        entries[1].IsBinary.ShouldBeTrue();\n        entries[1].Path.ShouldBe("image.bin");\n        entries[2].OldPath.ShouldBe("a/old.cs");\n        entries[2].Path.ShouldBe("b/new.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_UnicodePath_DecodedAsUtf8_QuotepathOff()\n    {\n        // OldPath, int? Added, int? Deleted, bool IsBinary);\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Implement `NumstatParser`.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NumstatParser.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Text;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Parses 'git diff --numstat -z' output. Each entry begins with\n/// "&lt;added&gt;\t&lt;deleted&gt;\t". For a normal change the path follows and is\n/// NUL-terminated. For a rename/copy the counts are followed immediately by a NUL,\n/// then "&lt;oldpath&gt;\0&lt;newpath&gt;\0". Binary files use "-" for both counts.\n/// </summary>\npublic static class NumstatParser\n{\n    private const char Nul = '\u0000';\n\n    public static IReadOnlyList<NumstatEntry> Parse(byte[] stdout)\n    {\n        if (stdout.Length == 0)\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        var text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(stdout);\n        var entries = new List<NumstatEntry>();\n        var index = 0;\n\n        while (index < text.Length)\n        {\n            // Each entry's count header is "added \t deleted \t" before the first NUL boundary.\n            // Find the end of "added\tdeleted\t": it is the position just past the second tab.\n            var firstTab = text.IndexOf('\t', index);\n            if (firstTab < 0)\n            {\n                break;\n            }\n\n            var secondTab = text.IndexOf('\t', firstTab + 1);\n            if (secondTab < 0)\n            {\n                break;\n            }\n\n            var addedToken = text[index..firstTab];\n            var deletedToken = text[(firstTab + 1)..secondTab];\n            var isBinary = addedToken == "-" && deletedToken == "-";\n            int? added = isBinary ? null : ParseCount(addedToken);\n            int? deleted = isBinary ? null : ParseCount(deletedToken);\n\n            // Position right after the second tab. A rename has a NUL here first.\n            var afterCounts = secondTab + 1;\n\n            if (afterCounts < text.Length && text[afterCounts] == Nul)\n            {\n                // Rename/copy: \0 oldpath \0 newpath \0\n                var oldStart = afterCounts + 1;\n                var oldEnd = text.IndexOf(Nul, oldStart);\n                if (oldEnd < 0)\n                {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                var newStart = oldEnd + 1;\n                var newEnd = text.IndexOf(Nul, newStart);\n                if (newEnd < 0)\n                {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                var oldPath = text[oldStart..oldEnd];\n                var newPath = text[newStart..newEnd];\n                entries.Add(new NumstatEntry(newPath, oldPath, added, deleted, isBinary));\n                index = newEnd + 1;\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                // Normal: path \0\n                var pathEnd = text.IndexOf(Nul, afterCounts);\n                if (pathEnd < 0)\n                {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                var path = text[afterCounts..pathEnd];\n                entries.Add(new NumstatEntry(path, null, added, deleted, isBinary));\n                index = pathEnd + 1;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return entries;\n    }\n\n    private static int ParseCount(string token)\n        => int.Parse(token, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 6 `NumstatParserTests` pass.\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NumstatEntry.cs src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NumstatParser.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/NumstatParserTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add NumstatParser for --numstat -z output\n\nParse added/deleted line counts and paths, handling the binary "-\t-"\nmarker (null counts) and the NUL-framed two-path rename/copy records,\nwith UTF-8 path decoding under core.quotepath=false.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.6: `NameStatusParser`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NameStatusEntry.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NameStatusParser.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/NameStatusParserTests.cs`\n\n`git diff --name-status -z -M -C` emits, per file, a status token then NUL-separated path(s). GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git.Parsing;\n\npublic class NameStatusParserTests\n{\n    private const string NUL = "\u0000";\n\n    private static byte[] Bytes(string s) => Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(s);\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_Added_MapsToAddedKind()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes("A" + NUL + "new.cs" + entries[0].Path.ShouldBe("new.cs");\n        entries[0].OldPath.ShouldBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_Modified_MapsToModifiedKind()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes("M" OldPath);\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Implement `NameStatusParser`.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NameStatusParser.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Parses 'git diff --name-status -z -M -C' output. Each record is a status token\n/// followed by NUL-separated path(s). A/M/D/T have one path; R&lt;nnn&gt;/C&lt;nnn&gt;\n/// (with a similarity index) have an old path then a new path. The leading status\n/// letter determines the ChangeKind; the numeric similarity suffix is ignored.\n/// </summary>\npublic static class NameStatusParser\n{\n    private const char Nul = '\u0000';\n\n    public static IReadOnlyList<NameStatusEntry> Parse(byte[] stdout)\n    {\n        if (stdout.Length == 0)\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        var text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(stdout);\n        // Split on NUL; the structure is token, path[, path] repeating.\n        var tokens = text.Split(Nul);\n        var entries = new List<NameStatusEntry>();\n        var i = 0;\n\n        while (i < tokens.Length)\n        {\n            var status = tokens[i];\n            if (status.Length == 0)\n            {\n                // Trailing empty segment after the final NUL.\n                i++;\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var letter = status[0];\n            if (letter is 'R' or 'C')\n            {\n                if (i + 2 >= tokens.Length)\n                {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                var oldPath = tokens[i + 1];\n                var newPath = tokens[i + 2];\n                var kind = letter == 'R' ? ChangeKind.Renamed : ChangeKind.Copied;\n                entries.Add(new NameStatusEntry(kind, newPath, oldPath));\n                i += 3;\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                if (i + 1 >= tokens.Length)\n                {\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                var path = tokens[i + 1];\n                entries.Add(new NameStatusEntry(MapKind(letter), path, null));\n                i += 2;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return entries;\n    }\n\n    private static ChangeKind MapKind(char letter) => letter switch\n    {\n        'A' => ChangeKind.Added,\n        'M' => ChangeKind.Modified,\n        'D' => ChangeKind.Deleted,\n        'T' => ChangeKind.TypeChanged,\n        _ => ChangeKind.Modified\n    };\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 9 `NameStatusParserTests` pass.\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NameStatusEntry.cs src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/NameStatusParser.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/NameStatusParserTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add NameStatusParser for --name-status -z -M -C output\n\nMap A/M/D/T to ChangeKind and parse R<nnn>/C<nnn> rename/copy records\n(similarity-index suffix ignored) into old/new path pairs, with UTF-8\ndecoding.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.7: `StatusPorcelainV2Parser`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2Parser.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2ParserTests.cs`\n\n`git status --porcelain=v2 -z` emits NUL-terminated lines. Line kinds:\n- `1 <XY> <sub> <mH> <mI> <mW> <hH> <hI> <path>` — ordinary changed entry.\n- `2 <XY> <sub> <mH> <mI> <mW> <hH> <hI> <Xscore> <path>\0<origPath>` — rename/copy; under `-z` the path and orig-path are split by an extra NUL (the orig path is its own NUL-terminated field immediately following).\n- `u <xy> <sub> <m1> <m2> <m3> <mW> <h1> <h2> <h3> <path>` — unmerged (conflicted).\n- `? <path>` — untracked.\n- `! <path>` — ignored (we skip these).\n\nThe `XY` field holds two staging/worktree status letters; `D` in either column means deleted, `A` means added, otherwise modified.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests with exact porcelain-v2 framing.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2ParserTests.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git.Parsing;\n\npublic class StatusPorcelainV2ParserTests\n{\n    private const string NUL = "\u0000";\n\n    private static byte[] Bytes(string s) => Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(s);\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_Untracked_QuestionMarkLine_MapsToUntracked()\n    {\n        // "? newfile.txt\0"\n        var stdout = Bytes("? newfile.txt" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Untracked);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("newfile.txt");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_OrdinaryModified_TypeOneLine_MapsToModified()\n    {\n        // "1 .M N... 100644 100644 100644 <h> <h> src/app.cs\0"\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "1 .M N... 100644 100644 100644 1111111111111111111111111111111111111111 " +\n            "1111111111111111111111111111111111111111 src/app.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Modified);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("src/app.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_OrdinaryAdded_XYHasA_MapsToAdded()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "1 A. N... 000000 100644 100644 0000000000000000000000000000000000000000 " +\n            "2222222222222222222222222222222222222222 added.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Added);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("added.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_OrdinaryDeleted_XYHasD_MapsToDeleted()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "1 .D N... 100644 100644 000000 3333333333333333333333333333333333333333 " +\n            "3333333333333333333333333333333333333333 removed.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Deleted);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("removed.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_Renamed_TypeTwoLine_SetsNewAndOldPath()\n    {\n        // Type 2: "2 R. N... <m> <m> <m> <h> <h> R100 new.cs\0old.cs\0"\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "2 R. N... 100644 100644 100644 4444444444444444444444444444444444444444 " +\n            "4444444444444444444444444444444444444444 R100 new.cs" + NUL + "old.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Renamed);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("new.cs");\n        files[0].OldPath.ShouldBe("old.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_Unmerged_TypeULine_MapsToConflicted()\n    {\n        // Type u: "u UU N... <m1> <m2> <m3> <mW> <h1> <h2> <h3> conflicted.cs\0"\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "u UU N... 100644 100644 100644 100644 " +\n            "5555555555555555555555555555555555555555 " +\n            "6666666666666666666666666666666666666666 " +\n            "7777777777777777777777777777777777777777 conflicted.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Conflicted);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("conflicted.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_IgnoredEntries_AreSkipped()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes("! ignored.log" + NUL + "? real.txt" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("real.txt");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_MixedAllLineTypes_ParsedInOrder()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes(\n            "1 .M N... 100644 100644 100644 aaaa aaaa changed.cs" + NUL +\n            "? untracked.txt" + NUL +\n            "2 R. N... 100644 100644 100644 bbbb bbbb R100 dst.cs" + NUL + "srcname.cs" + NUL +\n            "u UU N... 100644 100644 100644 100644 c1 c2 c3 conflict.cs" + NUL);\n\n        var files = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout);\n\n        files.Count.ShouldBe(4);\n        files[0].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Modified);\n        files[0].Path.ShouldBe("changed.cs");\n        files[1].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Untracked);\n        files[1].Path.ShouldBe("untracked.txt");\n        files[2].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Renamed);\n        files[2].Path.ShouldBe("dst.cs");\n        files[2].OldPath.ShouldBe("srcname.cs");\n        files[3].Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Conflicted);\n        files[3].Path.ShouldBe("conflict.cs");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_UntrackedUnicodePath_DecodedAsUtf8()\n    {\n        var stdout = Bytes("? café/notes-é.md" + NUL);\n\n        StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(stdout)[0].Path.ShouldBe("café/notes-é.md");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_EmptyOutput_ReturnsEmptyList()\n    {\n        StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse([]).ShouldBeEmpty();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the tests; expect compile failure.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: build FAILS with `CS0246: StatusPorcelainV2Parser`. Red state.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Implement `StatusPorcelainV2Parser`.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2Parser.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Text;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Parses 'git status --porcelain=v2 -z' output into ChangedFile rows. Record kinds:\n/// '1' ordinary change, '2' rename/copy (followed by a NUL-separated original path),\n/// 'u' unmerged/conflicted, '?' untracked, '!' ignored (skipped). For types 1 and 2\n/// the two-letter XY field decides Added/Deleted/Modified.\n/// </summary>\npublic static class StatusPorcelainV2Parser\n{\n    private const char Nul = '\u0000';\n\n    public static IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile> Parse(byte[] stdout)\n    {\n        if (stdout.Length == 0)\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        var text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(stdout);\n        // Each record is NUL-terminated. A type-2 record's original path is the\n        // immediately following NUL-terminated field, so we walk segments by index.\n        var segments = text.Split(Nul);\n        var files = new List<ChangedFile>();\n        var i = 0;\n\n        while (i < segments.Length)\n        {\n            var segment = segments[i];\n            if (segment.Length == 0)\n            {\n                i++;\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var marker = segment[0];\n            switch (marker)\n            {\n                case '?':\n                    files.Add(new ChangedFile(PathAfterPrefix(segment), null, ChangeKind.Untracked, null, null, false));\n                    i++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '!':\n                    // Ignored entry — not part of the changed-files view.\n                    i++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '1':\n                    files.Add(ParseOrdinary(segment));\n                    i++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '2':\n                    // Rename/copy: the original path is the next NUL-terminated segment.\n                    var origPath = i + 1 < segments.Length ? segments[i + 1] : string.Empty;\n                    files.Add(ParseRename(segment, origPath));\n                    i += 2;\n                    break;\n\n                case 'u':\n                    files.Add(new ChangedFile(LastSpaceSeparatedField(segment), null, ChangeKind.Conflicted, null, null, false));\n                    i++;\n                    break;\n\n                default:\n                    i++;\n                    break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return files;\n    }\n\n    private static ChangedFile ParseOrdinary(string segment)\n    {\n        // "1 <XY> <sub> <mH> <mI> <mW> <hH> <hI> <path>"\n        var fields = segment.Split(' ', 9);\n        var xy = fields.Length > 1 ? fields[1] : "..";\n        var path = fields.Length > 8 ? fields[8] : string.Empty;\n        return new ChangedFile(path, null, KindFromXy(xy), null, null, false);\n    }\n\n    private static ChangedFile ParseRename(string segment, string origPath)\n    {\n        // "2 <XY> <sub> <mH> <mI> <mW> <hH> <hI> <Xscore> <path>"\n        var fields = segment.Split(' ', 10);\n        var xy = fields.Length > 1 ? fields[1] : "..";\n        var path = fields.Length > 9 ? fields[9] : string.Empty;\n        var kind = xy.Length > 0 && xy[0] == 'C' ? ChangeKind.Copied : ChangeKind.Renamed;\n        return new ChangedFile(path, origPath, kind, null, null, false);\n    }\n\n    private static ChangeKind KindFromXy(string xy)\n    {\n        if (xy.Contains('D'))\n        {\n            return ChangeKind.Deleted;\n        }\n\n        if (xy.Contains('A'))\n        {\n            return ChangeKind.Added;\n        }\n\n        return ChangeKind.Modified;\n    }\n\n    private static string PathAfterPrefix(string segment)\n        // "? <path>" / "! <path>" — path starts after the 2-char prefix.\n        => segment.Length > 2 ? segment[2..] : string.Empty;\n\n    private static string LastSpaceSeparatedField(string segment)\n    {\n        var lastSpace = segment.LastIndexOf(' ');\n        return lastSpace >= 0 && lastSpace + 1 < segment.Length ? segment[(lastSpace + 1)..] : string.Empty;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 10 `StatusPorcelainV2ParserTests` pass. (Note: the unmerged path is extracted as the last space-separated field on the line; the type-1 path is field index 8; renames pull the original path from the following NUL segment.)\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2Parser.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/StatusPorcelainV2ParserTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add StatusPorcelainV2Parser for untracked/conflicted/renames\n\nParse 'git status --porcelain=v2 -z' records: ? untracked, 1 ordinary\n(XY -> Added/Deleted/Modified), 2 rename/copy (original path from the\nfollowing NUL field), u conflicted, skipping ! ignored entries, with\nUTF-8 path decoding.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.8: `UnifiedDiffParser`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/UnifiedDiffParser.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/UnifiedDiffParserTests.cs`\n\nThis parses textual unified-diff content (the part after the `@@` hunk headers). It produces `DiffHunk`s with `DiffLine`s; `IntraSpans` are always empty here (intra-line enrichment is a later phase). It must handle multiple hunks, additions (`+`), deletions (`-`), context (space), the `@@ -a,b +c,d @@ optional-section-heading` header (including the single-line `-a +c` form where count defaults to 1), and the `\ No newline at end of file` marker (which is not a content line and must not advance line numbers).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests.** Create Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git.Parsing;\n\npublic class UnifiedDiffParserTests\n{\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_SingleHunk_ContextAddedDeleted_AssignsLineNumbers()\n    {\n        var diff =\n            "@@ -1,3 +1,4 @@\n" +\n            " context one\n" +\n            "-removed line\n" +\n            "+added line A\n" +\n            "+added line B\n" +\n            " context two\n";\n\n        var hunks = UnifiedDiffParser.Parse(diff);\n\n        hunks.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        var h = hunks[0];\n        h.OldStart.ShouldBe(1);\n        h.OldCount.ShouldBe(3);\n        h.NewStart.ShouldBe(1);\n        h.NewCount.ShouldBe(4);\n        h.Lines.Count.ShouldBe(5);\n\n        // context one: old 1, new 1\n        h.Lines[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Context);\n        h.Lines[0].OldLineNumber.ShouldBe(1);\n        h.Lines[0].NewLineNumber.ShouldBe(1);\n\n        // removed: old 2, no new\n        h.Lines[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Deleted);\n        h.Lines[1].OldLineNumber.ShouldBe(2);\n        h.Lines[1].NewLineNumber.ShouldBeNull();\n        h.Lines[1].Text.ShouldBe("removed line");\n\n        // added A: no old, new 2\n        h.Lines[2].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Added);\n        h.Lines[2].OldLineNumber.ShouldBeNull();\n        h.Lines[2].NewLineNumber.ShouldBe(2);\n        h.Lines[2].Text.ShouldBe("added line A");\n\n        // added B: no old, new 3\n        h.Lines[3].NewLineNumber.ShouldBe(3);\n\n        // context two: old 3, new 4\n        h.Lines[4].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Context);\n        h.Lines[4].OldLineNumber.ShouldBe(3);\n        h.Lines[4].NewLineNumber.ShouldBe(4);\n\n        h.Lines.ShouldAllBe(l => l.IntraSpans.Count == 0);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_MultipleHunks_BothParsed()\n    {\n        var diff =\n            "@@ -1,2 +1,2 @@\n" +\n            "-old1\n" +\n            "+new1\n" +\n            " ctx\n" +\n            "@@ -10,1 +10,2 @@ void Method()\n" +\n            " keep\n" +\n            "+inserted\n";\n\n        var hunks = UnifiedDiffParser.Parse(diff);\n\n        hunks.Count.ShouldBe(2);\n        hunks[0].OldStart.ShouldBe(1);\n        hunks[1].OldStart.ShouldBe(10);\n        hunks[1].NewStart.ShouldBe(10);\n        hunks[1].Header.ShouldBe("@@ -10,1 +10,2 @@ void Method()");\n        hunks[1].Lines[0].Text.ShouldBe("keep");\n        hunks[1].Lines[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Added);\n hunks[0].OldStart.ShouldBe(5);\n        hunks[0].OldCount.ShouldBe(1);\n        hunks[0].NewStart.ShouldBe(5);\n        hunks[0].NewCount.ShouldBe(1);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void
