+\n            "+new last\n" +\n            "\\ No newline at end of file\n";\n\n        var hunks = UnifiedDiffParser.Parse(diff);\n\n        // Only the - and + content lines become DiffLines; markers are dropped.\n        hunks[0].Lines.Count.ShouldBe(2);\n        hunks[0].Lines[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Deleted);\n        hunks[0].Lines[0].Text.ShouldBe("old last");\n        hunks[0].Lines[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffLineKind.Added);\n        hunks[0].Lines[1].Text.ShouldBe("new last");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_IgnoresFileHeaderLines_BeforeFirstHunk()\n    {\n        var diff =\n            "diff --git a/f.cs b/f.cs\n" +\n            "index 1234567..89abcde 100644\n" +\n            "--- a/f.cs\n" +\n            "+++ b/f.cs\n" +\n            "@@ -1,1 +1,1 @@\n" +\n            "-a\n" +\n            "+b\n";\n\n        var hunks = UnifiedDiffParser.Parse(diff);\n\n        hunks.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n        hunks[0].Lines.Count.ShouldBe(2);\n        hunks[0].Lines[0].Text.ShouldBe("a");\n        hunks[0].Lines[1].Text.ShouldBe("b");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Parse_EmptyInput_ReturnsEmptyList()\n    {\n        UnifiedDiffParser.Parse("").ShouldBeEmpty();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the tests; expect compile failure.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: build FAILS with `CS0246: UnifiedDiffParser`. Red state.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Implement `UnifiedDiffParser`.** Write `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/UnifiedDiffParser.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Parses unified-diff text into DiffHunks. Recognizes "@@ -a,b +c,d @@ heading"\n/// hunk headers (count defaults to 1 when omitted), and within each hunk classifies\n/// lines by their leading character: ' ' context, '+' added, '-' deleted. The\n/// "\ No newline at end of file" marker and any pre-hunk file-header lines are\n/// ignored. IntraSpans are left empty (intra-line enrichment happens later).\n/// </summary>\npublic static class UnifiedDiffParser\n{\n    public static IReadOnlyList<DiffHunk> Parse(string diffText)\n    {\n        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(diffText))\n        {\n            return [];\n        }\n\n        var lines = diffText.Replace("\r\n", "\n").Split('\n');\n        var hunks = new List<DiffHunk>();\n\n        int oldLine = 0;\n        int newLine = 0;\n        string header = string.Empty;\n        int oldStart = 0, oldCount = 0, newStart = 0, newCount = 0;\n        List<DiffLine>? current = null;\n\n        foreach (var raw in lines)\n        {\n            if (raw.StartsWith("@@", StringComparison.Ordinal))\n            {\n                if (current is not null)\n                {\n                    hunks.Add(new DiffHunk(oldStart, oldCount, newStart, newCount, header, current));\n                }\n\n                (oldStart, oldCount, newStart, newCount) = ParseHunkHeader(raw);\n                header = raw;\n                oldLine = oldStart;\n                newLine = newStart;\n                current = [];\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            if (current is null)\n            {\n                // Still in the pre-hunk file header (diff --git / index / --- / +++).\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            if (raw.Length == 0)\n            {\n                // A truly empty array element (e.g. trailing split entry) — ignore.\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            var marker = raw[0];\n            var text = raw.Length > 1 ? raw[1..] : string.Empty;\n\n            switch (marker)\n            {\n                case ' ':\n                    current.Add(new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Context, oldLine, newLine, text, []));\n                    oldLine++;\n                    newLine++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '-':\n                    current.Add(new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Deleted, oldLine, null, text, []));\n                    oldLine++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '+':\n                    current.Add(new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Added, null, newLine, text, []));\n                    newLine++;\n                    break;\n\n                case '\\':\n                    // "\ No newline at end of file" — metadata, not a content line.\n                    break;\n\n                default:\n                    // Unknown leading char outside a hunk body — ignore defensively.\n                    break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (current is not null)\n        {\n            hunks.Add(new DiffHunk(oldStart, oldCount, newStart, newCount, header, current));\n        }\n\n        return hunks;\n    }\n\n    private static (int OldStart, int OldCount, int NewStart, int NewCount) ParseHunkHeader(string header)\n    {\n        // Format: "@@ -oldStart[,oldCount] +newStart[,newCount] @@[ heading]"\n        var firstAt = header.IndexOf("@@", StringComparison.Ordinal);\n        var secondAt = header.IndexOf("@@", firstAt + 2, StringComparison.Ordinal);\n        var ranges = header[(firstAt + 2)..secondAt].Trim();\n\n        var parts = ranges.Split(' ', StringSplitOptions.RemoveEmptyEntries);\n        var (oldStart, oldCount) = ParseRange(parts[0]); // leading '-'\n        var (newStart, newCount) = ParseRange(parts[1]); // leading '+'\n        return (oldStart, oldCount, newStart, newCount);\n    }\n\n    private static (int Start, int Count) ParseRange(string token)\n    {\n        // token is like "-12,5" or "+3" — strip the sign, split on ','.\n        var body = token[1..];\n        var comma = body.IndexOf(',');\n        if (comma < 0)\n        {\n            return (int.Parse(body, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture), 1);\n        }\n\n        var start = int.Parse(body[..comma], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        var count = int.Parse(body[(comma + 1)..], CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n        return (start, count);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 6 `UnifiedDiffParserTests` pass.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/UnifiedDiffParser.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/UnifiedDiffParserTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add UnifiedDiffParser for @@ hunks and +/-/space lines\n\nParse unified-diff text into DiffHunks with per-line old/new line\nnumbers, supporting multiple hunks, the single-line range form\n(count defaults to 1), pre-hunk file-header skipping and the\nno-newline-at-EOF marker. IntraSpans left empty for later enrichment.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 2.9: `ChangedFileMerge`\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/ChangedFileMerge.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/ChangedFileMergeTests.cs`\n\n`ChangedFileMerge.Merge` combines the three sources into the final `IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile>`: `name-status` provides the authoritative `ChangeKind` and old/new paths, `numstat` provides the `+/-` counts and the binary flag, and `extra` (from `StatusPorcelainV2Parser`) adds untracked/conflicted files that the diff sources do not report (e.g. untracked files in the working-tree view). Entries are keyed by their new path; `extra` paths not already present are appended.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing tests.** Create  var numstat = new NumstatEntry[]\n        {\n            new("src/app.cs", null, 12, 3, false)\n        };\n        var nameStatus = new NameStatusEntry[]\n        {\n    public void Merge_AllEmpty_ReturnsEmptyList()\n    {\n        ChangedFileMerge.Merge([], [], []).ShouldBeEmpty();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the tests; expect compile failure.** Entries are keyed by new path. An 'extra' entry for\n/// an already-present path overrides the kind (e.g. Conflicted wins) while keeping\n/// the numstat counts; an 'extra' entry for a new path is appended.\n/// </summary>\npublic static class ChangedFileMerge\n{\n    public static IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile> Merge(\n        IReadOnlyList<NumstatEntry> numstat,\n        IReadOnlyList<NameStatusEntry> nameStatus,\n        IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile> extra)\n    {\n        var nameStatusByPath = new Dictionary<string, NameStatusEntry>(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n        foreach (var ns in nameStatus)\n        {\n            nameStatusByPath[ns.Path] = ns;\n        }\n\n        var ordered = new List<ChangedFile>();\n        var indexByPath = new Dictionary<string, int>(StringComparer.Ordinal);\n\n        // 1. numstat drives the primary list (it has counts + binary flag).\n        foreach (var entry in numstat)\n        {\n            ChangeKind kind;\n            string? oldPath;\n            if (nameStatusByPath.TryGetValue(entry.Path, out var ns))\n            {\n                kind = ns.Kind;\n                oldPath = ns.OldPath ?? entry.OldPath;\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                kind = ChangeKind.Modified;\n                oldPath = entry.OldPath;\n            }\n\n            indexByPath[entry.Path] = ordered.Count;\n            ordered.Add(new ChangedFile(entry.Path, oldPath, kind, entry.Added, entry.Deleted, entry.IsBinary));\n        }\n\n        // 2. name-status entries with no numstat counterpart (rare; defensive).\n        foreach (var ns in nameStatus)\n        {\n            if (!indexByPath.ContainsKey(ns.Path))\n            {\n                indexByPath[ns.Path] = ordered.Count;\n                ordered.Add(new ChangedFile(ns.Path, ns.OldPath, ns.Kind, null, null, false));\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 3. extra (untracked/conflicted): override kind for existing paths,\n        //    append new paths.\n        foreach (var ex in extra)\n        {\n            if (indexByPath.TryGetValue(ex.Path, out var existingIndex))\n            {\n                var existing = ordered[existingIndex];\n                ordered[existingIndex] = existing with { Kind = ex.Kind };\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                indexByPath[ex.Path] = ordered.Count;\n                ordered.Add(ex);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return ordered;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests; expect PASS.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: zero warnings; all 7 `ChangedFileMergeTests` pass.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the full Core test suite as a phase gate.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build GitDelta.sln && dotnet test tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `dotnet build` reports `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)` (TreatWarningsAsErrors is on), and the test run shows all Phase 2 tests passing (`Failed: 0`).\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.** Run:\n\n```powershell\ngit add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/Parsing/ChangedFileMerge.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/Parsing/ChangedFileMergeTests.cs\ngit commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add ChangedFileMerge to combine diff/status sources\n\nMerge numstat (counts + binary flag), name-status (authoritative kind\nand rename old-path) and porcelain-v2 extras (untracked/conflicted)\ninto the final ChangedFile list, keyed by new path, with conflicted\nstatus overriding the diff-derived kind while preserving counts.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n## Phase 3: Core: Git Reader, Repo Discovery, Diff Spec & Intra-line\n\nThis phase builds the executable heart of `GitDelta.Core`: the `DiffSpec` ref-argument mapper, the DiffPlex-backed intra-line differ, the intra-line enricher, the full `CliGitReader` (driven by a fake `IGitProcessRunner` so no real git is ever spawned in tests), and the `CoreModule` Autofac registrations. It depends on the models, `IGitReader`/`IGitProcessRunner` interfaces, `DiffSpec`, `GitConstants`, `GitResult`, `GitAvailability`, and the pure parsers (`GitLogParser`, `NumstatParser`, `NameStatusParser`, `StatusPorcelainV2Parser`, `UnifiedDiffParser`, `ChangedFileMerge`) established in the earlier phases.\n\nAll work is TDD where the logic is unit-testable. ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Git;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git;\n\n  public class DiffSpecArgsTests\n  {\n      [Fact]\n      public void ToDiffArgs_WorkingTreeVsHead_ReturnsHead()\n      {\n          var args = DiffSpecArgs.ToDiffArgs(new DiffSpec.WorkingTreeVsHead(), isRootCommit: false);\n\n          args.ShouldBe(new[] { "HEAD" ToDiffArgs_CommitVsParent_RootCommit_UsesEmptyTreeSha()\n      {\n          var args = DiffSpecArgs.ToDiffArgs(new DiffSpec.CommitVsParent("root999"), isRootCommit: true);\n\n new[] { GitConstants.EmptyTreeSha, c.Sha }\n                  : new[] { c.Sha + "^", c.Sha },\n              DiffSpec.TwoCommits t => new[] { t.BaseSha, t.TargetSha },\n              _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(spec), spec, "Unknown DiffSpec variant."),\n          };\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffSpecArgsTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 5`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Git/DiffSpecArgs.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/DiffSpecArgsTests.cs\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  feat(core): add DiffSpecArgs.ToDiffArgs ref mapping\n\n  Maps WorkingTreeVsHead/CommitVsParent/TwoCommits to git diff ref args,\n  using the empty-tree SHA for root commits.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 3.2: DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer — word-level intra-line spans\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests.cs`\n\n> Note: `IIntraLineDiffer`, `IntraSpan`, and `IntraSpanKind` already exist from the earlier phase. This task adds the concrete DiffPlex implementation. Ensure `DiffPlex` is referenced via central package management (it should already be pinned in `Directory.Packages.props`; if `GitDelta.Core.csproj` lacks `<PackageReference Include="DiffPlex" />`, add it in Step 3).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test on real strings**\n\n  `IntraSpan` carries `(int Start, int Length, IntraSpanKind Kind)` and represents a character range within a single line. For the pair `deleted = "the quick brown fox"` / `added = "the slow brown fox"`, the differing word is `quick` (deleted, chars 4..9) vs `slow` (added, chars 4..8). We assert the differ isolates exactly those changed ranges and leaves the shared `"the "` / `" brown fox"` untouched.\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Diff;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Diff;\n\n  public class DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests\n  {\n      private readonly DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer _sut = new();\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Compute_OneChangedWord_IsolatesThatWordOnBothSides()\n      {\n          var (deleted, added) = _sut.Compute("the quick brown fox", "the slow brown fox");\n\n          // Deleted side: "quick" occupies chars [4, 5) length 5.\n          deleted.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n          deleted[0].Kind.ShouldBe(IntraSpanKind.Deleted);\n          "the quick brown fox".Substring(deleted[0].Start, deleted[0].Length).ShouldBe("quick");\n\n          // Added side: "slow" occupies chars [4, 4) length 4.\n          added.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n          added[0].Kind.ShouldBe(IntraSpanKind.Added);\n          "the slow brown fox".Substring(added[0].Start, added[0].Length).ShouldBe("slow");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Compute_IdenticalLines_ReturnsNoSpans()\n      {\n          var (deleted, added) = _sut.Compute("same text here", "same text here");\n\n          deleted.ShouldBeEmpty();\n          added.ShouldBeEmpty();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Compute_PureInsertionAtEnd_ReportsOnlyAddedSpan()\n      {\n          var (deleted, added) = _sut.Compute("int x = 1", "int x = 1; // note");\n\n          deleted.ShouldBeEmpty();\n          added.Count.ShouldBeGreaterThan(0);\n          added.ShouldAllBe(s => s.Kind == IntraSpanKind.Added);\n          // The added text must include the appended fragment.\n          var addedText = string.Concat(added.Select(s => "int x = 1; // note".Substring(s.Start, s.Length)));\n          addedText.ShouldContain("// note");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Compute_PureDeletion_ReportsOnlyDeletedSpan()\n      {\n          var (deleted, added) = _sut.Compute("int x = 1; // note", "int x = 1");\n\n          added.ShouldBeEmpty();\n          deleted.Count.ShouldBeGreaterThan(0);\n          deleted.ShouldAllBe(s => s.Kind == IntraSpanKind.Deleted);\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Compute_SpansAreWithinLineBounds()\n      {\n          const string del = "alpha beta gamma";\n          const string add = "alpha BETA gamma";\n\n          var (deleted, added) = _sut.Compute(del, add);\n\n          foreach (var s in deleted)\n          {\n              s.Start.ShouldBeGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0);\n              (s.Start + s.Length).ShouldBeLessThanOrEqualTo(del.Length);\n          }\n          foreach (var s in added)\n          {\n              s.Start.ShouldBeGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0);\n              (s.Start + s.Length).ShouldBeLessThanOrEqualTo(add.Length);\n          }\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the test — expect a COMPILE failure**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `CS0246: The type or namespace name 'DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer' could not be found`. If the `<ItemGroup>` does not already contain it, add this line inside the existing package `<ItemGroup>` in `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj` (version comes from central management, so no `Version` attribute here):\n\n  ```xml\n  <PackageReference Include="DiffPlex" />\n  ```\n\n  Then create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using DiffPlex;\n  using DiffPlex.Chunkers;\n  using DiffPlex.Model;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Computes word-level intra-line change spans for a deleted/added line pair using DiffPlex.\n  /// Returned spans are character ranges into the respective input line.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer : IIntraLineDiffer\n  {\n      private readonly IDiffer _differ = new Differ();\n\n      public (IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> Deleted, IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> Added) Compute(\n          string deletedLine, string addedLine)\n      {\n          if (deletedLine == addedLine)\n          {\n              return (Array.Empty<IntraSpan>(), Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());\n          }\n\n          // Word chunker => word-level granularity (matches the spec's "word-level" intra-line highlighting).\n          DiffResult result = _differ.CreateDiffs(\n              deletedLine, addedLine,\n              ignoreWhitespace: false, ignoreCase: false,\n              new WordChunker());\n\n          string[] pieces = result.PiecesOld;\n\n          var deleted = new List<IntraSpan>();\n          var added = new List<IntraSpan>();\n\n          foreach (DiffBlock block in result.DiffBlocks)\n          {\n              if (block.DeleteCountA > 0)\n              {\n                  AddSpan(deleted, pieces, block.DeleteStartA, block.DeleteCountA, IntraSpanKind.Deleted);\n              }\n\n              if (block.InsertCountB > 0)\n              {\n                  AddSpan(added, result.PiecesNew, block.InsertStartB, block.InsertCountB, IntraSpanKind.Added);\n              }\n          }\n\n          return (deleted, added);\n      }\n\n      private static void AddSpan(\n          List<IntraSpan> spans, string[] pieces, int startPiece, int countPiece, IntraSpanKind kind)\n      {\n          // Convert a [startPiece, startPiece+countPiece) piece range into a character [start, length) range.\n          int charStart = 0;\n          for (int i = 0; i < startPiece; i++)\n          {\n              charStart += pieces[i].Length;\n          }\n\n          int charLength = 0;\n          for (int i = startPiece; i < startPiece + countPiece; i++)\n          {\n              charLength += pieces[i].Length;\n          }\n\n          spans.Add(new IntraSpan(charStart, charLength, kind));\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 5`. If `WordChunker` or `result.PiecesOld`/`PiecesNew` member names differ in the pinned DiffPlex version, adjust the using/members to match — the public DiffPlex surface (`Differ`, `WordChunker`, `DiffResult.PiecesOld/PiecesNew`, `DiffBlock.DeleteStartA/DeleteCountA/InsertStartB/InsertCountB`) is what these tests bind to.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer.cs src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/DiffPlexIntraLineDifferTests.cs\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  feat(core): add DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer for word-level spans\n\n  Maps DiffPlex word-chunk diff blocks to character-range IntraSpans\n  for deleted/added line pairs.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 3.3: IntraLineEnricher.Enrich — pair consecutive delete/add runs\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Diff/IntraLineEnricher.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/IntraLineEnricherTests.cs`\n\nThe enricher walks every hunk; within each hunk it finds maximal consecutive runs of `Deleted` lines immediately followed by `Added` lines. When a deleted-run and the following added-run are **equal length**, it pairs them 1:1 (deleted[i] ↔ added[i]) and runs the `IIntraLineDiffer` to fill `IntraSpans` on both. Unequal runs, or Context lines, are left with empty `IntraSpans`. Returns a new `FileDiff` (records are immutable).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test (with a tiny stub differ so the test is deterministic)**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/IntraLineEnricherTests.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Diff;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Diff;\n\n  public class IntraLineEnricherTests\n  {\n      // Deterministic stub: marks the whole deleted line and whole added line as one span each.\n      private sealed class WholeLineDiffer : IIntraLineDiffer\n      {\n          public (IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> Deleted, IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> Added) Compute(\n              string deletedLine, string addedLine) =>\n              (\n                  new[] { new IntraSpan(0, deletedLine.Length, IntraSpanKind.Deleted) },\n                  new[] { new IntraSpan(0, addedLine.Length, IntraSpanKind.Added) }\n              );\n      }\n\n      private static DiffLine Line(DiffLineKind kind, string text) =>\n          new(kind, null, null, text, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());\n\n      private static FileDiff DiffWith(params DiffLine[] lines)\n      {\n          var file = new ChangedFile("a.txt", null, ChangeKind.Modified, 1, 1, IsBinary: false);\n          var hunk = new DiffHunk(1, lines.Length, 1, lines.Length, "@@ -1 +1 @@", lines);\n          return new FileDiff(file, new[] { hunk }, IsBinary: false, IsTruncated: false);\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Enrich_EqualLengthDeleteThenAddRun_PairsAndFillsSpans()\n      {\n          var diff = DiffWith(\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Deleted, "old one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Deleted, "old two"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "new one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "new two"));\n\n          var result = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, new WholeLineDiffer());\n\n          var enriched = result.Hunks[0].Lines;\n          enriched[0].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1); // deleted "old one"\n          enriched[0].IntraSpans[0].Kind.ShouldBe(IntraSpanKind.Deleted);\n          enriched[0].IntraSpans[0].Length.ShouldBe("old one".Length);\n          enriched[1].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1); // deleted "old two"\n          enriched[2].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1); // added "new one"\n          enriched[2].IntraSpans[0].Kind.ShouldBe(IntraSpanKind.Added);\n          enriched[3].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1); // added "new two"\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Enrich_UnequalRunLengths_LeavesSpansEmpty()\n      {\n          var diff = DiffWith(\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Deleted, "old one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "new one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "new two"));\n\n          var result = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, new WholeLineDiffer());\n\n          foreach (var line in result.Hunks[0].Lines)\n          {\n              line.IntraSpans.ShouldBeEmpty();\n          }\n Line(DiffLineKind.Deleted, "old one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "new one"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Context, "also unchanged"));\n\n          var result = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, new WholeLineDiffer());\n\n          var lines = result.Hunks[0].Lines;\n          lines[0].IntraSpans.ShouldBeEmpty();         // leading context\n          lines[1].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1);       // deleted paired\n          lines[2].IntraSpans.Count.ShouldBe(1);       // added paired\n          lines[3].IntraSpans.ShouldBeEmpty();         // trailing context\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Enrich_AddsWithNoPrecedingDelete_LeavesSpansEmpty()\n      {\n          var diff = DiffWith(\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Context, "ctx"),\n              Line(DiffLineKind.Added, "brand new"));\n\n          var result = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, new WholeLineDiffer());\n\n          foreach result = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, new WholeLineDiffer());\n\n          result.File.Path.ShouldBe("a.txt");\n          result.IsBinary.ShouldBeFalse();\n          result.IsTruncated.ShouldBeFalse();\n          result.Hunks[0].Header.ShouldBe("@@ -1 +1 @@");\n          result.Hunks[0].OldStart.ShouldBe(1);\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the the input is not mutated.\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class IntraLineEnricher\n  {\n      public static FileDiff Enrich(FileDiff diff, IIntraLineDiffer differ)\n      {\n          var newHunks = new List<DiffHunk>(diff.Hunks.Count);\n\n          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)\n          {\n              newHunks.Add(EnrichHunk(hunk, differ));\n          }\n\n          return diff with { Hunks = newHunks };\n      }\n\n      private static DiffHunk EnrichHunk(DiffHunk hunk, IIntraLineDiffer differ)\n      {\n          var lines = hunk.Lines;\n          var result = new DiffLine[lines.Count];\n          for (int i = 0; i < lines.Count; i++)\n          {\n              result[i] = lines[i];\n          }\n\n          int index = 0;\n          while (index < lines.Count)\n          {\n              if (lines[index].Kind != DiffLineKind.Deleted)\n              {\n                  index++;\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              // Collect the maximal run of consecutive Deleted lines.\n              int deleteStart = index;\n              while (index < lines.Count && lines[index].Kind == DiffLineKind.Deleted)\n              {\n                  index++;\n              }\n              int deleteCount = index - deleteStart;\n\n              // Collect the maximal run of Added lines immediately following.\n              int addStart = index;\n              while (index < lines.Count && lines[index].Kind == DiffLineKind.Added)\n              {\n                  index++;\n              }\n              int addCount = index - addStart;\n\n              // Pair 1:1 only when the runs are equal length and both non-empty.\n              if (deleteCount > 0 && deleteCount == addCount)\n              {\n                  for (int k = 0; k < deleteCount; k++)\n                  {\n                      DiffLine del = lines[deleteStart + k];\n                      DiffLine add = lines[addStart + k];\n\n                      var (delSpans, addSpans) = differ.Compute(del.Text, add.Text);\n\n                      result[deleteStart + k] = del with { IntraSpans = delSpans };\n                      result[addStart + k] = add with { IntraSpans = addSpans };\n                  }\n              }\n          }\n\n          return hunk with { Lines = result };\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~IntraLineEnricherTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 5`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Diff/IntraLineEnricher.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Diff/IntraLineEnricherTests.cs\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  feat(core): add IntraLineEnricher to pair delete/add runs\n\n  Pairs equal-length consecutive Deleted-then-Added line runs 1:1 and\n  fills IntraSpans via the supplied IIntraLineDiffer, returning a new FileDiff.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 3.4: CliGitReader — CheckGitAsync & FindRepositoryRootAsync\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/CliGitReader.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/CliGitReaderTests.cs`\n\n> Note: `IGitReader`, `IGitProcessRunner`, `GitResult`, and `GitAvailability` already exist. `CliGitReader` composes an injected `IGitProcessRunner` plus the pure parsers and the `IIntraLineDiffer`. private static GitResult Ok(byte[] stdout) =>\n          new(0, stdout, string.Empty);\n\n      private static GitResult Fail(string stderr) =>\n          new(128, Array.Empty<byte>(), stderr);\n\n      private void SetupRun(GitResult result) =>\n          _runner.RunAsync(Arg.Any<string>(), Arg.Any<IReadOnlyList<string>>(), Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n                 .Returns(Task.FromResult(result));\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task CheckGitAsync_ModernVersion_IsInstalledAndMeetsMinimum()\n      {\n          SetupRun(Ok("git version Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Git/CliGitReader.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Globalization;\n  using System.Text;\n  using System.Text.RegularExpressions;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Diff;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Git;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Reads repository information by shelling out to the git CLI via <see cref="IGitProcessRunner"/>\n  /// and parsing the output with the pure parsers in GitDelta.Core.Git.Parsing.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed partial class CliGitReader : IGitReader\n  {\n      /// <summary>Files whose hunk count makes the textual diff too large to render; we truncate.</summary>\n      public const int LargeFileHunkLineThreshold = 20_000;\n\n      private readonly IGitProcessRunner _runner;\n      private readonly IIntraLineDiffer _intraLineDiffer;\n\n      public CliGitReader(IGitProcessRunner runner, IIntraLineDiffer intraLineDiffer)\n      {\n          _runner = runner;\n          _intraLineDiffer = intraLineDiffer;\n      }\n\n      public async Task<GitAvailability> CheckGitAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n      {\n          GitResult result = await _runner\n              .RunAsync(Directory.GetCurrentDirectory(), new[] { "--version" }, ct)\n              .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n          if (!result.Success)\n          {\n              return new GitAvailability(IsInstalled: false, Version: null, MeetsMinimum: false);\n          }\n\n          string text = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(result.StdOut).Trim();\n          Match m = GitVersionRegex().Match(text);\n          if (!m.Success)\n          {\n              return new GitAvailability(IsInstalled: true, Version: null, MeetsMinimum: false);\n          }\n\n          string version = m.Groups["v"].Value;\n          int major = int.Parse(m.Groups["major"].Value, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n          int minor = int.Parse(m.Groups["minor"].Value, CultureInfo.InvariantCulture);\n          bool meets = major > 2 || (major == 2 && minor >= 30);\n\n          return new GitAvailability(IsInstalled: true, Version: version, MeetsMinimum: meets);\n      }\n\n      public async Task<string?> FindRepositoryRootAsync(string startDirectory, CancellationToken ct)\n      {\n          GitResult result = await _runner\n              .RunAsync(startDirectory, new[] { "rev-parse", "--show-toplevel" }, ct)\n              .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n          if (!result.Success)\n          {\n              return null;\n          }\n\n          string top = Encoding.UTF8.GetString(result.StdOut).Trim();\n          return string.IsNullOrEmpty(top) ? null : top;\n      }\n\n      public Task<IReadOnlyList<CommitInfo>> GetHistoryAsync(string repoRoot, int skip, int maxCount, CancellationToken ct) =>\n          throw new NotImplementedException();\n\n      public Task<IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile>> GetChangedFilesAsync(string repoRoot, DiffSpec spec, CancellationToken ct) =>\n          throw new NotImplementedException();\n\n      public Task<FileDiff> GetFileDiffAsync(string repoRoot, DiffSpec spec, string path, int contextLines, CancellationToken ct) =>\n          throw new NotImplementedException();\n\n      [GeneratedRegex(@"git version (?<v>(?<major>\d+)\.(?<minor>\d+)\S*)", RegexOptions.CultureInvariant)]\n      private static partial Regex GitVersionRegex();\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test For `WorkingTreeVsHead` it **also** runs `git status --porcelain=v2 -z` (parsed by `StatusPorcelainV2Parser`) to capture untracked/conflicted files, passing those as the `extra` list. Root-commit detection: `CommitVsParent` whose commit has no parent must diff against the empty tree — we detect this with `git rev-list --count <sha>^` (exit non-zero ⇒ root) before computing the ref args. NSubstitute returns canned bytes keyed on the args.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test**\n\n  Create NumstatParser.Parse(numstatResult.StdOut)\n              : Array.Empty<NumstatEntry>();\n\n          IReadOnlyList<NameStatusEntry> nameStatus = nameStatusResult.Success\n              ? NameStatusParser.Parse(nameStatusResult.StdOut)\n              : Array.Empty<NameStatusEntry>();\n\n          IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile> extra = Array.Empty<ChangedFile>();\n          if (spec is DiffSpec.WorkingTreeVsHead)\n          {\n              GitResult statusResult = await _runner\n                  .RunAsync(repoRoot, new[] { "status", "--porcelain=v2", "-z" }, ct)\n                  .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n              if (statusResult.Success)\n              {\n                  extra = StatusPorcelainV2Parser.Parse(statusResult.StdOut);\n              }\n          }\n\n          return ChangedFileMerge.Merge(numstat, nameStatus, extra);\n      }\n\n      private async Task<bool> IsRootCommitAsync(string repoRoot, string sha, CancellationToken ct)\n      {\n          // 'rev-list --count <sha>^' fails when the commit has no parent (i.e. it is a root commit).\n          GitResult result = await _runner\n              .RunAsync(repoRoot, new[] { "rev-list", "--count", sha + "^" }, ct)\n              .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n          return !result.Success;\n      }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~CliGitReaderChangedFilesTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed! It sets `IsBinary = true` (with no hunks) when git reports `Binary files ... differ`, and `IsTruncated = true` when the total parsed hunk-line count exceeds `LargeFileHunkLineThreshold` (in which case hunks are dropped to keep the model light). The `ChangedFile` it wraps is derived from the changed-files list for the same spec (so we get correct `Kind`/counts); if the path is not in that list we synthesize a `Modified` entry. Root-commit handling reuses `IsRootCommitAsync`.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Git/CliGitReaderFileDiffTests.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Text;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Diff;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Git;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using NSubstitute;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Git;\n\n  public class CliGitReaderFileDiffTests\n  {\n      private const string NUL = "\u0000";\n\n      private readonly IGitProcessRunner _runner = Substitute.For<IGitProcessRunner>();\n      private readonly CliGitReader _sut;\n\n      public CliGitReaderFileDiffTests()\n      {\n          _sut = new CliGitReader(_runner, new DiffPlexIntraLineDiffer());\n      }\n\n      private void Route(Func<IReadOnlyList<string>, GitResult> selector) =>\n          _runner.RunAsync(Arg.Any<string>(), Arg.Any<IReadOnlyList<string>>(), Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n                 .Returns(ci => Task.FromResult(selector(ci.ArgAt<IReadOnlyList<string>>(1))));\n\n      private static GitResult Ok(string s) => new(0, Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(s), string.Empty);\n\n      private const string TextualDiff =\n          "diff --git a/app.cs b/app.cs\n" +\n          "index 1111111..2222222 100644\n" +\n          "--- a/app.cs\n" +\n          "+++ b/app.cs\n" +\n          "@@ -1,3 +1,3 @@\n" +\n          " context line\n" +\n          "-var quick = 1;\n" +\n          "+var slow = 1;\n" +\n          " trailing line\n";\n\n      private void RouteTextual()\n      {\n          string numstat = "1\t1\tapp.cs" + NUL;\n          string nameStatus = "M" + NUL + "app.cs" + NUL;\n          Route(args =>\n          {\n              if (args.Contains("rev-list")) return Ok("1\n");\n              if (args.Contains("--numstat")) return Ok(numstat);\n              if (args.Contains("--name-status")) return Ok(nameStatus);\n              return Ok(TextualDiff); // the per-file 'git diff -U.. -- path'\n          });\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task GetFileDiffAsync_PassesContextRefsAndPathSeparator()\n      {\n          IReadOnlyList<string>? diffArgs = null;\n          string numstat = "1\t1\tapp.cs" + NUL;\n          string nameStatus = "M" + NUL + "app.cs" + NUL;\n          Route(args =>\n          {\n              if (args.Contains("rev-list")) return Ok("1\n");\n              if (args.Contains("--numstat")) return Ok(numstat);\n              if (args.Contains("--name-status")) return Ok(nameStatus);\n              diffArgs = args;\n              return Ok(TextualDiff);\n          });\n\n          await _sut.GetFileDiffAsync(\n              "C:/repo", new DiffSpec.TwoCommits("baseSha", "targetSha"), "app.cs", contextLines: 5, CancellationToken.None);\n\n          diffArgs.ShouldNotBeNull();\n          diffArgs![0].ShouldBe("diff");\n          diffArgs.ShouldContain("-U5");\n          diffArgs.ShouldContain("baseSha");\n          diffArgs.ShouldContain("targetSha");\n          diffArgs.ShouldContain("--");\n          diffArgs[^1].ShouldBe("app.cs");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task GetFileDiffAsync_ParsesHunksAndEnrichesIntraLine()\n      {\n          RouteTextual();\n\n          var diff = await _sut.GetFileDiffAsync(\n              "C:/repo", new DiffSpec.TwoCommits("baseSha", "targetSha"), "app.cs", contextLines: 3, CancellationToken.None);\n\n          diff.IsBinary.ShouldBeFalse();\n          diff.IsTruncated.ShouldBeFalse();\n          diff.Hunks.Count.ShouldBe(1);\n\n          var deleted = diff.Hunks[0].Lines.Single(l => l.Kind == DiffLineKind.Deleted);\n          var added = diff.Hunks[0].Lines.Single(l => l.Kind == DiffLineKind.Added);\n\n          // Intra-line enrichment paired the single delete/add and isolated quick -> slow.\n          deleted.IntraSpans.ShouldNotBeEmpty();\n          added.IntraSpans.ShouldNotBeEmpty();\n          deleted.Text.Substring(deleted.IntraSpans[0].Start, deleted.IntraSpans[0].Length).ShouldBe("quick");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task GetFileDiffAsync_BinaryFile_SetsIsBinaryAndNoHunks()\n      {\n          string numstat = "-\t-\timg.png" + NUL; // binary marker\n          string nameStatus = "M" + NUL + "img.png" + NUL;\n          Route(args =>\n          {\n              if (args.Contains("rev-list")) return Ok("1\n");\n              if (args.Contains("--numstat")) return Ok(numstat);\n              if (args.Contains("--name-status")) return Ok(nameStatus);\n              return Ok("diff --git a/img.png b/img.png\nBinary files a/img.png and b/img.png differ\n");\n          });\n\n          var diff = await _sut.GetFileDiffAsync(\n              "C:/repo", new DiffSpec.TwoCommits("baseSha", "targetSha"), "img.png", contextLines: 3, CancellationToken.None);\n\n          diff.IsBinary.ShouldBeTrue();\n          diff.Hunks.ShouldBeEmpty();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task GetFileDiffAsync_OverLineThreshold_SetsIsTruncatedAndDropsHunks()\n      {\n          // Build a unified diff whose body exceeds the truncation threshold.\n          var sb = new StringBuilder();\n          sb.Append("diff --git a/big.cs b/big.cs\n--- a/big.cs\n+++ b/big.cs\n");\n          int lines = CliGitReader.LargeFileHunkLineThreshold + 10;\n          sb.Append("@@ -1," + lines + " +1," + lines + " @@\n");\n          for (int i = 0; i < lines; i++)\n          {\n              sb.Append("+added line " + i + "\n");\n          }\n\n          string numstat = lines + "\t0\tbig.cs" + NUL;\n          string nameStatus = "M" + NUL + "big.cs" + NUL;\n          Route(args =>\n          {\n              if (args.Contains("rev-list")) return Ok("1\n");\n              if (args.Contains("--numstat")) return Ok(numstat);\n              if (args.Contains("--name-status")) return Ok(nameStatus);\n              return Ok(sb.ToString());\n          });\n\n          var diff = await _sut.GetFileDiffAsync(\n              "C:/repo", new DiffSpec.TwoCommits("baseSha", "targetSha"), "big.cs", contextLines: 3, CancellationToken.None);\n\n          diff.IsTruncated.ShouldBeTrue();\n          diff.Hunks.ShouldBeEmpty();\n          diff.IsBinary.ShouldBeFalse();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public async Task GetFileDiffAsync_CarriesChangedFileMetadata()\n      {\n          RouteTextual();\n\n          var diff = await _sut.GetFileDiffAsync(\n              "C:/repo", new DiffSpec.TwoCommits("baseSha", "targetSha"), "app.cs", contextLines: 3, CancellationToken.None);\n\n          diff.File.Path.ShouldBe("app.cs");\n          diff.File.Kind.ShouldBe(ChangeKind.Modified);\n      }\n  }\n Encoding.UTF8.GetString(result.StdOut) : string.Empty;\n\n          // Binary: git emits a "Binary files ... differ" line and no hunks.\n          if (file.IsBinary || diffText.Contains("Binary files ", StringComparison.Ordinal))\n          {\n              return new FileDiff(file with { IsBinary = true }, Array.Empty<DiffHunk>(),\n                                  IsBinary: true, IsTruncated: false);\n          }\n\n          IReadOnlyList<DiffHunk> hunks = UnifiedDiffParser.Parse(diffText);\n\n          int totalLines = 0;\n          foreach (DiffHunk h in hunks)\n          {\n              totalLines += h.Lines.Count;\n          }\n\n          if (totalLines > LargeFileHunkLineThreshold)\n          {\n              return new FileDiff(file, Array.Empty<DiffHunk>(), IsBinary: false, IsTruncated: true);\n          }\n\n          var diff = new FileDiff(file, hunks, IsBinary: false, IsTruncated: false);\n          return IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, _intraLineDiffer);\n      }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test — expect PASS**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~CliGitReaderFileDiffTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed! It maps the process command-line args plus the current working directory to a `LaunchAction`, per the backbone `ArgRouter.Route` contract and spec §4 ("Launch & CLI behavior"). All logic here is WPF-free, deterministic, and fully unit-tested; the bootstrap (a later UI phase) will call `FindRepositoryRootAsync` on the resulting `RepoPath` and downgrade `OpenRepoWorkingTree` to `ShowStartScreen` when the path is not a repo.\n\nThis phase assumes Phase 1 has already created `src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj` (root namespace `GitDelta.Core`, `net10.0`) and `tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj` (xUnit v3, references `GitDelta.Core`, with Shouldly available via central package management) and that the solution builds with zero warnings under `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true`.\n\n### Task 4.1: LaunchAction model (LaunchActionKind + LaunchAction record)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/LaunchAction.cs`\n- Test: (none — this task is a pure data declaration with no behavior; it is exercised by the `ArgRouter` tests in Task 4.2)\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the `LaunchActionKind` enum and `LaunchAction` record.**\n  These are the exact backbone types. `LaunchAction` carries an optional `RepoPath` that is only populated for `OpenRepoWorkingTree`. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/LaunchAction.cs` with the complete contents below.\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Cli;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// The high-level action the application bootstrap should take, decided purely\n/// from the process command-line arguments and the current working directory.\n/// </summary>\npublic enum LaunchActionKind\n{\n    /// <summary>Show the brand/Open-folder start screen (no usable repo context).</summary>\n    ShowStartScreen,\n\n    /// <summary>Open a repository at <see cref="LaunchAction.RepoPath"/> in working-tree-vs-HEAD mode.</summary>\n    OpenRepoWorkingTree,\n\n    /// <summary>Write CLI help text to the parent console and exit.</summary>\n    PrintHelp,\n\n    /// <summary>Write the version string to the parent console and exit.</summary>\n    PrintVersion,\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// The routing decision produced by <see cref="ArgRouter.Route"/>.\n/// <see cref="RepoPath"/> is non-null only when <see cref="Kind"/> is\n/// <see cref="LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree"/>.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed record LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind Kind, string? RepoPath = null);\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Build the Core project to confirm the new file compiles.**\n  Run the exact command:\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/GitDelta.Core.csproj\n```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded` with `0 Warning(s)` and `0 Error(s)`. If it fails, the most likely cause is a missing `Cli` folder — the file path itself creates the folder, so a failure here is a real compile error to fix before continuing.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Commit the model.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/LaunchAction.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add LaunchAction model for CLI routing\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 4.2: ArgRouter.Route (TDD)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/ArgRouter.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Cli/ArgRouterTests.cs`\n\nRouting rules (from the backbone and spec §4), applied in this exact precedence:\n1. If any arg is `--help`, `-h`, or `-?` → `PrintHelp` (help wins over everything, even if a path is also present).\n2. Else if any arg is `--version` or `-v` → `PrintVersion`.\n3. Else if a first **non-flag** arg is present → `OpenRepoWorkingTree(thatPath)` (a "flag" is any arg starting with `-`).\n4. Else (no args, or only flags we did not recognize) → `OpenRepoWorkingTree(cwd)`.\n\nThe bootstrap is responsible for the final `ShowStartScreen` downgrade when `FindRepositoryRootAsync` returns null, so `ArgRouter` itself never returns `ShowStartScreen`. Recognized-flag matching is case-insensitive (`--HELP` routes to help) and uses ordinal comparison.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test file.**\n  This table covers every case the assignment requires: `--help`, `-h`, `-?`, `--version`, `-v`, a path arg, no args (=> cwd), and flags mixed with a path (help-wins-over-path). It also pins the precedence (help beats version) and the "unknown flag only falls through to cwd" behavior. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Cli/ArgRouterTests.cs` with the complete contents below.\n\n```csharp\nusing GitDelta.Core.Cli;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Cli;\n\npublic class ArgRouterTests\n{\n    private const string Cwd = @"C:\work\some-repo";\n\n    [Theory]\n    [InlineData("--help")]\n    [InlineData("-h")]\n    [InlineData("-?")]\n    [InlineData("--HELP")] // recognized flags are case-insensitive\n    public void Route_HelpFlag_ReturnsPrintHelp(string flag)\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { flag }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Theory]\n    [InlineData("--version")]\n    [InlineData("-v")]\n    [InlineData("--VERSION")] // recognized flags are case-insensitive\n    public void Route_VersionFlag_ReturnsPrintVersion(string flag)\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { flag }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_PathArg_ReturnsOpenRepoWorkingTreeWithThatPath()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { @"D:\projects\other-repo" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBe(@"D:\projects\other-repo");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_NoArgs_ReturnsOpenRepoWorkingTreeWithCwd()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(Array.Empty<string>(), Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBe(Cwd);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_HelpFlagMixedWithPath_HelpWins()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { @"D:\projects\other-repo", "--help" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_VersionFlagMixedWithPath_VersionWins()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { @"D:\projects\other-repo", "-v" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_HelpAndVersionTogether_HelpTakesPrecedence()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { "--version", "--help" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_FlagBeforePath_UsesFirstNonFlagArgAsPath()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { "--unknown", @"E:\repo" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBe(@"E:\repo");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_OnlyUnrecognizedFlag_FallsBackToCwd()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { "--unknown" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBe(Cwd);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Route_TwoPathArgs_UsesFirstNonFlagArg()\n    {\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(new[] { @"C:\first", @"C:\second" }, Cwd);\n\n        action.Kind.ShouldBe(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree);\n        action.RepoPath.ShouldBe(@"C:\first");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the test and confirm it FAILS to compile.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\n  Expected: the build fails with errors like `CS0103: The name 'ArgRouter' does not exist in the current context` (the `ArgRouter` class does not exist yet). This is the expected red state — no tests run because compilation fails.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Write the minimal `ArgRouter` implementation.**\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/ArgRouter.cs` with the complete contents below. It implements the exact precedence pinned by the tests.\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Cli;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Pure, WPF-free router that maps process command-line arguments plus the\n/// current working directory to a <see cref="LaunchAction"/>.\n/// </summary>\n/// <remarks>\n/// Precedence: help flags beat version flags, which beat a repo path, which\n/// beats the current working directory. This type never returns\n/// <see cref="LaunchActionKind.ShowStartScreen"/>; the application bootstrap\n/// downgrades an <see cref="LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree"/> result to\n/// the start screen when the path turns out not to be a git repository.\n/// </remarks>\npublic static class ArgRouter\n{\n    private static readonly string[] HelpFlags = { "--help", "-h", "-?" };\n    private static readonly string[] VersionFlags = { "--version", "-v" };\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Decides the launch action from raw command-line <paramref name="args"/>\n    /// (excluding the executable name) and the process <paramref name="cwd"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static LaunchAction Route(IReadOnlyList<string> args, string cwd)\n    {\n        for (var i = 0; i < args.Count; i++)\n        {\n            if (MatchesAny(args[i], HelpFlags))\n            {\n                return new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp);\n            }\n        }\n\n        for (var i = 0; i < args.Count; i++)\n        {\n            if (MatchesAny(args[i], VersionFlags))\n            {\n                return new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion);\n            }\n        }\n\n        for (var i = 0; i < args.Count; i++)\n        {\n            if (!IsFlag(args[i]))\n            {\n                return new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree, args[i]);\n            }\n        }\n\n        return new LaunchAction(LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree, cwd);\n    }\n\n    private static bool IsFlag(string arg) =>\n        arg.StartsWith('-');\n\n    private static bool MatchesAny(string arg, string[] flags)\n    {\n        foreach (var flag in flags)\n        {\n            if (string.Equals(arg, flag, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase))\n            {\n                return true;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return false;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests and confirm they PASS.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj\n```\n\n  Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 18, Skipped: 0` (10 `[Theory]` rows across the two flag tests plus 8 `[Fact]` cases = 18 executed test cases). The build must report `0 Warning(s)` — `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true` means any warning fails the run.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit the router and its tests.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Cli/ArgRouter.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Cli/ArgRouterTests.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add ArgRouter for CLI argument routing\n\nRoutes --help/-h/-?, --version/-v, a path arg, and no-args=>cwd to a\nLaunchAction, with help taking precedence over version and version over\na repo path. Covered by ArgRouterTests.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n## Phase 5: UI — App Bootstrap, DI, Shell Window & Theme\n\nThis phase wires up the WPF application host: `App.xaml` / `App.xaml.cs` (IHost + Autofac, three global exception handlers, structured logging), a `UiModule` and `LoggingModule`, a `ThemeService` that applies `AppSettings.Theme` via WPF-UI's `ApplicationThemeManager`, the `ui:FluentWindow` `MainWindow` shell, the `StartView`, and the 3-pane `ShellView` workspace with a placeholder for the Phase 7 `DiffView` control.\n\nThese are XAML views, App bootstrap, and a thin WPF-coupled `ThemeService` — none are unit-testable in isolation, so verification is **build + manual run**, not fake unit tests. The only exception is `ThemeService`'s pure mapping logic, which we extract into a static helper and TDD.\n\n> **Dependency note:** This phase references the ViewModels from the BACKBONE (`MainWindowViewModel`, `StartViewModel`, `ShellViewModel`, etc.) which are implemented in **Phase 6**. To keep this phase building on its own, the very first task adds **minimal stub ViewModels** that match the exact BACKBONE constructor signatures and the members the XAML binds to. Phase 6 replaces the stub bodies with the real implementations (same public surface), so the views written here keep compiling unchanged.\n\n---\n\n### Task 5.1: UI project file, WPF-UI packages, and minimal ViewModel stubs\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/AssemblyInfo.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/StartViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/ShellViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/WorkingTreeRowViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/FileRowViewModel.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/DiffDocumentViewModel.cs`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Pin the UI NuGet package versions in central package management.**\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props` and add the WPF-UI / MVVM / DI / hosting / logging packages inside the existing `<ItemGroup>` of `<PackageVersion>` entries. The `OnDispatcherUnhandledException` handler is implemented in `App.xaml.cs` (Task 5.3).\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the LoggingModule** (NLog → `%LOCALAPPDATA%\GitDelta\Logs`, registered as `ILogger<T>` for DI).\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/DependencyInjection/LoggingModule.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using Autofac;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n  using NLog.Extensions.Logging;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.DependencyInjection;\n\n  public sealed class LoggingModule : Module\n  {\n      protected override void Load(ContainerBuilder builder)\n      {\n          var logDir = Path.Combine(\n              Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.LocalApplicationData),\n              "GitDelta", "Logs");\n          Directory.CreateDirectory(logDir);\n\n          var config = new NLog.Config.LoggingConfiguration();\n          var fileTarget = new NLog.Targets.FileTarget("file")\n          {\n              FileName = Path.Combine(logDir, "gitdelta-${shortdate}.log"),\n              Layout = "${longdate} ${level:uppercase=true} ${logger} ${message} ${exception:format=tostring}",\n              MaxArchiveFiles = 14,\n              ArchiveAboveSize = 5_000_000,\n          };\n          var asyncTarget = new NLog.Targets.Wrappers.AsyncTargetWrapper(fileTarget);\n          config.AddRule(NLog.LogLevel.Info, NLog.LogLevel.Fatal, asyncTarget);\n          NLog.LogManager.Configuration = config;\n\n          builder.Register(_ =>\n              {\n                  var factory = LoggerFactory.Create(b => b.AddNLog());\n                  return factory;\n              })\n              .As<ILoggerFactory>()\n              .SingleInstance();\n\n          builder.RegisterGeneric(typeof(Logger<>))\n              .As(typeof(ILogger<>))\n              .SingleInstance();\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Create the UiModule** — composes **three** global exception handlers with structured logging. `DispatcherUnhandledException` is wired via XAML attribute (Task 5.2); the other two are wired in code here.\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Threading;\n  using Autofac;\n  using Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\n  using GitDelta.UI.DependencyInjection;\n  using GitDelta.UI.Services;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI;\n\n  public partial class App : Application\n  {\n      private IHost? _host;\n\n      protected override void OnStartup(StartupEventArgs e)\n      {\n          base.OnStartup(e);\n\n          // Global handler 2/3: exceptions on non-UI threads.\n          AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += OnDomainUnhandledException;\n\n          // Global handler 3/3: unobserved faulted Tasks.\n          TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException += OnUnobservedTaskException;\n\n          _host = Host.CreateDefaultBuilder()\n              .UseServiceProviderFactory(new AutofacServiceProviderFactory())\n              .ConfigureContainer<ContainerBuilder>(builder =>\n              {\n                  builder.RegisterModule<LoggingModule>();\n                  builder.RegisterModule<UiModule>();\n              })\n              .ConfigureServices(services =>\n              {\n                  services.AddHostedService<ApplicationHostService>();\n              })\n              .Build();\n\n          _host.Start();\n      }\n\n      protected override async void OnExit(ExitEventArgs e)\n      {\n          if (_host is not null)\n          {\n              await _host.StopAsync();\n              _host.Dispose();\n          }\n\n          NLog.LogManager.Shutdown();\n          base.OnExit(e);\n      }\n\n      // Global handler 1/3: exceptions on the WPF UI (Dispatcher) thread.\n      private void OnDispatcherUnhandledException(object sender, DispatcherUnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)\n      {\n          GetLogger()?.LogCritical(e.Exception, "Unhandled UI (dispatcher) exception");\n\n          MessageBox.Show(\n              $"An unexpected error occurred:\n\n{e.Exception.Message}",\n              "GitDelta",\n              MessageBoxButton.OK,\n              MessageBoxImage.Error);\n\n          // Keep the app alive after logging + notifying the user.\n          e.Handled = true;\n      }\n\n      private void OnDomainUnhandledException(object sender, UnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)\n      {\n          if (e.ExceptionObject is Exception ex)\n          {\n              GetLogger()?.LogCritical(ex, "Unhandled non-UI (AppDomain) exception. Terminating={Terminating}", e.IsTerminating);\n          }\n      }\n\n      private void OnUnobservedTaskException(object? sender, UnobservedTaskExceptionEventArgs e)\n      {\n          GetLogger()?.LogError(e.Exception, "Unobserved task exception");\n          e.SetObserved();\n      }\n\n      private ILogger<App>? GetLogger() =>\n          _host?.Services.GetService<ILoggerFactory>()?.CreateLogger<App>();\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > All three handlers log through the DI `ILoggerFactory` (NLog). None swallow silently: the dispatcher handler logs + shows a message and keeps running; the AppDomain handler logs a critical record; the Task handler logs an error and marks the exception observed. This satisfies the spec's "no silent/empty catches" rule.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the ApplicationHostService** — applies the saved theme via `IThemeService`, resolves the `MainWindow`, shows it, and kicks off CLI-routed initialization. It uses `ArgRouter` (from Core) on `Environment.GetCommandLineArgs()` to choose start vs. open-repo, then calls `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/ApplicationHostService.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Cli;\n  using GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\n  using GitDelta.UI.Views;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;\n  using Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\n  public sealed class ApplicationHostService : IHostedService\n  {\n      private readonly IServiceProvider _serviceProvider;\n      private readonly IThemeService _themeService;\n      private readonly ILogger<ApplicationHostService> _logger;\n\n      public ApplicationHostService(\n          IServiceProvider serviceProvider,\n          IThemeService themeService,\n          ILogger<ApplicationHostService> logger)\n      {\n          _serviceProvider = serviceProvider;\n          _themeService = themeService;\n          _logger = logger;\n      }\n\n      public Task StartAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n      {\n          if (Application.Current.Windows.OfType<MainWindow>().Any())\n          {\n              return Task.CompletedTask;\n          }\n\n          // Apply persisted theme before any window is shown to avoid a flash.\n          _themeService.ApplyFromSettings();\n\n          var window = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<MainWindow>();\n          var viewModel = _serviceProvider.GetRequiredService<MainWindowViewModel>();\n          window.DataContext = viewModel;\n\n          window.Loaded += async (_, _) =>\n          {\n              try\n              {\n                  var cliArgs = Environment.GetCommandLineArgs().Skip(1).ToArray();\n                  var action = ArgRouter.Route(cliArgs, Directory.GetCurrentDirectory());\n                  await viewModel.InitializeAsync(action, CancellationToken.None);\n              }\n              catch (Exception ex)\n              {\n                  _logger.LogError(ex, "Failed to initialize main window content");\n              }\n          };\n\n          window.Show();\n          return Task.CompletedTask;\n      }\n\n      public Task StopAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken) => Task.CompletedTask;\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > The `--help` / `--version` console fast-path (the `PrintHelp` / `PrintVersion` `LaunchActionKind`s and `AttachConsole`) is handled by a separate console-bootstrap task in the CLI phase, before the GUI host starts. This service handles only the GUI launch actions (`OpenRepoWorkingTree` / `ShowStartScreen`).\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  cd C:/code/projects/GitDelta; git add -A; git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add App host bootstrap and ApplicationHostService\n\n  IHost with AutofacServiceProviderFactory wiring LoggingModule and\n  UiModule, three global exception handlers (Dispatcher/AppDomain/\n  TaskScheduler) with structured logging, and a hosted service that\n  applies the saved theme, shows MainWindow, and runs CLI-routed init.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@</parameter>\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Task 5.4: ThemeService (TDD the pure mapping; thin WPF apply layer)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IThemeService.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/ThemeService.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Settings/ThemeMapping.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Settings/ThemeMappingTests.cs`\n\nThe WPF apply (`ApplicationThemeManager.Apply`) cannot be unit-tested, but the decision logic "given `AppTheme`, what should the effective dark/light resolution be when System is requested?" is pure. We extract that into a WPF-free helper in Core and TDD it; the `ThemeService` is a thin adapter that calls WPF-UI.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test for the pure theme-resolution helper.**\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Settings/ThemeMappingTests.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Settings;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Settings;\n\n  public class ThemeMappingTests\n  {\n      [Fact]\n      public void ResolveIsDark_Light_ReturnsFalse()\n      {\n          ThemeMapping.ResolveIsDark(AppTheme.Light, systemIsDark: true).ShouldBeFalse();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void ResolveIsDark_Dark_ReturnsTrue()\n      {\n          ThemeMapping.ResolveIsDark(AppTheme.Dark, systemIsDark: false).ShouldBeTrue();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void ResolveIsDark_System_FollowsSystemDark()\n      {\n          ThemeMapping.ResolveIsDark(AppTheme.System, systemIsDark: true).ShouldBeTrue();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void ResolveIsDark_System_FollowsSystemLight()\n      {\n          ThemeMapping.ResolveIsDark(AppTheme.System, systemIsDark: false).ShouldBeFalse();\n      }\n\n      [Theory]\n      [InlineData(AppTheme.Light, AppTheme.Dark)]\n      [InlineData(AppTheme.Dark, AppTheme.Light)]\n      [InlineData(AppTheme.System, AppTheme.Dark)]\n      public void Toggle_FromExplicitOrSystem_FlipsToOppositeOfCurrentEffective(AppTheme current, AppTheme expected)\n      {\n          // current effective dark? Light=>false, Dark=>true, System(systemIsDark:false)=>false.\n          ThemeMapping.Toggle(current, systemIsDark: false).ShouldBe(expected);\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the test and watch it fail to compile/run** (the helper does not exist yet).\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ThemeMappingTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: build error `The name 'ThemeMapping' does not exist` / `error CS0103`, i.e. FAIL (does not compile).\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Implement the pure helper in Core.**\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Settings/ThemeMapping.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.Core.Settings;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// WPF-free resolution of <see cref="AppTheme"/> into an effective dark/light decision.\n  /// Kept in Core so it is unit-testable without referencing WPF-UI.\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class ThemeMapping\n  {\n      /// <summary>Resolves whether the effective theme is dark.</summary>\n      public static bool ResolveIsDark(AppTheme theme, bool systemIsDark) => theme switch\n      {\n          AppTheme.Light => false,\n          AppTheme.Dark => true,\n          _ => systemIsDark,\n      };\n\n      /// <summary>Returns the explicit theme that is the opposite of the current effective theme.</summary>\n      public static AppTheme Toggle(AppTheme current, bool systemIsDark) =>\n          ResolveIsDark(current, systemIsDark) ? AppTheme.Light : AppTheme.Dark;\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Re-run the test, expect PASS.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ThemeMappingTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 7` (4 facts + 3 theory cases).\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Create the IThemeService interface** (UI-side adapter contract).\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IThemeService.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\n  public interface IThemeService\n  {\n      /// <summary>True when the effective application theme is dark.</summary>\n      bool IsDark { get; }\n\n      /// <summary>Loads the persisted <see cref="AppTheme"/> and applies it via WPF-UI.</summary>\n      void ApplyFromSettings();\n\n      /// <summary>Applies a specific theme and persists it.</summary>\n      void Apply(AppTheme theme);\n\n      /// <summary>Toggles between explicit light and dark, applies, and persists.</summary>\n      void Toggle();\n\n      /// <summary>Raised whenever the effective theme changes.</summary>\n      event Action<bool>? IsDarkChanged;\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Implement ThemeService** — a thin WPF-UI adapter that delegates the decision to the tested `ThemeMapping` helper, applies via `ApplicationThemeManager`, and persists through `ISettingsStore`.\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/ThemeService.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Settings;\n  using Wpf.Ui.Appearance;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\n  public sealed class ThemeService : IThemeService\n  {\n      private readonly ISettingsStore _settings;\n\n      public ThemeService(ISettingsStore settings)\n      {\n          _settings = settings;\n      }\n\n      public bool IsDark { get; private set; }\n\n      public event Action<bool>? IsDarkChanged;\n\n      public void ApplyFromSettings()\n      {\n          var theme = _settings.Load().Theme;\n          ApplyCore(theme);\n      }\n\n      public void Apply(AppTheme theme)\n      {\n          var current = _settings.Load();\n          _settings.Save(current with { Theme = theme });\n          ApplyCore(theme);\n      }\n\n      public void Toggle()\n      {\n          var current = _settings.Load().Theme;\n          var next = ThemeMapping.Toggle(current, SystemIsDark());\n          Apply(next);\n      }\n\n      private void ApplyCore(AppTheme theme)\n      {\n          switch (theme)\n          {\n              case AppTheme.Light:\n                  ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Light, WindowBackdropType.Mica, updateAccent: true);\n                  break;\n              case AppTheme.Dark:\n                  ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Dark, WindowBackdropType.Mica, updateAccent: true);\n                  break;\n              default:\n                  ApplicationThemeManager.ApplySystemTheme();\n                  break;\n          }\n\n          var resolved = ThemeMapping.ResolveIsDark(theme, SystemIsDark());\n          if (resolved != IsDark)\n          {\n              IsDark = resolved;\n              IsDarkChanged?.Invoke(IsDark);\n          }\n          else\n          {\n              IsDark = resolved;\n          }\n      }\n\n      private static bool SystemIsDark() =>\n          ApplicationThemeManager.GetSystemTheme() == SystemTheme.Dark;\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > If `ApplicationThemeManager.GetSystemTheme()` returns a `SystemTheme` value other than `Dark` (e.g. `Light`, `HCWhite`), `SystemIsDark()` is `false`, which is the correct light default. The `IsDarkChanged` event lets the diff control (Phase 7) swap its DarkPlus/LightPlus brushes.\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  cd C:/code/projects/GitDelta; git add -A; git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add ThemeService with TDD pure theme-resolution helper\n\n  ThemeMapping (Core, WPF-free, unit-tested) resolves AppTheme into a\n  dark/light decision; ThemeService adapts it onto WPF-UI\n  ApplicationThemeManager, persists via ISettingsStore, exposes IsDark.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@</parameter>\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Task 5.5: MainWindow — FluentWindow shell hosting CurrentContent\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/MainWindow.xaml`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/MainWindow.xaml.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/ViewLocators.xaml`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create a DataTemplate dictionary** that maps the content ViewModels to their views (so a `ContentControl` bound to `CurrentContent` renders the right `UserControl`). `StartView` and `ShellView` are created in Tasks 5.6 and 5.7.\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/ViewLocators.xaml`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <ResourceDictionary\n      xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"\n      xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"\n      xmlns:vm="clr-namespace:GitDelta.UI.ViewModels"\n      xmlns:views="clr-namespace:GitDelta.UI.Views">\n\n      <DataTemplate DataType="{x:Type vm:StartViewModel}">\n          <views:StartView />\n      </DataTemplate>\n\n      <DataTemplate DataType="{x:Type vm:ShellViewModel}">\n          <views:ShellView />\n      </DataTemplate>\n\n  </ResourceDictionary>\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Register the view-locator dictionary in App.xaml** so the templates are available app-wide.
