```\n\n  > The Open Folder button binds to `CurrentContent.OpenFolderCommand`; both `StartViewModel` and `ShellViewModel` expose an `OpenFolderCommand` (BACKBONE), so the binding resolves regardless of which content is active. `RepoName` is only present on `ShellViewModel`, so the `FallbackValue=''` keeps it blank on the start screen. The theme toggle goes through code-behind to call `IThemeService.Toggle()` directly (a window-level concern, not content-specific).\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Create MainWindow.xaml.cs** — inherits `FluentWindow`, implements `IWindow`, watches the system theme, and routes the theme-toggle click to the injected `IThemeService`.\n\n  File `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/MainWindow.xaml.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using GitDelta.UI.Services;\n  using Wpf.Ui.Appearance;\n  using Wpf.Ui.Controls;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Views;\n\n  public partial class MainWindow : FluentWindow, IWindow\n  {\n      private readonly IThemeService _themeService;\n\n      public MainWindow(IThemeService themeService)\n      {\n          _themeService = themeService;\n          InitializeComponent();\n\n          // Track Windows light/dark changes while AppTheme.System is in effect.\n          SystemThemeWatcher.Watch(this);\n      }\n\n      private void OnToggleThemeClick(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)\n      {\n          _themeService.Toggle();\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > The window's `DataContext` (the `MainWindowViewModel`) is assigned by `ApplicationHostService` (Task 5.3), not in the constructor, so the window can stay a DI singleton while its content is driven by the host.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Add the MainWindow IWindow note to the manifest — none needed; build now.** Because `StartView` and `ShellView` referenced by `ViewLocators.xaml` do not exist yet, do **not** build the full UI project here. All testable logic is driven by TDD against `tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests` with xUnit v3 + NSubstitute + Shouldly, mocking `IGitReader`, `IIntraLineDiffer`, and `ISettingsStore`. To keep `OpenFolder` testable without a real WPF dialog, this phase introduces an `IFolderPicker` abstraction in `GitDelta.UI` (the concrete WPF implementation is registered in the UI Autofac module in Phase 9).\n\nAssumptions carried in from earlier phases: the solution, projects, central package management, `Directory.Build.props` (`Nullable=enable`, `ImplicitUsings=enable`, `LangVersion=14`, `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true`), the entire `GitDelta.Core` surface (Models, Git, Diff, Cli, Settings), and the `GitDelta.UI.UnitTests` project (referencing `GitDelta.UI`, with xUnit v3 + NSubstitute + Shouldly package references) all already exist and build. Every command below uses absolute paths and assumes the working directory is `C:/code/projects/GitDelta` unless stated.\n\n> Convention for this phase: all ViewModels are `public partial class ... : ObservableObject` (CommunityToolkit.Mvvm). `[ObservableProperty]` generates the public CLR property from the private backing field (`_isBusy` → `IsBusy`). `[RelayCommand]` on `Foo`/`FooAsync` generates `FooCommand`. Tests call the generated members.\n\n---\n\n### Task 6.1: IFolderPicker abstraction + CommitRowViewModel\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IFolderPicker.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModelTests.cs`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the IFolderPicker abstraction.** This is a pure interface (not unit-testable on its own; it exists so other ViewModels can be tested with a mock). The WPF implementation is registered in\n/// the UI Autofac module (Phase 9).\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IFolderPicker\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Shows a folder-selection dialog. Returns the chosen absolute folder\n    /// path, or <c>null</c> if the user cancelled.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name="title">Dialog title.</param>\n    string? "1 minute ago" : $"{m} minutes ago";\n        }\n        if (delta.TotalHours < 24)\n        {\n            int h = (int)delta.TotalHours;\n            return h == 1 ? "1 hour ago" : $"{h} hours ago";\n        }\n        if (delta.TotalDays < 30)\n        {\n            int d = (int)delta.TotalDays;\n            return d == 1 ? "1 day ago" : $"{d} days ago";\n        }\n        if (delta.TotalDays < 365)\n        {\n            int mo = (int)(delta.TotalDays / 30);\n            return mo == 1 ? "1 month ago" : $"{mo} months ago";\n        }\n\n        int y = (int)(delta.TotalDays / 365);\n        return y == 1 ? "1 year ago" : $"{y} years ago";\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test Added { get; }\n    public int? Deleted { get; }\n    public bool IsBinary { get; }\n    public string StatusGlyph { get; }\n\n    private static string MapGlyph(ChangeKind kind) => kind switch\n    {\n        ChangeKind.Added => "A",\n        ChangeKind.Modified => "M",\n        ChangeKind.Deleted => "D",\n        ChangeKind.Renamed => "R",\n        ChangeKind.Copied => "C",\n        ChangeKind.TypeChanged => "T",\n        ChangeKind.Untracked => "U",\n        ChangeKind.Conflicted => "!",\n        _ => "?"\n    };\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Run both tests and confirm they PASS.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~WorkingTreeRowViewModelTests|FullyQualifiedName~FileRowViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 11`.\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Holds the current\n/// <see cref="FileDiff"/> plus the view-affecting toggles.\n/// </summary>\npublic partial class DiffDocumentViewModel : ObservableObject\n{\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private FileDiff? _fileDiff;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private DiffViewMode _viewMode = DiffViewMode.SideBySide;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _showWhitespace;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _wordWrap;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private int _tabSize = 4;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private string? _syntaxLanguageId;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _isDarkTheme;\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void ToggleViewMode()\n    {\n        ViewMode = ViewMode == DiffViewMode.SideBySide\n            ? DiffViewMode.Unified\n            : DiffViewMode.SideBySide;\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void ToggleWhitespace()\n    {\n        ShowWhitespace = !ShowWhitespace;\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void ToggleWordWrap()\n    {\n        WordWrap = !WordWrap;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffDocumentViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.ComponentModel;\nusing CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.Input;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Bindable mirror of <see cref="AppSettings"/> for the settings dialog.\n/// <see cref="Result"/> exposes the (possibly edited) settings; the shell\n/// inspects <see cref="SaveRequested"/> to decide whether to persist.\n/// </summary>\npublic partial class SettingsViewModel : ObservableObject\n{\n    private readonly AppSettings _original;\n\n    public SettingsViewModel(AppSettings current)\n    {\n        _original = current;\n        _theme = current.Theme;\n        _defaultDiffView = current.DefaultDiffView;\n        _contextLines = current.ContextLines;\n        _tabSize = current.TabSize;\n        _syntaxHighlighting = current.SyntaxHighlighting;\n        _externalEditorCommand = current.ExternalEditorCommand;\n        Result = current;\n    }\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private AppTheme _theme;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private DiffViewMode _defaultDiffView;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private int _contextLines;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private int _tabSize;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _syntaxHighlighting;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private string? _externalEditorCommand;\n\n    /// <summary>The settings to apply once the dialog closes.</summary>\n    public AppSettings Result { get; private set; }\n\n    /// <summary>True after <see cref="SaveCommand"/> has executed.</summary>\n    public bool SaveRequested { get; private set; }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void Save()\n    {\n        Result = _original with\n        {\n            Theme = Theme,\n            DefaultDiffView = DefaultDiffView,\n            ContextLines = ContextLines,\n            TabSize = TabSize,\n            SyntaxHighlighting = SyntaxHighlighting,\n            ExternalEditorCommand = ExternalEditorCommand\n        };\n        SaveRequested = true;\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void Cancel()\n    {\n        Result = _original;\n        SaveRequested = false;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test GitDelta needs Git for Windows " +\n        "(version 2.30 or newer). Install it, then restart GitDelta.";\n\n    /// <summary>Raised with the chosen absolute folder path.</summary>\n    public event Action<string>? RepositorySelected;\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private Task OpenFolderAsync()\n    {\n        string? folder = _folderPicker.PickFolder("Open a Git repository");\n        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(folder))\n        {\n            RepositorySelected?.Invoke(folder);\n        }\n\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~StartViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 4`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/StartViewModel.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/ViewModels/StartViewModelTests.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): add StartViewModel with folder picker and git-missing warning\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 6.6: ShellViewModel — construction, LoadRepositoryAsync, git-missing handling\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/ShellViewModel.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/ViewModels/ShellViewModelTests.cs`\n\nThis task creates `ShellViewModel` with its full public surface but implements only construction + `LoadRepositoryAsync`. GitDelta.Core.Git;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Settings;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Diff;\nusing GitDelta.UI.Services;\nusing GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\nusing NSubstitute;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.ViewModels;\n\npublic class ShellViewModelTests\n{\n    private readonly IGitReader _git = Substitute.For<IGitReader>();\n    private = Substitute.For<IFolderPicker>();\n\n    public ShellViewModelTests()\n    {\n        _settings.Load().Returns(new AppSettings());\n        _git.CheckGitAsync(Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n            .Returns(new GitAvailability(true, "2.40.1", true));\n        _git.GetHistoryAsync(Arg.Any<string>(), Arg.Any<int>(), Arg.Any<int>(), Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n            .Returns(Array.Empty<CommitInfo>());\n        _git.GetChangedFilesAsync(Arg.Any<string>(), Arg.Any<DiffSpec>(), Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n            .Returns(Array.Empty<ChangedFile>());\n    }\n\n    private ShellViewModel Create() =>\n        new(_git, _intra, _settings, _picker);\n\n    private static CommitInfo Commit(string sha, params string[] parents) =>\n        new(sha, sha[..Math.Min(7, sha.Length)], parents,\n            "A", "a@x", DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch,\n            "A", "a@x", DateTimeOffset.UnixEpoch, "subject", "body");\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void        sut.Diff.ShouldNotBeNull();\n        sut.WorkingTreeRow.ShouldNotBeNull();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task LoadRepositoryAsync_SetsRepoRootAndName_AndMarksLoaded()\n    {\n        var sut = Create();\n\n        await sut.LoadRepositoryAsync(@"C:\code\projects\GitDelta", CancellationToken.None);\n\n        sut.RepoRoot.ShouldBe(@"C:\code\projects\GitDelta");\n        sut.RepoName.ShouldBe("GitDelta");\n        sut.IsRepoLoaded.ShouldBeTrue();\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task LoadRepositoryAsync_PopulatesHistoryFromGitReader()\n    {\n        _git.GetHistoryAsync(Arg.Any<string>(), 0, Arg.Any<int>(), Arg.Any<CancellationToken>())\n            .Returns(new[] { Commit("aaaaaaa1"), Commit("bbbbbbb2") });\n        var sut = Create();\n\n        await sut.LoadRepositoryAsync(@"C:\repo", CancellationToken.None);\n\n        sut.History.Count.ShouldBe(2);\n        sut.History[0].Sha.ShouldBe("aaaaaaa1");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task LoadRepositoryAsync_DefaultsToWorkingTreeComparison()\n    {\n        var sut = Create();\n\n        await sut.LoadRepositoryAsync(@"C:\repo", CancellationToken.None);\n\n        sut.WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected.ShouldBeTrue();\n        await _git.Received().GetChangedFilesAsync(\n            @"C:\repo",\n            Arg.Is<DiffSpec>(s => s is DiffSpec.WorkingTreeVsHead),\n            Arg.Any<CancellationToken>());\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public async Task LoadRepositoryAsync_WhenGitMissing_SetsStatusMessage_AndDoesNotLoad()\n    {\n (Tasks 6.7 and 6.8 extend this same file; the members they fill in are present as stubs here so the type compiles and the collections exist.)\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Collections.ObjectModel;\nusing System.IO;\nusing CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.ComponentModel;\nusing CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.Input;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Diff;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Git;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Settings;\nusing GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// The 3-pane workspace: history (left), changed files (middle), diff (right).\n/// Owns the selection-to-DiffSpec recomputation and orchestrates IGitReader.\n/// </summary>\npublic partial class ShellViewModel : ObservableObject\n{\n    private const int HistoryPageSize = 100;\n\n    private readonly IGitReader _gitReader;\n    private readonly IIntraLineDiffer _intraLineDiffer;\n    private readonly ISettingsStore _settings;\n    private readonly IFolderPicker _folderPicker;\n\n    private AppSettings _appSettings;\n    private int _historyLoaded;\n\n    public ShellViewModel(\n        IGitReader gitReader,\n        IIntraLineDiffer intraLineDiffer,\n        ISettingsStore settings,\n        IFolderPicker folderPicker)\n    {\n        _gitReader = gitReader;\n        _intraLineDiffer = intraLineDiffer;\n        _settings = settings;\n        _folderPicker = folderPicker;\n        _appSettings = settings.Load();\n\n        WorkingTreeRow = new WorkingTreeRowViewModel();\n        Diff = new DiffDocumentViewModel\n        {\n            ViewMode = _appSettings.DefaultDiffView,\n            TabSize = _appSettings.TabSize,\n            IsDarkTheme = _appSettings.Theme == AppTheme.Dark\n        };\n    }\n\n    public string? RepoRoot { get; private set; }\n    public string? RepoName { get; private set; }\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _isRepoLoaded;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private bool _isBusy;\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private string? _statusMessage;\n\n    public WorkingTreeRowViewModel WorkingTreeRow { get; }\n\n    public ObservableCollection<CommitRowViewModel> History { get; } = [];\n\n    public ObservableCollection<CommitRowViewModel> SelectedCommits { get; } = [];\n\n    public ObservableCollection<FileRowViewModel> ChangedFiles { get; } = [];\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private FileRowViewModel? _selectedFile;\n\n    public DiffDocumentViewModel Diff { get; }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Loads a repository: validates git, sets RepoRoot/RepoName, loads the\n    /// first history page, and shows the working-tree-vs-HEAD comparison.\n    /// </summary>\n    public async Task LoadRepositoryAsync(string repoRoot, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        IsBusy = true;\n        try\n        {\n            GitAvailability availability = await _gitReader.CheckGitAsync(ct);\n            if (!availability.IsInstalled)\n            {\n                StatusMessage = "Git was not found on your PATH. " +\n                    "Install Git for Windows (2.30 or newer) and restart GitDelta.";\n                IsRepoLoaded = false;\n                return;\n            }\n\n            if (!availability.MeetsMinimum)\n            {\n                StatusMessage = $"Git {availability.Version} is too old. " +\n                    "GitDelta needs Git 2.30 or newer.";\n                IsRepoLoaded = false;\n                return;\n            }\n\n            RepoRoot = repoRoot;\n            RepoName = GetRepoName(repoRoot);\n\n            History.Clear();\n            SelectedCommits.Clear();\n            _historyLoaded = 0;\n\n            IReadOnlyList<CommitInfo> page =\n                await _gitReader.GetHistoryAsync(repoRoot, 0, HistoryPageSize, ct);\n            foreach (CommitInfo commit in page)\n            {\n                History.Add(new CommitRowViewModel(commit));\n            }\n\n            _historyLoaded = page.Count;\n            IsRepoLoaded = true;\n            StatusMessage = null;\n\n            SelectWorkingTree();\n            await RecomputeComparisonAsync(ct);\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            IsBusy = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static string GetRepoName(string repoRoot)\n    {\n        string trimmed = repoRoot.TrimEnd('/', '\\');\n        string name = Path.GetFileName(trimmed);\n        return string.IsNullOrEmpty(name) ? trimmed : name;\n    }\n\n    // --- Filled in by Task 6.7 (comparison) and 6.8 (diff + commands) ---\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void SelectWorkingTree()\n    {\n        WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected = true;\n        foreach (CommitRowViewModel row in History)\n        {\n            row.IsSelected = false;\n        }\n        SelectedCommits.Clear();\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Builds the current DiffSpec from selection and loads ChangedFiles.\n    /// </summary>\n    public Task SetComparisonAsync(DiffSpec spec, CancellationToken ct) =>\n        Task.CompletedTask; // implemented in Task 6.7\n\n    private Task RecomputeComparisonAsync(CancellationToken ct) =>\n        Task.CompletedTask; // implemented in Task 6.7\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ShellViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 6`. (`LoadRepositoryAsync_DefaultsToWorkingTreeComparison` passes because `SelectWorkingTree` sets `WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected` and `RecomputeComparisonAsync` — implemented in 6.7 — already calls `GetChangedFilesAsync`. FAIL.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ShellViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: build `GetChangedFilesAsync` for non-working-tree specs). RED.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Replace the comparison stubs with the full implementation.** In `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/ShellViewModel.cs`, replace the `SelectWorkingTree`, `SetComparisonAsync`, and `RecomputeComparisonAsync` members (everything under the `// --- Filled in by Task 6.7 ...` comment) with:\n\n```csharp\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private async Task SelectWorkingTreeAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected = true;\n        foreach (CommitRowViewModel row in History)\n        {\n            row.IsSelected = false;\n        }\n        SelectedCommits.Clear();\n        await RecomputeComparisonAsync(ct);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Toggles selection of a commit row and recomputes the comparison.\n    /// At most two commits may be selected; selecting a third drops the\n    /// oldest selection (FIFO).\n    /// </summary>\n    public async Task SelectCommitAsync(CommitRowViewModel commit, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected = false;\n\n        if (SelectedCommits.Contains(commit))\n        {\n            SelectedCommits.Remove(commit);\n            commit.IsSelected = false;\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            SelectedCommits.Add(commit);\n            commit.IsSelected = true;\n\n            while (SelectedCommits.Count > 2)\n            {\n                CommitRowViewModel dropped = SelectedCommits[0];\n                SelectedCommits.RemoveAt(0);\n                dropped.IsSelected = false;\n            }\n        }\n\n        await RecomputeComparisonAsync(ct);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Loads ChangedFiles for the given spec into the middle pane.\n    /// </summary>\n    public async Task SetComparisonAsync(DiffSpec spec, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        if (RepoRoot is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        IsBusy = true;\n        try\n        {\n            IReadOnlyList<ChangedFile> files =\n                await _gitReader.GetChangedFilesAsync(RepoRoot, spec, ct);\n\n            ChangedFiles.Clear();\n            foreach (ChangedFile file in files)\n            {\n                ChangedFiles.Add(new FileRowViewModel(file));\n            }\n\n            SelectedFile = null;\n            Diff.FileDiff = null;\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            IsBusy = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private async Task RecomputeComparisonAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        DiffSpec? spec = BuildSpecFromSelection();\n        if (spec is null)\n        {\n            ChangedFiles.Clear();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        await SetComparisonAsync(spec, ct);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Maps the current selection to a DiffSpec:\n    /// working tree => WorkingTreeVsHead; one commit => CommitVsParent;\n    /// two commits => TwoCommits(older, newer). History is newest-first,\n    /// so the higher index is the older (base) commit.\n    /// </summary>\n    private DiffSpec? BuildSpecFromSelection()\n    {\n        if (WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected)\n        {\n            return new DiffSpec.WorkingTreeVsHead();\n        }\n\n        if (SelectedCommits.Count == 1)\n        {\n            return new DiffSpec.CommitVsParent(SelectedCommits[0].Sha);\n        }\n\n        if (SelectedCommits.Count == 2)\n        {\n            int indexA = History.IndexOf(SelectedCommits[0]);\n            int indexB = History.IndexOf(SelectedCommits[1]);\n\n            // Larger index = older = base; smaller index = newer = target.\n            CommitRowViewModel older = indexA >= indexB ? SelectedCommits[0] : SelectedCommits[1];\n            CommitRowViewModel newer = indexA >= indexB ? SelectedCommits[1] : SelectedCommits[0];\n\n            return new DiffSpec.TwoCommits(older.Sha, newer.Sha);\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n```\n\n> Note: this renames the parameterless `SelectWorkingTree` command to the async `SelectWorkingTreeAsync` (generating `SelectWorkingTreeCommand`). Update the call site inside `LoadRepositoryAsync` accordingly in the next step.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Update the LoadRepositoryAsync call site.** In `ShellViewModel.cs`, inside `LoadRepositoryAsync`, replace the two lines:\n\n```csharp\n            SelectWorkingTree();\n            await RecomputeComparisonAsync(ct);\n```\n\nwith:\n\n```csharp\n            await SelectWorkingTreeAsync(ct);\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run all ShellViewModel tests and confirm they PASS.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ShellViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 10` (the 6 from Task 6.6 + 4 new). RepositoryOpenRequested;\n\n    /// <summary>Raised when the user opens the settings dialog.</summary>\n    public event Action? SettingsRequested;\n\n    /// <summary>Raised with the absolute path of the file to open externally.</summary>\n    public event Action<string>? EditorRequested;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Loads the per-file diff for the current comparison, enriches it with\n    /// intra-line spans, and pushes it into the diff document.\n    /// </summary>\n    public async Task ShowFileDiffAsync(FileRowViewModel file, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        if (RepoRoot is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        DiffSpec? spec = BuildSpecFromSelection();\n        if (spec is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        SelectedFile = file;\n        IsBusy = true;\n        try\n        {\n            FileDiff diff = await _gitReader.GetFileDiffAsync(\n                RepoRoot, spec, file.DisplayPath, _appSettings.ContextLines, ct);\n\n            FileDiff enriched = IntraLineEnricher.Enrich(diff, _intraLineDiffer);\n\n            Diff.SyntaxLanguageId = _appSettings.SyntaxHighlighting\n                ? LanguageIdFromPath(file.DisplayPath)\n                : null;\n            Diff.FileDiff = enriched;\n        }\n        finally\n        {\n            IsBusy = false;\n        }\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private Task OpenFolderAsync()\n    {\n        string? folder = _folderPicker.PickFolder("Open a Git repository");\n        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(folder))\n        {\n            RepositoryOpenRequested?.Invoke(folder);\n        }\n\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private async Task RefreshAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        await RecomputeComparisonAsync(ct);\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private async Task LoadMoreHistoryAsync(CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        if (RepoRoot is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        IReadOnlyList<CommitInfo> page =\n            await _gitReader.GetHistoryAsync(RepoRoot, _historyLoaded, HistoryPageSize, ct);\n        foreach (CommitInfo commit in page)\n        {\n            History.Add(new CommitRowViewModel(commit));\n        }\n\n        _historyLoaded += page.Count;\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void ToggleTheme()\n    {\n        bool nowDark = !Diff.IsDarkTheme;\n        Diff.IsDarkTheme = nowDark;\n\n        _appSettings = _appSettings with\n        {\n            Theme = nowDark ? AppTheme.Dark : AppTheme.Light\n        };\n        _settings.Save(_appSettings);\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void OpenSettings()\n    {\n        SettingsRequested?.Invoke();\n    }\n\n    [RelayCommand]\n    private void OpenFileInEditor()\n    {\n        if (SelectedFile is null || RepoRoot is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        string absolute = Path.Combine(RepoRoot, SelectedFile.DisplayPath);\n        EditorRequested?.Invoke(absolute);\n    }\n\n    private static string? LanguageIdFromPath(string path)\n    {\n        string ext = Path.GetExtension(path).TrimStart('.').ToLowerInvariant();\n        return ext.Length == 0 ? null : ext;\n    }\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Reconcile applied settings on save.** `ShowFileDiffAsync` and `ToggleTheme` both read/replace `_appSettings`; confirm the field is mutable (`private AppSettings _appSettings;` declared in Task 6.6). Routes the launch action to either the start\n/// screen (<see cref="StartViewModel"/>) or the workspace\n/// (<see cref="ShellViewModel"/>), and swaps content when the user opens a\n/// different repository.\n/// </summary>\npublic partial class MainWindowViewModel : ObservableObject\n{\n    private readonly IGitReader _gitReader;\n    private readonly ISettingsStore _settings;\n    private readonly Func<StartViewModel> _startFactory;\n    private readonly Func<ShellViewModel> _shellFactory;\n\n    public MainWindowViewModel(\n        IGitReader gitReader,\n        ISettingsStore settings,\n        Func<StartViewModel> startFactory,\n        Func<ShellViewModel> shellFactory)\n    {\n        _gitReader = gitReader;\n        _settings = settings;\n        _startFactory = startFactory;\n        _shellFactory = shellFactory;\n    }\n\n    [ObservableProperty]\n    private ObservableObject? _currentContent;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Routes the parsed launch action. PrintHelp/PrintVersion are handled by\n    /// the bootstrap before the window appears, so here they fall through to\n    /// the start screen. OpenRepoWorkingTree resolves the repo root; if it is\n    /// not a repository, falls back to the start screen.\n    /// </summary>\n    public async Task InitializeAsync(LaunchAction action, CancellationToken ct)\n    {\n        switch (action.Kind)\n        {\n            case LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree:\n                string start = action.RepoPath ?? Directory.GetCurrentDirectory();\n                string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(start, ct);\n                if (root is null)\n                {\n                    await ShowStartAsync();\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    await OpenRepositoryAsync(root);\n                }\n                break;\n\n            case LaunchActionKind.ShowStartScreen:\n            case LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp:\n            case LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion:\n            default:\n                await ShowStartAsync();\n                break;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Shows the start screen and wires its repository-selected event.</summary>\n    public Task ShowStartAsync()\n    {\n        StartViewModel start = _startFactory();\n        start.RepositorySelected += OnRepositorySelected;\n        CurrentContent = start;\n        return Task.CompletedTask;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Loads the repository at <paramref name="repoRoot"/> into the shell.</summary>\n    public async Task OpenRepositoryAsync(string repoRoot)\n    {\n        ShellViewModel shell = _shellFactory();\n        shell.RepositoryOpenRequested += OnShellRepositoryOpenRequested;\n        CurrentContent = shell;\n        await shell.LoadRepositoryAsync(repoRoot, CancellationToken.None);\n    }\n\n    private async void OnRepositorySelected(string folder)\n    {\n        string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);\n        await OpenRepositoryAsync(root ?? folder);\n    }\n\n    private async void OnShellRepositoryOpenRequested(string folder)\n    {\n        string? root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);\n        await OpenRepositoryAsync(root ?? folder);\n    }\n}\n```\n\n> Note the `using System.IO;` is supplied by `ImplicitUsings` for `Directory`; if `TreatWarningsAsErrors` flags it as ambiguous it is already covered. If the build complains `Directory` is not found, add `using System.IO;` at the top.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the test and confirm it PASSES.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~MainWindowViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 7`. If `StartScreen_RepositorySelected_OpensThatRepository` is flaky because of the `async void` event handler, the `await Task.Yield()` in the test plus the synchronous (mocked, completed) `FindRepositoryRootAsync` make the continuation run before the assertion; if it still races, the mock returning a completed `Task` from `Returns(...)` guarantees synchronous completion.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModelTests.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): add MainWindowViewModel routing start screen vs shell\n\nInitializeAsync routes each LaunchActionKind; OpenRepoWorkingTree resolves\nthe repo root and falls back to the start screen when the path is not a repo.\nOpenRepositoryAsync loads the shell; start-screen and shell open events both\nre-resolve and switch repositories.\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n---\n\n### Task 6.10: Full ViewModel suite green + zero-warning build gate\n\n**Files:**\n- Verify only (no new files).\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Run the entire UI unit-test project.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: all Phase 6 tests pass — `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 62` (5 + 4 + 1 [WorkingTree 4 / FileRow 7 = 11] ... concretely: CommitRow 5, WorkingTree 4, FileRow 7, DiffDocument 5, Settings 5, Start 4, Shell 19, MainWindow 7 = 56). AvalonEdit text rendering, background painting, margin drawing, and scroll-sync are **not unit-testable** (they require a live WPF visual tree and a windowed render pass), so every task here uses **implementation + `dotnet build` + a manual run-and-observe verification**, never a fake unit test. The Core diff model (`FileDiff`, `DiffHunk`, `DiffLine`, `IntraSpan`) from earlier phases is the single source of truth fed into this control.\n\nTask 7.1 ships an **MVP escape hatch** (DiffPlex.Wpf) so the shell is wireable immediately; Tasks 7.2–7.9 build the real AvalonEdit `DiffView` per the BACKBONE contract; Phase 8 layers TextMate syntax on top.\n\n### Task 7.1: MVP fallback — DiffPlex.Wpf SideBySideDiffViewer host control\n\n> NOTE (execution): SKIPPED intentionally. The real AvalonEdit `DiffView`\n> (Tasks 7.2–7.9 + Phase 8) was implemented directly and builds/tests clean,\n> so the DiffPlex.Wpf escape hatch was never needed. DiffPlex.Wpf is not\n> referenced. This task is left unchecked by design.\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml.cs`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n\nThis is the documented MVP escape hatch from spec §8: ship DiffPlex.Wpf's `SideBySideDiffViewer` first so the shell has a working diff pane before the bespoke AvalonEdit `DiffView` (Task 7.2+) is finished. The Core `FileDiff` model is reused: we reconstruct old/new text from the hunks and let DiffPlex.Wpf re-diff for display. When the real `DiffView` is ready, the shell swaps the control and deletes this file; nothing in Core changes.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Pin the DiffPlex.Wpf package version centrally**\n\n  Add the WPF rendering package alongside the existing DiffPlex core entry in central package management. Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props` and add the `PackageVersion` line inside the existing `<ItemGroup>`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <PackageVersion Include="DiffPlex.Wpf" Version="1.4.4" />\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Reference DiffPlex.Wpf from the UI project**\n\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` and add inside the package `<ItemGroup>` (version omitted — central management supplies it):\n\n  ```xml\n  <PackageReference Include="DiffPlex.Wpf" />\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Add a static text reconstructor that turns a FileDiff into old/new text**\n\n  DiffPlex.Wpf wants two plain strings. We rebuild them from the hunks: deleted+context lines form the "old" side, added+context lines form the "new" side. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml.cs` with this complete content (XAML follows in Step 4):\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Text;\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Controls;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// MVP escape hatch (spec §8): hosts DiffPlex.Wpf's SideBySideDiffViewer.\n  /// Reconstructs old/new text from the Core FileDiff hunks and lets DiffPlex.Wpf\n  /// re-diff for display. Replaced by the AvalonEdit DiffView (Task 7.2+).\n  /// </summary>\n  public partial class MvpDiffView : UserControl\n  {\n      public static readonly DependencyProperty FileDiffProperty =\n          DependencyProperty.Register(\n              nameof(FileDiff), typeof(FileDiff), typeof(MvpDiffView),\n              new PropertyMetadata(null, OnFileDiffChanged));\n\n      public FileDiff? FileDiff\n      {\n          get => (FileDiff?)GetValue(FileDiffProperty);\n          set => SetValue(FileDiffProperty, value);\n      }\n\n      public MvpDiffView()\n      {\n          InitializeComponent();\n      }\n\n      private static void OnFileDiffChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)\n      {\n          ((MvpDiffView)d).Render((FileDiff?)e.NewValue);\n      }\n\n      private void Render(FileDiff? diff)\n      {\n          if (diff is null)\n          {\n              Viewer.OldText = string.Empty;\n              Viewer.NewText = string.Empty;\n              return;\n          }\n\n          if (diff.IsBinary)\n          {\n              Viewer.OldText = "(binary file — no textual diff)";\n              Viewer.NewText = "(binary file — no textual diff)";\n              return;\n          }\n\n          var (oldText, newText) = Reconstruct(diff);\n          Viewer.OldText = oldText;\n          Viewer.NewText = newText;\n\n          if (diff.IsTruncated)\n          {\n              Viewer.NewText += Environment.NewLine + "… (diff truncated — file too large)";\n          }\n      }\n\n      private static (string OldText, string NewText) Reconstruct(FileDiff diff)\n      {\n          var oldSb = new StringBuilder();\n          var newSb = new StringBuilder();\n          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)\n          {\n              foreach (DiffLine line in hunk.Lines)\n              {\n                  switch (line.Kind)\n                  {\n                      case DiffLineKind.Context:\n                          oldSb.AppendLine(line.Text);\n                          newSb.AppendLine(line.Text);\n                          break;\n                      case DiffLineKind.Deleted:\n                          oldSb.AppendLine(line.Text);\n                          break;\n                      case DiffLineKind.Added:\n                          newSb.AppendLine(line.Text);\n                          break;\n                  }\n              }\n          }\n\n          return (oldSb.ToString(), newSb.ToString());\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Add the XAML that hosts the DiffPlex.Wpf viewer**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <UserControl\n      x:Class="GitDelta.UI.Controls.MvpDiffView"\n      xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"\n      xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"\n      xmlns:diffwpf="clr-namespace:DiffPlex.Wpf.Controls;assembly=DiffPlex.Wpf">\n      <Grid Background="{DynamicResource ApplicationBackgroundBrush}">\n          <diffwpf:SideBySideDiffViewer x:Name="Viewer" />\n      </Grid>\n  </UserControl>\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 5: Build the UI project**\n\n  Run from `C:/code/projects/GitDelta`:\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. (Note: `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true` means any nullable or obsolete warning fails the build — there should be none here.)\n\n- [ ] **Step 6: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/MvpDiffView.xaml.cs Directory.Packages.props src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add DiffPlex.Wpf MVP diff view escape hatch\n\n  Hosts SideBySideDiffViewer, reconstructing old/new text from the Core\n  FileDiff model. Lets the shell wire a working diff pane before the\n  bespoke AvalonEdit DiffView lands. Binary and truncated fallbacks included.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.2: AvalonEdit packages + DiffView skeleton with all dependency properties\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`\n\nThis task establishes the real `DiffView : UserControl` exactly per the BACKBONE contract: all seven dependency properties (`FileDiff`, `ViewMode`, `ShowWhitespace`, `WordWrap`, `TabSize`, `SyntaxLanguageId`, `IsDarkTheme`) with CLR wrappers, plus stub bodies for the four public methods (`GoToNextChange`, `GoToPreviousChange`, `ShowFind`, `CopySelection`). Rendering wiring comes in later tasks; this is the contract surface and the two-`TextEditor` layout.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Pin AvalonEdit centrally**\n\n  Add to the `<ItemGroup>` in `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <PackageVersion Include="AvalonEdit" Version="6.3.1.120" />\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Reference AvalonEdit and allow net6.0-windows forward-compat**\n\n  AvalonEdit 6.3.1.120 ships `net6.0-windows` assemblies; they load fine on net10 but the SDK emits NU1701-style and possible nullable/obsolete warnings. With `TreatWarningsAsErrors=true` (spec §15 risk) we scope a `NoWarn` to keep zero-warning builds. In `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` add inside the package `<ItemGroup>`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <PackageReference Include="AvalonEdit" />\n  ```\n\n  Then add a dedicated property group at the end of the same csproj (before `</Project>`):\n\n  ```xml\n  <PropertyGroup>\n    <!-- AvalonEdit 6.x ships net6.0-windows assemblies; loads forward-compat on net10.\n         Scope-suppress the cross-targeting restore warning only (spec §15 risk). -->\n    <NoWarn>$(NoWarn);NU1701</NoWarn>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Create the DiffView code-behind with every dependency property + method stubs**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. This is the complete contract surface; private fields reference the two named editors from the XAML (Step 4):\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Controls;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Read-only AvalonEdit-based diff renderer. SideBySide uses two editors with\n  /// filler/imaginary lines and mirrored scroll; Unified uses a single editor.\n  /// Backbone contract: 7 dependency properties + GoToNextChange / GoToPreviousChange\n  /// / ShowFind / CopySelection.\n  /// </summary>\n  public partial class DiffView : UserControl\n  {\n      public DiffView()\n      {\n          InitializeComponent();\n      }\n\n      #region FileDiff\n      public static readonly DependencyProperty FileDiffProperty =\n          DependencyProperty.Register(\n              nameof(FileDiff), typeof(FileDiff), typeof(DiffView),\n              new PropertyMetadata(null, OnRenderInputChanged));\n\n      public FileDiff?
