This builder is **pure C# with no WPF dependency**, so it IS unit-testable — follow TDD here. It produces, for each compare mode, the document text plus a per-document-line classification array, including filler lines for side-by-side alignment.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Create the row-kind enum and document model record**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffRowKind.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>Per-display-line classification used by renderers/margin/colorizer.</summary>\n  public enum DiffRowKind\n  {\n      Context,\n      Added,\n      Deleted,\n      Modified,\n      /// <summary>Imaginary/filler row that exists only to keep the two split sides aligned.</summary>\n      Filler,\n  }\n  ```\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentModel.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>One display line in a built diff document.</summary>\n  public sealed record DiffRow(\n      DiffRowKind Kind,\n      string Text,\n      int? OldLineNumber,\n      int? NewLineNumber,\n      IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> IntraSpans);\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// A fully built side of a diff document: the joined text (one <see cref="DiffRow"/>\n  /// per line) plus the indexed per-line classification. Document line numbers are 1-based;\n  /// Rows[0] corresponds to AvalonEdit line 1.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed record DiffDocumentSide(string Text, IReadOnlyList<DiffRow> Rows);\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Result of building a document for a compare mode. For Unified, only\n  /// <see cref="Unified"/> is populated; for SideBySide, <see cref="Left"/> and\n  /// <see cref="Right"/> are populated and are guaranteed equal in row count.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed record DiffDocumentModel(\n      DiffDocumentSide? Unified,\n      DiffDocumentSide? Left,\n      DiffDocumentSide? Right);\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Write the failing test for the builder**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/DiffDocumentBuilderTests.cs`. These exercise filler-line alignment (the core correctness concern) and unified inlining:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n  using Shouldly;\n  using Xunit;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.Controls;\n\n  public sealed class DiffDocumentBuilderTests\n  {\n      private static FileDiff MakeDiff(params DiffLine[] lines)\n      {\n          var hunk = new DiffHunk(1, 0, 1, 0, "@@ -1 +1 @@", lines);\n          var file = new ChangedFile("a.cs", null, ChangeKind.Modified, 1, 1, false);\n          return new FileDiff(file, new[] { hunk }, IsBinary: false, IsTruncated: false);\n      }\n\n      private static DiffLine Ctx(string t, int oldN, int newN) =>\n          new(DiffLineKind.Context, oldN, newN, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());\n\n      private static DiffLine Del(string t, int oldN) =>\n          new(DiffLineKind.Deleted, oldN, null, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());\n\n      private static DiffLine Add(string t, int newN) =>\n          new(DiffLineKind.Added, null, newN, t, Array.Empty<IntraSpan>());\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void SideBySide_aligns_unequal_runs_with_filler_rows()\n      {\n          // one deletion, two additions => right side gets the extra add,\n          // left side gets a filler to stay aligned.\n          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(\n              Ctx("ctx", 1, 1),\n              Del("gone", 2),\n              Add("new1", 2),\n              Add("new2", 3));\n\n          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);\n\n          model.Left.ShouldNotBeNull();\n          model.Right.ShouldNotBeNull();\n          model.Left!.Rows.Count.ShouldBe(model.Right!.Rows.Count);\n\n          // Row 0 = context on both sides.\n          model.Left.Rows[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Context);\n          model.Right.Rows[0].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Context);\n\n          // Row 1: left deleted "gone", right modified "new1".\n          model.Left.Rows[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Deleted);\n          model.Left.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("gone");\n          model.Right.Rows[1].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Modified);\n          model.Right.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("new1");\n\n          // Row 2: left filler, right added "new2".\n          model.Left.Rows[2].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Filler);\n          model.Left.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe(string.Empty);\n          model.Right.Rows[2].Kind.ShouldBe(DiffRowKind.Added);\n          model.Right.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe("new2");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void SideBySide_text_has_one_line_per_row()\n      {\n          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(Ctx("a", 1, 1), Del("b", 2), Add("c", 2));\n          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);\n\n          model.Left!.Text.Split('\n').Length.ShouldBe(model.Left.Rows.Count);\n          model.Right!.Text.Split('\n').Length.ShouldBe(model.Right.Rows.Count);\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Unified_inlines_deletes_then_adds_in_order()\n      {\n          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(Ctx("a", 1, 1), Del("b", 2), Add("c", 2));\n          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.Unified);\n\n          model.Unified.ShouldNotBeNull();\n          model.Left.ShouldBeNull();\n          model.Right.ShouldBeNull();\n\n          model.Unified!.Rows.Select(r => r.Kind).ShouldBe(new[]\n          {\n              DiffRowKind.Context, DiffRowKind.Deleted, DiffRowKind.Added,\n          });\n          model.Unified.Rows[1].Text.ShouldBe("b");\n          model.Unified.Rows[2].Text.ShouldBe("c");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Modified_pair_keeps_intra_spans_on_both_sides()\n      {\n          var delSpans = new[] { new IntraSpan(0, 4, IntraSpanKind.Deleted) };\n          var addSpans = new[] { new IntraSpan(0, 3, IntraSpanKind.Added) };\n          FileDiff diff = MakeDiff(\n              new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Deleted, 1, null, "gone", delSpans),\n              new DiffLine(DiffLineKind.Added, null, 1, "new", addSpans));\n\n          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide);\n\n          model.Left!.Rows[0].IntraSpans.ShouldBe(delSpans);\n          model.Right!.Rows[0].IntraSpans.ShouldBe(addSpans);\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2 (run): Run the test and watch it fail to compile**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffDocumentBuilderTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: **build error** — `DiffDocumentBuilder` does not exist yet (`CS0103`/`The name 'DiffDocumentBuilder' does not exist`). This is the expected red state.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Implement the builder**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentBuilder.cs`. The alignment rule mirrors spec §8: within a hunk, consecutive deleted lines pair 1:1 with the following added lines (those pairs render as `Modified`); leftover deletes/adds get filler on the opposite side.\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Text;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Builds the display document(s) and per-line classification once from a FileDiff\n  /// (spec §8 indexed lookup). Pure C#, no WPF — unit-tested.\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class DiffDocumentBuilder\n  {\n      private static readonly IReadOnlyList<IntraSpan> NoSpans = Array.Empty<IntraSpan>();\n\n      public static DiffDocumentModel Build(FileDiff diff, DiffViewMode mode) =>\n          mode == DiffViewMode.Unified ? BuildUnified(diff) : BuildSideBySide(diff);\n\n      private static DiffDocumentModel BuildUnified(FileDiff diff)\n      {\n          var rows = new List<DiffRow>();\n          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)\n          {\n              foreach (DiffLine line in hunk.Lines)\n              {\n                  DiffRowKind kind = line.Kind switch\n                  {\n                      DiffLineKind.Added => DiffRowKind.Added,\n                      DiffLineKind.Deleted => DiffRowKind.Deleted,\n                      _ => DiffRowKind.Context,\n                  };\n                  rows.Add(new DiffRow(kind, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));\n              }\n          }\n\n          return new DiffDocumentModel(ToSide(rows), Left: null, Right: null);\n      }\n\n      private static DiffDocumentModel BuildSideBySide(FileDiff diff)\n      {\n          var left = new List<DiffRow>();\n          var right = new List<DiffRow>();\n\n          foreach (DiffHunk hunk in diff.Hunks)\n          {\n              // Group consecutive deleted/added runs so we can pair them 1:1.\n              int i = 0;\n              IReadOnlyList<DiffLine> lines = hunk.Lines;\n              while (i < lines.Count)\n              {\n                  DiffLine line = lines[i];\n                  if (line.Kind == DiffLineKind.Context)\n                  {\n                      left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Context, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));\n                      right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Context, line.Text, line.OldLineNumber, line.NewLineNumber, line.IntraSpans));\n                      i++;\n                      continue;\n                  }\n\n                  int delStart = i;\n                  while (i < lines.Count && lines[i].Kind == DiffLineKind.Deleted)\n                  {\n                      i++;\n                  }\n\n                  int addStart = i;\n                  while (i < lines.Count && lines[i].Kind == DiffLineKind.Added)\n                  {\n                      i++;\n                  }\n\n                  EmitRun(lines, delStart, addStart, i, left, right);\n              }\n          }\n\n          PadToEqual(left, right);\n          return new DiffDocumentModel(Unified: null, ToSide(left), ToSide(right));\n      }\n\n      private static void EmitRun(\n          IReadOnlyList<DiffLine> lines, int delStart, int addStart, int end,\n          List<DiffRow> left, List<DiffRow> right)\n      {\n          int delCount = addStart - delStart;\n          int addCount = end - addStart;\n          int pairs = Math.Min(delCount, addCount);\n\n          // Paired lines => Modified on both sides (intra-spans carry through).\n          for (int p = 0; p < pairs; p++)\n          {\n              DiffLine d = lines[delStart + p];\n              DiffLine a = lines[addStart + p];\n              left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Modified, d.Text, d.OldLineNumber, null, d.IntraSpans));\n              right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Modified, a.Text, null, a.NewLineNumber, a.IntraSpans));\n          }\n\n          // Leftover deletions: left=Deleted, right=Filler.\n          for (int p = pairs; p < delCount; p++)\n          {\n              DiffLine d = lines[delStart + p];\n              left.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Deleted, d.Text, d.OldLineNumber, null, NoSpans));\n              right.Add(Filler());\n          }\n\n          // Leftover additions: left=Filler, right=Added.\n          for (int p = pairs; p < addCount; p++)\n          {\n              DiffLine a = lines[addStart + p];\n              left.Add(Filler());\n              right.Add(new DiffRow(DiffRowKind.Added, a.Text, null, a.NewLineNumber, NoSpans));\n          }\n      }\n\n      private static DiffRow Filler() =>\n          new(DiffRowKind.Filler, string.Empty, null, null, NoSpans);\n\n      private static void PadToEqual(List<DiffRow> left, List<DiffRow> right)\n      {\n          while (left.Count < right.Count)\n          {\n              left.Add(Filler());\n          }\n\n          while (right.Count < left.Count)\n          {\n              right.Add(Filler());\n          }\n      }\n\n      private static DiffDocumentSide ToSide(IReadOnlyList<DiffRow> rows)\n      {\n          var sb = new StringBuilder();\n          for (int r = 0; r < rows.Count; r++)\n          {\n              if (r > 0)\n              {\n                  sb.Append('\n');\n              }\n\n              sb.Append(rows[r].Text);\n          }\n\n          return new DiffDocumentSide(sb.ToString(), rows);\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests — expect green**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~DiffDocumentBuilderTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed! - Failed: 0, Passed: 4`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffRowKind.cs src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentModel.cs src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffDocumentBuilder.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/DiffDocumentBuilderTests.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): build indexed diff document + per-line classification\n\n  DiffDocumentBuilder turns a Core FileDiff into per-mode display documents:\n  unified inlines delete-then-add; side-by-side pairs runs 1:1 as Modified and\n  emits filler rows so the two sides stay aligned. Intra-spans carry through.\n  Pure C#, fully unit-tested.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.4: Diff brush palette bound to WPF-UI DynamicResource keys\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffBrushes.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`\n\nThe renderers need semi-transparent add/delete/modify backgrounds, solid intra-span tints, and change-bar colors that read correctly over the Mica backdrop and adapt to theme (spec §8: "semi-transparent diff backgrounds so Mica/selection still read"; "editor brushes bound to WPF-UI DynamicResource keys"). We define a resource dictionary of brushes and a tiny C# accessor that resolves them at render time so theme swaps re-color the diff without rebuilding documents.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Create the brush resource dictionary**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml`. Alpha values keep backgrounds translucent so Mica shows through; intra (word) tints are stronger. The keys are referenced by name from `DiffBrushes.cs`:\n\n  ```xml\n  <ResourceDictionary\n      xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"\n      xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml">\n\n      <!-- Full-line backgrounds (semi-transparent so Mica/selection read through) -->\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedLineBrush"    Color="#3322C55E" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedLineBrush"  Color="#33EF4444" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffModifiedLineBrush" Color="#33F59E0B" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffFillerLineBrush"   Color="#14808080" />\n\n      <!-- Intra-line (word-level) tints, layered over the line background -->\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedSpanBrush"   Color="#5522C55E" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedSpanBrush" Color="#55EF4444" />\n\n      <!-- Change-bar margin colors (solid) -->\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffAddedBarBrush"    Color="#FF22C55E" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffDeletedBarBrush"  Color="#FFEF4444" />\n      <SolidColorBrush x:Key="DiffModifiedBarBrush" Color="#FFF59E0B" />\n  </ResourceDictionary>\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Merge the dictionary into App resources**\n\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml` and add the dictionary to the existing `<ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>` (it already merges the WPF-UI theme/control dictionaries — add ours after them so our keys win):\n\n  ```xml\n  <ResourceDictionary Source="pack://application:,,,/GitDelta.UI;component/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml" />\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Create a C# accessor that resolves brushes by key at render time**\n\n  Renderers run on the UI thread and need `System.Windows.Media.Brush` instances; resolving from `Application.Current.Resources` each render keeps theme swaps live. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffBrushes.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Media;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Resolves diff render brushes from merged application resources by key.\n  /// Resolving live (not caching) lets theme swaps recolor the diff (spec §8).\n  /// Falls back to hard-coded brushes if a key is missing (e.g. design-time).\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class DiffBrushes\n  {\n      public static Brush AddedLine => Resolve("DiffAddedLineBrush", 0x33, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);\n      public static Brush DeletedLine => Resolve("DiffDeletedLineBrush", 0x33, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);\n      public static Brush ModifiedLine => Resolve("DiffModifiedLineBrush", 0x33, 0xF5, 0x9E, 0x0B);\n      public static Brush FillerLine => Resolve("DiffFillerLineBrush", 0x14, 0x80, 0x80, 0x80);\n\n      public static Brush AddedSpan => Resolve("DiffAddedSpanBrush", 0x55, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);\n      public static Brush DeletedSpan => Resolve("DiffDeletedSpanBrush", 0x55, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);\n\n      public static Brush AddedBar => Resolve("DiffAddedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0x22, 0xC5, 0x5E);\n      public static Brush DeletedBar => Resolve("DiffDeletedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0xEF, 0x44, 0x44);\n      public static Brush ModifiedBar => Resolve("DiffModifiedBarBrush", 0xFF, 0xF5, 0x9E, 0x0B);\n\n      private static Brush Resolve(string key, byte a, byte r, byte g, byte b)\n      {\n          if (Application.Current?.TryFindResource(key) is Brush brush)\n          {\n              return brush;\n          }\n\n          var fallback = new SolidColorBrush(Color.FromArgb(a, r, g, b));\n          fallback.Freeze();\n          return fallback;\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. (Pack URI typos surface here as XAML parse / `IOException` at build of the baml — if it builds clean the dictionary path is correct.)\n\n- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffBrushes.cs src/GitDelta.UI/Resources/DiffBrushes.xaml src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add theme-aware diff brush palette\n\n  Semi-transparent line backgrounds (Mica reads through), solid intra-span\n  tints, and change-bar colors as a merged ResourceDictionary plus a live\n  resolver so theme swaps recolor the diff without rebuilding documents.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.5: Full-line background renderer (IBackgroundRenderer)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffLineBackgroundRenderer.cs`\n\nPer spec §8 / BACKBONE: a custom `IBackgroundRenderer` paints full-line add/delete/modify (and filler) backgrounds using `BackgroundGeometryBuilder`. It reads its classification from the `DiffDocumentSide.Rows` array (built in 7.3), indexing by AvalonEdit document line number. This is pure rendering — **manual verification only**.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the background renderer**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffLineBackgroundRenderer.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Media;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Paints full-line add/delete/modify/filler backgrounds behind the text,\n  /// driven by the precomputed per-line classification. Operates only on visible\n  /// lines (AvalonEdit virtualization).\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class DiffLineBackgroundRenderer : IBackgroundRenderer\n  {\n      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;\n\n      public KnownLayer Layer => KnownLayer.Background;\n\n      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)\n      {\n          _side = side;\n      }\n\n      public void Draw(TextView textView, DrawingContext drawingContext)\n      {\n          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;\n          if (side is null || textView.VisualLinesValid == false)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          textView.EnsureVisualLines();\n\n          foreach (VisualLine vl in textView.VisualLines)\n          {\n              int docLine = vl.FirstDocumentLine.LineNumber; // 1-based\n              int rowIndex = docLine - 1;\n              if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              Brush? brush = side.Rows[rowIndex].Kind switch\n              {\n                  DiffRowKind.Added => DiffBrushes.AddedLine,\n                  DiffRowKind.Deleted => DiffBrushes.DeletedLine,\n                  DiffRowKind.Modified => DiffBrushes.ModifiedLine,\n                  DiffRowKind.Filler => DiffBrushes.FillerLine,\n                  _ => null,\n              };\n\n              if (brush is null)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              var geoBuilder = new BackgroundGeometryBuilder\n              {\n                  AlignToWholePixels = true,\n                  CornerRadius = 0,\n              };\n\n              foreach (Rect rect in BackgroundGeometryBuilder.GetRectsForSegment(\n                  textView, vl.FirstDocumentLine, extendToFullWidthAtLineEnd: true))\n              {\n                  var full = new Rect(0, rect.Top, textView.ActualWidth, rect.Height);\n                  geoBuilder.AddRectangle(textView, new RectSegment(full));\n              }\n\n              Geometry geometry = geoBuilder.CreateGeometry();\n              if (geometry is not null)\n              {\n                  drawingContext.DrawGeometry(brush, null, geometry);\n              }\n          }\n      }\n\n      /// <summary>Adapts a raw Rect to the ISegment-on-textview API of the geometry builder.</summary>\n      private sealed class RectSegment : ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.ISegment\n      {\n          private readonly Rect _rect;\n          public RectSegment(Rect rect) => _rect = rect;\n\n          // Not used for pixel-rect geometry, but required by the interface.\n          public int Offset => 0;\n          public int Length => 0;\n          public int EndOffset => 0;\n\n          public Rect Rect => _rect;\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > Implementation note: AvalonEdit's `BackgroundGeometryBuilder.AddRectangle(TextView, ISegment)` resolves segment offsets to rectangles internally; for full-width line fills the simplest robust approach is `AddRectangle(double x, double y, double width, double height)` from the per-line `Rect`. If your AvalonEdit build exposes `geoBuilder.AddRectangle(full.Left, full.Top, full.Width, full.Height)` directly, prefer that overload and delete the `RectSegment` helper. Verify which overload exists in 6.3.1.120 during Step 2.\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Reconcile the geometry API against AvalonEdit 6.3.1.120 and simplify**\n\n  Open the AvalonEdit assembly metadata to confirm the available overload, then prefer the direct-rect overload. Replace the inner `foreach`/`RectSegment` block in `Draw` with the simpler, definitely-present overload:\n\n  ```csharp\n              var geoBuilder = new BackgroundGeometryBuilder { AlignToWholePixels = true };\n              foreach (Rect rect in BackgroundGeometryBuilder.GetRectsForSegment(\n                  textView, vl.FirstDocumentLine, extendToFullWidthAtLineEnd: true))\n              {\n                  geoBuilder.AddRectangle(\n                      textView,\n                      new ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.TextSegment\n                      {\n                          StartOffset = vl.FirstDocumentLine.Offset,\n                          Length = vl.FirstDocumentLine.Length,\n                      });\n                  break; // one segment per line is enough; full-width handled below\n              }\n\n              Geometry? geometry = geoBuilder.CreateGeometry();\n              if (geometry is not null)\n              {\n                  drawingContext.DrawGeometry(brush, null, geometry);\n              }\n  ```\n\n  Then delete the `RectSegment` nested class. This uses only public, version-stable APIs (`GetRectsForSegment`, `AddRectangle(TextView, ISegment)`, `TextSegment`). Build to confirm the API resolves:\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/DiffLineBackgroundRenderer.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add full-line diff background renderer\n\n  IBackgroundRenderer that paints add/delete/modify/filler line backgrounds\n  via BackgroundGeometryBuilder over visible lines only, driven by the\n  precomputed per-line classification.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.6: Change-bar margin + intra-line colorizing transformer\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/ChangeBarMargin.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/IntraLineColorizer.cs`\n\nTwo more per-line render components: a thin **change-bar margin** drawing the green/red/orange gutter stripe (BACKBONE / spec §8), and a `DocumentColorizingTransformer` that applies the intra-span tints from the model. The colorizer is added to the editor's `LineTransformers` *after* the syntax transformer (Phase 8), so its background tint layers on top of syntax foreground colors. Manual verification only.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the change-bar margin**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/ChangeBarMargin.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Windows;\n  using System.Windows.Media;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Editing;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// A narrow gutter margin that draws a solid change-bar (green/red/orange)\n  /// for each added/deleted/modified line, driven by the per-line classification.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class ChangeBarMargin : AbstractMargin\n  {\n      private const double BarWidth = 4.0;\n      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;\n\n      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)\n      {\n          _side = side;\n          InvalidateVisual();\n      }\n\n      protected override Size MeasureOverride(Size availableSize) => new(BarWidth, 0);\n\n      protected override void OnRender(DrawingContext drawingContext)\n      {\n          base.OnRender(drawingContext);\n\n          TextView? textView = TextView;\n          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;\n          if (textView is null || side is null || textView.VisualLinesValid == false)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          foreach (VisualLine vl in textView.VisualLines)\n          {\n              int rowIndex = vl.FirstDocumentLine.LineNumber - 1;\n              if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              Brush? brush = side.Rows[rowIndex].Kind switch\n              {\n                  DiffRowKind.Added => DiffBrushes.AddedBar,\n                  DiffRowKind.Deleted => DiffBrushes.DeletedBar,\n                  DiffRowKind.Modified => DiffBrushes.ModifiedBar,\n                  _ => null,\n              };\n\n              if (brush is null)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              double top = vl.VisualTop - textView.VerticalOffset;\n              double height = vl.Height;\n              drawingContext.DrawRectangle(brush, null, new Rect(0, top, BarWidth, height));\n          }\n      }\n\n      protected override void OnTextViewChanged(TextView oldTextView, TextView newTextView)\n      {\n          if (oldTextView is not null)\n          {\n              oldTextView.VisualLinesChanged -= OnVisualLinesChanged;\n          }\n\n          base.OnTextViewChanged(oldTextView, newTextView);\n\n          if (newTextView is not null)\n          {\n              newTextView.VisualLinesChanged += OnVisualLinesChanged;\n          }\n\n          InvalidateVisual();\n      }\n\n      private void OnVisualLinesChanged(object? sender, EventArgs e) => InvalidateVisual();\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the intra-line colorizer**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/IntraLineColorizer.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;\n  using GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Applies intra-line (word-level) background tints from IntraSpan ranges.\n  /// Added after the syntax transformer so its background layers over syntax\n  /// foreground colors (spec §8). Per-visible-line via AvalonEdit virtualization.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class IntraLineColorizer : DocumentColorizingTransformer\n  {\n      private DiffDocumentSide? _side;\n\n      public void SetSide(DiffDocumentSide? side)\n      {\n          _side = side;\n      }\n\n      protected override void ColorizeLine(ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document.DocumentLine line)\n      {\n          DiffDocumentSide? side = _side;\n          if (side is null)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          int rowIndex = line.LineNumber - 1;\n          if (rowIndex < 0 || rowIndex >= side.Rows.Count)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          DiffRow row = side.Rows[rowIndex];\n          if (row.IntraSpans.Count == 0)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          int lineStart = line.Offset;\n          int lineLength = line.Length;\n\n          foreach (IntraSpan span in row.IntraSpans)\n          {\n              int spanStart = span.Start;\n              int spanEnd = span.Start + span.Length;\n\n              // Clamp to the actual line bounds (defensive against off-by-one in source data).\n              if (spanStart < 0)\n              {\n                  spanStart = 0;\n              }\n\n              if (spanEnd > lineLength)\n              {\n                  spanEnd = lineLength;\n              }\n\n              if (spanEnd <= spanStart)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              System.Windows.Media.Brush tint = span.Kind == IntraSpanKind.Added\n                  ? DiffBrushes.AddedSpan\n                  : DiffBrushes.DeletedSpan;\n\n              ChangeLinePart(\n                  lineStart + spanStart,\n                  lineStart + spanEnd,\n                  element => element.TextRunProperties.SetBackgroundBrush(tint));\n          }\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/ChangeBarMargin.cs src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/IntraLineColorizer.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add change-bar margin and intra-line colorizer\n\n  ChangeBarMargin draws the green/red/orange gutter stripe per line.\n  IntraLineColorizer applies word-level IntraSpan tints via a\n  DocumentColorizingTransformer, layered over syntax foreground colors.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.7: Wire renderers into DiffView; read-only editor setup; binary/truncated fallbacks; display options\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`\n\nNow connect the pieces from 7.3–7.6 into the control: configure each editor read-only with undo disabled, attach the background renderer / change-bar margin / intra-line colorizer per editor, build documents on `FileDiff`/`ViewMode` change, toggle split vs unified visibility, apply binary/truncated overlays, and honor `ShowWhitespace`/`WordWrap`/`TabSize`. Manual verification.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Add per-editor render attachment helper + fields**\n\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. Add these usings at the top:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Editing;\n  ```\n\n  Add private renderer fields and a configuration method inside the class (replace the placeholder `LeftEditorRef`/`RightEditorRef`/`UnifiedEditorRef` properties from Task 7.2 — they are no longer needed):\n\n  ```csharp\n      // One renderer/margin/colorizer per editor surface.\n      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _leftBg = new();\n      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _rightBg = new();\n      private readonly DiffLineBackgroundRenderer _unifiedBg = new();\n\n      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _leftBar = new();\n      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _rightBar = new();\n      private readonly ChangeBarMargin _unifiedBar = new();\n\n      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _leftIntra = new();\n      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _rightIntra = new();\n      private readonly IntraLineColorizer _unifiedIntra = new();\n\n      private bool _editorsConfigured;\n\n      private void ConfigureEditorsOnce()\n      {\n          if (_editorsConfigured)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          ConfigureEditor(LeftEditor, _leftBg, _leftBar, _leftIntra);\n          ConfigureEditor(RightEditor, _rightBg, _rightBar, _rightIntra);\n          ConfigureEditor(UnifiedEditor, _unifiedBg, _unifiedBar, _unifiedIntra);\n          _editorsConfigured = true;\n      }\n\n      private void ConfigureEditor(\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor,\n          DiffLineBackgroundRenderer bg,\n          ChangeBarMargin bar,\n          IntraLineColorizer intra)\n      {\n          // Read-only, no undo/edit subsystem cost (spec §8).\n          editor.IsReadOnly = true;\n          editor.Document = new TextDocument();\n          editor.Document.UndoStack.SizeLimit = 0;\n          editor.Options.EnableHyperlinks = false;\n          editor.Options.EnableEmailHyperlinks = false;\n          editor.Options.AllowScrollBelowDocument = false;\n\n          editor.TextArea.TextView.BackgroundRenderers.Add(bg);\n          editor.TextArea.LeftMargins.Insert(0, bar);\n          editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers.Add(intra); // intra last for now; syntax inserts before it in Phase 8\n      }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the render pipeline (document build + mode toggle + fallbacks)**\n\n  Add the rendering methods and replace the empty `OnRenderInputChanged` / `OnDisplayOptionChanged` callbacks:\n\n  ```csharp\n      private static void OnRenderInputChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)\n      {\n          ((DiffView)d).Rebuild();\n      }\n\n      private static void OnDisplayOptionChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)\n      {\n          ((DiffView)d).ApplyDisplayOptions();\n      }\n\n      private void Rebuild()\n      {\n          ConfigureEditorsOnce();\n          FileDiff? diff = FileDiff;\n\n          if (diff is null)\n          {\n              ShowOverlay(EmptyState, null);\n              return;\n          }\n\n          if (diff.IsBinary)\n          {\n              ShowOverlay(PlaceholderState, "Binary file — no textual diff");\n              return;\n          }\n\n          // Real content: hide overlays, build documents.\n          EmptyState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n          PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n\n          DiffDocumentModel model = DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(diff, ViewMode);\n\n          if (ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified)\n          {\n              SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n              UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;\n              LoadSide(UnifiedEditor, _unifiedBg, _unifiedBar, _unifiedIntra, model.Unified);\n          }\n          else\n          {\n              UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n              SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;\n              LoadSide(LeftEditor, _leftBg, _leftBar, _leftIntra, model.Left);\n              LoadSide(RightEditor, _rightBg, _rightBar, _rightIntra, model.Right);\n          }\n\n          ApplyDisplayOptions();\n\n          if (diff.IsTruncated)\n          {\n              // Show overlay text but keep the (partial) diff visible behind it as a banner.\n              PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;\n              PlaceholderState.VerticalAlignment = VerticalAlignment.Bottom;\n              PlaceholderState.Text = "Diff truncated — file too large to show in full";\n          }\n      }\n\n      private void LoadSide(\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor,\n          DiffLineBackgroundRenderer bg,\n          ChangeBarMargin bar,\n          IntraLineColorizer intra,\n          DiffDocumentSide? side)\n      {\n          editor.Document.Text = side?.Text ?? string.Empty;\n          bg.SetSide(side);\n          bar.SetSide(side);\n          intra.SetSide(side);\n          editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();\n      }\n\n      private void ShowOverlay(System.Windows.Controls.TextBlock overlay, string? text)\n      {\n          SplitRoot.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n          UnifiedEditor.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n          EmptyState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n          PlaceholderState.Visibility = Visibility.Collapsed;\n\n          overlay.VerticalAlignment = VerticalAlignment.Center;\n          if (text is not null)\n          {\n              overlay.Text = text;\n          }\n\n          overlay.Visibility = Visibility.Visible;\n      }\n\n      private void ApplyDisplayOptions()\n      {\n          ConfigureEditorsOnce();\n          bool wrap = WordWrap && ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified; // word-wrap disabled in split (spec §8)\n          foreach (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor in new[] { LeftEditor, RightEditor, UnifiedEditor })\n          {\n              editor.WordWrap = wrap;\n              editor.Options.ShowSpaces = ShowWhitespace;\n              editor.Options.ShowTabs = ShowWhitespace;\n              editor.Options.IndentationSize = TabSize < 1 ? 4 : TabSize;\n          }\n      }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Manual verification — temporary harness Manual verification.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Add the guarded scroll-sync wiring**\n\n  In `ConfigureEditorsOnce` (Task 7.7), after the three `ConfigureEditor` calls, hook the two split editors' scroll events. Add a guard field and the handlers to `DiffView.xaml.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n      private bool _syncingScroll;\n\n      private void HookSplitScrollSync()\n      {\n          LeftEditor.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffsetChanged += (_, _) =>\n              MirrorScroll(LeftEditor, RightEditor);\n          RightEditor.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffsetChanged += (_, _) =>\n              MirrorScroll(RightEditor, LeftEditor);\n      }\n\n      private void MirrorScroll(\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor source,\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor target)\n      {\n          if (_syncingScroll || ViewMode != DiffViewMode.SideBySide)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          _syncingScroll = true;\n          try\n          {\n              System.Windows.Vector offset = source.TextArea.TextView.ScrollOffset;\n              target.ScrollToVerticalOffset(offset.Y);\n              target.ScrollToHorizontalOffset(offset.X);\n          }\n          finally\n          {\n              _syncingScroll = false;\n          }\n      }\n  ```\n\n  Then add the hook call at the end of `ConfigureEditorsOnce`:\n\n  ```csharp\n          HookSplitScrollSync();\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Manual verification**\n\n  Re-add the temporary harness from Task 7.7 Step 4 but feed a larger `FileDiff` (duplicate the hunk lines ~60 times so the document overflows the viewport). Run:\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet run --project src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  **Observe:** scrolling the left editor (wheel or scrollbar) moves the right editor in lockstep, and vice versa, both vertically and horizontally. There is no visible jitter/oscillation (the re-entrancy guard prevents the feedback loop). Remove the harness afterward.\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): mirror side-by-side scroll with re-entrancy guard\n\n  Hooks both split editors ScrollOffsetChanged, mirroring vertical and\n  horizontal offsets; a _syncingScroll flag prevents the feedback loop.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 7.9: Next/prev change navigation + find panel + copy\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`\n\nImplement the four BACKBONE public methods for real: `GoToNextChange`/`GoToPreviousChange` jump the caret/scroll to the next changed (non-context, non-filler) row in the active editor; `ShowFind` opens AvalonEdit's built-in `SearchPanel`; `CopySelection` copies the active editor's selection. Manual verification.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Add a helper for the active editor and its side, plus install the search panel**\n\n  In `ConfigureEditor` (Task 7.7), install the search panel per editor. Add to the end of `ConfigureEditor`:\n\n  ```csharp\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(editor.TextArea);\n  ```\n\n  Add this active-editor resolver to `DiffView.xaml.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n      private ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor ActiveEditor =>\n          ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified ? UnifiedEditor : RightEditor;\n\n      private DiffDocumentSide? ActiveSide =>\n          ViewMode == DiffViewMode.Unified\n              ? (FileDiff is null ? null : DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(FileDiff, DiffViewMode.Unified).Unified)\n              : (FileDiff is null ? null : DiffDocumentBuilder.Build(FileDiff, DiffViewMode.SideBySide).Right);\n  ```\n\n  > Note: rebuilding here is cheap (the model is small and already cached conceptually); if profiling shows cost, store the last `DiffDocumentModel` from `Rebuild`. For correctness this is sufficient.\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the four public methods (replace the Task 7.2 stubs)**\n\n  ```csharp\n      public void GoToNextChange()\n      {\n          NavigateChange(forward: true);\n      }\n\n      public void GoToPreviousChange()\n      {\n          NavigateChange(forward: false);\n      }\n\n      public void ShowFind()\n      {\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(ActiveEditor.TextArea);\n          ActiveEditor.Focus();\n          // Opens the find panel; AvalonEdit binds Ctrl+F, but we surface it programmatically too.\n          ActiveEditor.TextArea.DefaultInputHandler.NestedInputHandlers\n              .OfType<ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchInputHandler>()\n              .FirstOrDefault()?\n              .CommandBindings\n              .OfType<System.Windows.Input.CommandBinding>()\n              .FirstOrDefault(b => b.Command == ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find);\n          // Simpler reliable path: route the Find routed command at the editor.\n          if (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.CanExecute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea))\n          {\n              ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea);\n          }\n      }\n\n      public void CopySelection()\n      {\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor = ActiveEditor;\n          if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(editor.SelectedText))\n          {\n              editor.Copy();\n          }\n      }\n\n      private void NavigateChange(bool forward)\n      {\n          DiffDocumentSide? side = ActiveSide;\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor = ActiveEditor;\n          if (side is null || side.Rows.Count == 0)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          int currentRow = editor.TextArea.Caret.Line - 1; // 0-based row index\n          int count = side.Rows.Count;\n          int step = forward ? 1 : -1;\n\n          for (int n = 1; n <= count; n++)\n          {\n              int idx = currentRow + (step * n);\n              if (idx < 0 || idx >= count)\n              {\n                  break;\n              }\n\n              DiffRowKind kind = side.Rows[idx].Kind;\n              if (kind is DiffRowKind.Added or DiffRowKind.Deleted or DiffRowKind.Modified)\n              {\n                  int docLine = idx + 1;\n                  editor.ScrollToLine(docLine);\n                  editor.TextArea.Caret.Line = docLine;\n                  editor.TextArea.Caret.Column = 1;\n                  editor.TextArea.Caret.BringCaretToView();\n                  return;\n              }\n          }\n      }\n  ```\n\n  > Note: `ShowFind`'s dead reflective lookup above is illustrative of the wrong path — keep ONLY the reliable `ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute` block. Delete the `NestedInputHandlers` lines so the method body is just: `SearchPanel.Install`, `Focus`, and the `Find.Execute` guard.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Clean up ShowFind to the reliable form**\n\n  Replace `ShowFind` with the final, minimal version:\n\n  ```csharp\n      public void ShowFind()\n      {\n          ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.SearchPanel.Install(ActiveEditor.TextArea);\n          ActiveEditor.Focus();\n          if (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.CanExecute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea))\n          {\n              ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Search.ApplicationCommands.Find.Execute(null, ActiveEditor.TextArea);\n          }\n      }\n  ```\n\n  Add the needed using at the top of the file:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Linq;\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 5: Manual verification**\n\n  Re-add the larger harness (Task 7.8). The language-id map and the guard are **pure logic — unit-tested (TDD)**; the tokenizing transformer and theme wiring are **rendering — manual verification**.\n\n### Task 8.1: TextMateSharp packages + language-id-from-extension map (TDD)\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/Directory.Packages.props`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/LanguageIdMap.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/LanguageIdMapTests.cs`\n\n`SyntaxLanguageId` is a TextMate language id (e.g. `csharp`, `typescript`). namespace GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.Controls;\n\n  public sealed class LanguageIdMapTests\n  {\n      [Theory]\n      [InlineData("Program.cs", "csharp")]\n      [InlineData("app.ts", "typescript")]\n      [InlineData("index.tsx", "typescriptreact")]\n      [InlineData("main.js", "javascript")]\n      [InlineData("data.json", "json")]\n      [InlineData("README.md", "markdown")]\n      [InlineData("style.css", "css")]\n      [InlineData("page.html", "html")]\n      [InlineData("build.ps1", "powershell")]\n      [InlineData("Dockerfile", "dockerfile")]\n      [InlineData("config.yml", "yaml")]\n      [InlineData("config.yaml", "yaml")]\n      public void Resolves_known_extensions(string path, string expected)\n      {\n          LanguageIdMap.FromPath(path).ShouldBe(expected);\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Is_case_insensitive()\n      {\n          LanguageIdMap.FromPath("PROGRAM.CS").ShouldBe("csharp");\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Unknown_extension_returns_null()\n      {\n          LanguageIdMap.FromPath("mystery.xyz").ShouldBeNull();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public System.IO;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Maps a file path to a TextMate language id used to select a grammar.\n  /// Returns null when no known grammar applies (caller skips highlighting).\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class LanguageIdMap\n  {\n      private static readonly IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> ByExtension =\n          new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n          {\n              [".cs"] = "csharp",\n              [".csx"] = "csharp",\n              [".ts"] = "typescript",\n              [".tsx"] = "typescriptreact",\n              [".js"] = "javascript",\n              [".jsx"] = "javascriptreact",\n              [".mjs"] = "javascript",\n              [".cjs"] = "javascript",\n              [".json"] = "json",\n              [".jsonc"] = "json",\n              [".md"] = "markdown",\n              [".markdown"] = "markdown",\n              [".css"] = "css",\n              [".scss"] = "scss",\n              [".less"] = "less",\n              [".html"] = "html",\n              [".htm"] = "html",\n              [".xml"] = "xml",\n              [".xaml"] = "xml",\n              [".ps1"] = "powershell",\n              [".psm1"] = "powershell",\n              [".yml"] = "yaml",\n              [".yaml"] = "yaml",\n              [".py"] = "python",\n              [".go"] = "go",\n              [".rs"] = "rust",\n              [".java"] = "java",\n              [".c"] = "c",\n              [".h"] = "cpp",\n              [".cpp"] = "cpp",\n              [".hpp"] = "cpp",\n              [".sql"] = "sql",\n              [".sh"] = "shellscript",\n              [".bash"] = "shellscript",\n              [".toml"] = "toml",\n              [".ini"] = "ini",\n          };\n\n      private static readonly IReadOnlyDictionary<string, string> ByFileName =\n          new Dictionary<string, string>(StringComparer.OrdinalIgnoreCase)\n          {\n              ["Dockerfile"] = "dockerfile",\n              [".gitignore"] = "ignore",\n              [".gitattributes"] = "ignore",\n          };\n\n      public static string? FromPath(string? path)\n      {\n          if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(path))\n          {\n              return null;\n          }\n\n          string fileName = Path.GetFileName(path);\n          if (ByFileName.TryGetValue(fileName, out string? byName))\n          {\n              return byName;\n          }\n\n          string ext = Path.GetExtension(path);\n          if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(ext) && ByExtension.TryGetValue(ext, out string? byExt))\n          {\n              return byExt;\n          }\n\n          return null;\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Run the tests — expect green**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~LanguageIdMapTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed! - Failed: 0, Passed: 15`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 5: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add Directory.Packages.props src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/LanguageIdMap.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/LanguageIdMapTests.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add TextMateSharp packages and language-id map\n\n  References TextMateSharp + .Grammars. .ShouldBeFalse();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Skips_when_too_many_chars()\n      {\n          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", lineCount: 10, totalChars: SyntaxGuard.MaxChars + 1, isBinary: false)\n              .ShouldBeFalse();\n      }\n\n      [Fact]\n      public void Allows_exactly_at_the_limits()\n      {\n          SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize("csharp", exist (`CS0103`).\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Implement the guard**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/SyntaxGuard.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Decides whether syntax tokenization should run for a document. Large or binary\n  /// content falls back to monochrome (spec §8 performance valve).\n  /// </summary>\n  public static class SyntaxGuard\n  {\n      public const int MaxLines = 20_000;\n      public const int MaxChars = 2_000_000;\n\n      public static bool ShouldTokenize(string? languageId, int lineCount, int totalChars, bool isBinary)\n      {\n          if (isBinary || string.IsNullOrEmpty(languageId))\n          {\n              return false;\n          }\n\n          if (lineCount > MaxLines || totalChars > MaxChars)\n          {\n              return false;\n          }\n\n          return true;\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Run — expect green**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet test tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~SyntaxGuardTests"\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Passed! - Failed: 0, Passed: 6`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/SyntaxGuard.cs tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/Controls/SyntaxGuardTests.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add tokenization size/binary guard\n\n  SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize skips highlighting when there is no language id,\n  the content is binary, or the document exceeds line/char limits (monochrome\n  fallback, spec §8). Fully unit-tested.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ''@\n  ```\n\n### Task 8.3: TextMate registry/theme provider\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateThemeProvider.cs`\n\nA small wrapper around TextMateSharp's `RegistryOptions`/`Registry` that exposes a grammar for a language id and the DarkPlus/LightPlus theme chosen by `IsDarkTheme`, plus a way to map a TextMate theme color (hex string) to a frozen WPF `Brush`. The tokenizing transformer (8.4) consumes this. Manual/build verification (it touches the TextMateSharp object model, not rendering).\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the provider**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateThemeProvider.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using System.Collections.Concurrent;\n  using System.Windows.Media;\n  using TextMateSharp.Grammars;\n  using TextMateSharp.Registry;\n  using TextMateSharp.Themes;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Wraps the TextMateSharp Registry: resolves a grammar by language id and the\n  /// DarkPlus/LightPlus theme by IsDarkTheme, and converts theme colors to frozen\n  /// WPF brushes (cached). Recreated when the theme changes.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class TextMateThemeProvider\n  {\n      private readonly RegistryOptions _options;\n      private readonly Registry _registry;\n      private readonly Theme _theme;\n      private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<int, Brush> _brushCache = new();\n      private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, Brush> _hexCache = new();\n\n      public TextMateThemeProvider(bool isDark)\n      {\n          IsDark = isDark;\n          _options = new RegistryOptions(isDark ? ThemeName.DarkPlus : ThemeName.LightPlus);\n          _registry = new Registry(_options);\n          _theme = _registry.GetTheme();\n      }\n\n      public bool IsDark { get; }\n\n      public Theme Theme => _theme;\n\n      /// <summary>Returns the grammar scope name for a VS Code language id, or null.</summary>\n      public string? GetScopeName(string languageId) => _options.GetScopeByLanguageId(languageId);\n\n      /// <summary>Loads the grammar for a language id, or null if unavailable.</summary>\n      public TextMateSharp.Grammars.IGrammar? LoadGrammar(string languageId)\n      {\n          string? scope = GetScopeName(languageId);\n          return scope is null ? null : _registry.LoadGrammar(scope);\n      }\n\n      /// <summary>Resolves a TextMate foreground color id to a frozen brush.</summary>\n      public Brush BrushForForeground(int foregroundId)\n      {\n          return _brushCache.GetOrAdd(foregroundId, id =>\n          {\n              string? hex = _theme.GetColor(id);\n              return BrushFromHex(hex);\n          });\n      }\n\n      private Brush BrushFromHex(string? hex)\n      {\n          if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(hex))\n          {\n              return Brushes.Transparent;\n          }\n\n          return _hexCache.GetOrAdd(hex, h =>\n          {\n              try\n              {\n                  var color = (Color)ColorConverter.ConvertFromString(h);\n                  var brush = new SolidColorBrush(color);\n                  brush.Freeze();\n                  return brush;\n              }\n              catch (FormatException)\n              {\n                  return Brushes.Transparent;\n              }\n          });\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > Note: TextMateSharp's exact accessor names can drift across versions (`GetScopeByLanguageId`, `Theme.GetColor(int)`, `IGrammar.TokenizeLine`). If a member name does not resolve in the pinned version, open the package's public surface via the IDE's "Go to Definition" on `RegistryOptions`/`Theme` and adjust the three call sites; the shape (registry → grammar → theme color id → hex) is stable.\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. If any TextMateSharp member fails to resolve, fix per the note above before proceeding.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateThemeProvider.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add TextMate registry/theme provider\n\n  Wraps the TextMateSharp Registry: grammar-by-language-id, DarkPlus/LightPlus\n  theme by IsDarkTheme, and cached frozen-brush conversion of theme colors.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 8.4: TextMate colorizing transformer (the adapter)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateColorizer.cs`\n\nThis is the core hand-written TextMate→AvalonEdit adapter (spec §15 risk). A `DocumentColorizingTransformer` that, per visible line, calls `IGrammar.TokenizeLine`, maps each token's scopes to a theme foreground color, and applies it as the line part's foreground. It carries grammar state line-to-line so multi-line constructs (block comments, strings) tokenize correctly. Manual verification.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Implement the colorizer**\n\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateColorizer.cs`:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Document;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;\n  using TextMateSharp.Grammars;\n\n  namespace GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;\n\n  /// <summary>\n  /// Hand-written TextMate -> AvalonEdit adapter (spec §15). Tokenizes each visible\n  /// line with IGrammar.TokenizeLine, threads grammar state line-to-line, and maps\n  /// each token's scopes to a theme foreground brush. Added to LineTransformers\n  /// BEFORE the intra-line colorizer so diff tints layer over syntax foregrounds.\n  /// </summary>\n  public sealed class TextMateColorizer : DocumentColorizingTransformer\n  {\n      private readonly TextMateThemeProvider _provider;\n      private readonly IGrammar _grammar;\n\n      // Cache of end-state per document line so re-tokenizing a single visible line\n      // can resume from the prior line's state. Index is 1-based line number.\n      private readonly Dictionary<int, IStateStack?> _lineStartState = new();\n\n      public TextMateColorizer(TextMateThemeProvider provider, IGrammar grammar)\n      {\n          _provider = provider;\n          _grammar = grammar;\n          _lineStartState[1] = null; // first line starts from the null state\n      }\n\n      protected override void ColorizeLine(DocumentLine line)\n      {\n          string text = CurrentContext.Document.GetText(line);\n          IStateStack? startState = GetStartState(line);\n\n          ITokenizeLineResult result = _grammar.TokenizeLine(text, startState, TimeSpan.MaxValue);\n\n          // Remember the end state as the next line's start state.\n          _lineStartState[line.LineNumber + 1] = result.RuleStack;\n\n          int lineStart = line.Offset;\n          foreach (IToken token in result.Tokens)\n          {\n              int tokenStart = lineStart + Math.Min(token.StartIndex, text.Length);\n              int tokenEnd = lineStart + Math.Min(token.EndIndex, text.Length);\n              if (tokenEnd <= tokenStart)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              int foreground = ResolveForeground(token.Scopes);\n              if (foreground <= 0)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              System.Windows.Media.Brush brush = _provider.BrushForForeground(foreground);\n              ChangeLinePart(tokenStart, tokenEnd, el => el.TextRunProperties.SetForegroundBrush(brush));\n          }\n      }\n\n      private IStateStack? GetStartState(DocumentLine line)\n      {\n          if (_lineStartState.TryGetValue(line.LineNumber, out IStateStack? state))\n          {\n              return state;\n          }\n\n          // Tokenize all preceding lines once to build the state chain up to this line.\n          IStateStack? running = null;\n          for (int n = 1; n < line.LineNumber; n++)\n          {\n              DocumentLine prior = CurrentContext.Document.GetLineByNumber(n);\n              string priorText = CurrentContext.Document.GetText(prior);\n              ITokenizeLineResult priorResult = _grammar.TokenizeLine(priorText, running, TimeSpan.MaxValue);\n              running = priorResult.RuleStack;\n              _lineStartState[n + 1] = running;\n          }\n\n          return running;\n      }\n\n      private int ResolveForeground(IReadOnlyList<string> scopes)\n      {\n          // Most-specific scope last; ask the theme for its style and take the foreground.\n          for (int i = scopes.Count - 1; i >= 0; i--)\n          {\n              List<TextMateSharp.Themes.ThemeTrieElementRule> rules =\n                  _provider.Theme.Match(new[] { scopes[i] });\n              foreach (TextMateSharp.Themes.ThemeTrieElementRule rule in rules)\n              {\n                  if (rule.foreground > 0)\n                  {\n                      return rule.foreground;\n                  }\n              }\n          }\n\n          return 0;\n      }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  > Note: TextMateSharp member spellings to confirm against the pinned version: `IStateStack` (older versions use `StackElement`), `IGrammar.TokenizeLine(string, IStateStack?, TimeSpan)`, `ITokenizeLineResult.Tokens`/`.RuleStack`, `IToken.StartIndex`/`.EndIndex`/`.Scopes`, and `Theme.Match(...)` returning rules with a `foreground` int. If any name differs, adjust the call site — the algorithm (resume state → tokenize → most-specific scope → theme foreground → brush) is the stable contract.\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. Resolve any TextMateSharp member-name mismatch per the note before continuing.\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Commit**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git add src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/Diff/Syntax/TextMateColorizer.cs\n  git commit -m @'\n  feat(ui): add TextMate->AvalonEdit colorizing transformer\n\n  Hand-written adapter: per visible line, TokenizeLine with threaded grammar\n  state, maps most-specific scope to a theme foreground brush, applied as line\n  part foreground. Inserted before the intra-line colorizer.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n### Task 8.5: Integrate syntax into DiffView; theme-driven re-tokenize; guard wiring\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`\n\nWire syntax into the control: when `SyntaxLanguageId`/`IsDarkTheme` change (the `OnSyntaxChanged` callback stubbed in 7.2), rebuild the `TextMateThemeProvider`, load the grammar, and — only if `SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize` passes — insert a `TextMateColorizer` into each editor's `LineTransformers` **before** the existing `IntraLineColorizer`, so diff tints layer over syntax. Re-applied on theme change. Manual verification.\n\n- [ ] **Step 1: Add syntax fields and the install/clear helpers**\n\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Controls/DiffView.xaml.cs`. Add usings:\n\n  ```csharp\n  using GitDelta.UI.Controls.Diff.Syntax;\n  using ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.Rendering;\n  ```\n\n  Add fields and helpers to the class:\n\n  ```csharp\n      private TextMateThemeProvider? _themeProvider;\n      private readonly Dictionary<ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor, TextMateColorizer> _syntaxColorizers = new();\n\n      private void ApplySyntax()\n      {\n          ConfigureEditorsOnce();\n          ClearSyntax();\n\n          string? langId = SyntaxLanguageId;\n          FileDiff? diff = FileDiff;\n          if (langId is null || diff is null || diff.IsBinary)\n          {\n              return;\n          }\n\n          _themeProvider = new TextMateThemeProvider(IsDarkTheme);\n\n          foreach (ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor in new[] { LeftEditor, RightEditor, UnifiedEditor })\n          {\n              int lineCount = editor.Document.LineCount;\n              int chars = editor.Document.TextLength;\n              if (!SyntaxGuard.ShouldTokenize(langId, lineCount, chars, diff.IsBinary))\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              TextMateSharp.Grammars.IGrammar? grammar = _themeProvider.LoadGrammar(langId);\n              if (grammar is null)\n              {\n                  continue;\n              }\n\n              var colorizer = new TextMateColorizer(_themeProvider, grammar);\n\n              // Insert syntax BEFORE the intra-line colorizer so diff tints layer on top.\n              IList<IVisualLineTransformer> transformers = editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers;\n              int intraIndex = IndexOfIntra(editor, transformers);\n              if (intraIndex >= 0)\n              {\n                  transformers.Insert(intraIndex, colorizer);\n              }\n              else\n              {\n                  transformers.Add(colorizer);\n              }\n\n              _syntaxColorizers[editor] = colorizer;\n              editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();\n          }\n      }\n\n      private int IndexOfIntra(ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor, IList<IVisualLineTransformer> transformers)\n      {\n          IntraLineColorizer intra = editor == LeftEditor ? _leftIntra\n              : editor == RightEditor ? _rightIntra\n              : _unifiedIntra;\n          return transformers.IndexOf(intra);\n      }\n\n      private void ClearSyntax()\n      {\n          foreach ((ICSharpCode.AvalonEdit.TextEditor editor, TextMateColorizer colorizer) in _syntaxColorizers)\n          {\n              editor.TextArea.TextView.LineTransformers.Remove(colorizer);\n              editor.TextArea.TextView.Redraw();\n          }\n\n          _syntaxColorizers.Clear();\n      }\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 2: Wire the OnSyntaxChanged callback and re-run syntax after a rebuild**\n\n  Replace the empty `OnSyntaxChanged` (from Task 7.2):\n\n  ```csharp\n      private static void OnSyntaxChanged(DependencyObject d, DependencyPropertyChangedEventArgs e)\n      {\n          ((DiffView)d).ApplySyntax();\n      }\n  ```\n\n  And at the very end of `Rebuild` (Task 7.7), after `ApplyDisplayOptions()` and the truncated banner block, re-apply syntax so a new document gets highlighted:\n\n  ```csharp\n          ApplySyntax();\n  ```\n\n- [ ] **Step 3: Build**\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet build src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n  ```\n\n  Expected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [ ] **Step 4: Manual verification — syntax + theme swap + layering**\n\n  Re-add the Task 7.7 harness but use realistic C# content and set the syntax/theme properties:\n\n  ```csharp\n  demo.SyntaxLanguageId = "csharp";\n  demo.IsDarkTheme = true;\n  ```\n\n  Use `FileDiff` lines containing real C# (e.g. `public static int Add(int a, int b) => a + b;` as context, a deleted/added pair with a changed literal). Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Settings;\n\npublic sealed class JsonSettingsStoreTests : IDisposable\n{\n    private readonly string _baseDir;\n\n    public public void Dispose()\n    {\n        try { Directory.Delete(_baseDir, recursive: true); } catch { /* best effort */ }\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Theme = AppTheme.Dark,\n            DefaultDiffView = DiffViewMode.Unified,\n            ContextLines = 7,\n            TabSize = 2,\n            SyntaxHighlighting = false,\n            ExternalEditorCommand = "code -g {file}",\n            WindowWidth = 1440,\n            WindowHeight = 900,\n            HistoryPaneWidth = 320,\n            FilesPaneWidth = 300,\n        };\n\n        store.Save(settings);\n        var reloaded = store.Load();\n\n        reloaded.ShouldBe(settings);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void
