   }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Save_CreatesFileUnderGitDeltaFolder()\n    {\n        var store = new JsonSettingsStore(_baseDir);\n\n        store.Save(new AppSettings { ContextLines = 5 });\n\n        File.Exists(Path.Combine(_baseDir, "GitDelta", "settings.json")).ShouldBeTrue();\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run the test and confirm it FAILS to compile.** `JsonSettingsStore` does not exist yet, so the compile fails (this is the expected red state):\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~JsonSettingsStoreTests"\n```\n\nExpected: build error `CS0246: The type or namespace name 'JsonSettingsStore' could not be found`.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Implement `JsonSettingsStore`.** It accepts a base directory (defaults to `%APPDATA%`), writes via temp-file-then-rename for crash safety, and returns defaults on missing/corrupt. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Settings/JsonSettingsStore.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.IO;\nusing System.Text.Json;\nusing System.Text.Json.Serialization;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Settings;\n\npublic sealed class JsonSettingsStore : ISettingsStore\n{\n    private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions SerializerOptions = new()\n    {\n        WriteIndented = true,\n        Converters = { new JsonStringEnumConverter() },\n    };\n\n    private readonly string _settingsPath;\n    private readonly Lock _gate = new();\n\n    /// <summary>Default constructor targets %APPDATA%/GitDelta/settings.json.</summary>\n    public JsonSettingsStore()\n        : this(Environment.GetFolderPath(Environment.SpecialFolder.ApplicationData))\n    {\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Test/seam constructor: <paramref name="baseDirectory"/> stands in for %APPDATA%.</summary>\n    public JsonSettingsStore(string baseDirectory)\n    {\n        _settingsPath = Path.Combine(baseDirectory, "GitDelta", "settings.json");\n    }\n\n    public AppSettings Load()\n    {\n        lock (_gate)\n        {\n            if (!File.Exists(_settingsPath))\n            {\n                return new AppSettings();\n            }\n\n            try\n            {\n                var json = File.ReadAllText(_settingsPath);\n                return JsonSerializer.Deserialize<AppSettings>(json, SerializerOptions) ?? new AppSettings();\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when (ex is JsonException or IOException or UnauthorizedAccessException)\n            {\n                return new AppSettings();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    public void Save(AppSettings settings)\n    {\n        lock (_gate)\n        {\n            var directory = Path.GetDirectoryName(_settingsPath)!;\n            Directory.CreateDirectory(directory);\n\n            var json = JsonSerializer.Serialize(settings, SerializerOptions);\n            var tempPath = _settingsPath + ".tmp";\n            File.WriteAllText(tempPath, json);\n            File.Move(tempPath, _settingsPath, overwrite: true);\n        }\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run the tests and confirm they PASS.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~JsonSettingsStoreTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 4`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Settings/JsonSettingsStore.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Settings/JsonSettingsStoreTests.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add JsonSettingsStore with round-trip + corrupt-file handling\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 9.2: Relative-date formatter for CommitRowViewModel (pure logic, TDD)\n\n`CommitRowViewModel.RelativeDate` needs a deterministic, testable formatter ("2 hours ago", "3 days ago", etc.). We extract it into a WPF-free static helper in Core so it can be unit-tested without instantiating a ViewModel, then have `CommitRowViewModel` call it.\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Models/RelativeTime.cs`\n- Test: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Models/RelativeTimeTests.cs`\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the failing test.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Models/RelativeTimeTests.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\nusing Shouldly;\nusing Xunit;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Tests.Models;\n\npublic sealed class RelativeTimeTests\n{\n    private static readonly DateTimeOffset Now = new(2026, 5, 29, 12, 0, 0, TimeSpan.Zero);\n\n    [Theory]\n    [InlineData(5, "just now")]            // 5 seconds ago\n    [InlineData(45, "just now")]           // < 1 minute\n    [InlineData(60, "1 minute ago")]\n    [InlineData(150, "2 minutes ago")]\n    [InlineData(3600, "1 hour ago")]\n    [InlineData(7200, "2 hours ago")]\n    [InlineData(86400, "yesterday")]\n    [InlineData(172800, "2 days ago")]\n    [InlineData(604800, "last week")]\n    [InlineData(1209600, "2 weeks ago")]\n    public void Format_ReturnsExpectedPhrase(int secondsAgo, string expected)\n    {\n        var when = Now.AddSeconds(-secondsAgo);\n\n        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe(expected);\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Format_MonthsAgo_ReturnsMonths()\n    {\n        var when = Now.AddDays(-70);\n\n        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("2 months ago");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Format_YearsAgo_ReturnsYears()\n    {\n        var when = Now.AddDays(-800);\n\n        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("2 years ago");\n    }\n\n    [Fact]\n    public void Format_FutureTimestamp_ClampsToJustNow()\n    {\n        var when = Now.AddSeconds(30);\n\n        RelativeTime.Format(when, Now).ShouldBe("just now");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Run and confirm it FAILS to compile.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~RelativeTimeTests"\n```\n\nExpected: build error `CS0103: The name 'RelativeTime' does not exist`.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Implement `RelativeTime`.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.Core/Models/RelativeTime.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\n/// <summary>WPF-free relative-time phrasing used by commit rows.</summary>\npublic static class RelativeTime\n{\n    public static string Format(DateTimeOffset when) => Format(when, DateTimeOffset.Now);\n\n    public static string Format(DateTimeOffset when, DateTimeOffset now)\n    {\n        var delta = now - when;\n        if (delta < TimeSpan.Zero)\n        {\n            delta = TimeSpan.Zero;\n        }\n\n        var seconds = delta.TotalSeconds;\n        if (seconds < 60)\n        {\n            return "just now";\n        }\n\n        var minutes = (int)(delta.TotalMinutes);\n        if (minutes < 60)\n        {\n            return minutes == 1 ? "1 minute ago" : $"{minutes} minutes ago";\n        }\n\n        var hours = (int)(delta.TotalHours);\n        if (hours < 24)\n        {\n            return hours == 1 ? "1 hour ago" : $"{hours} hours ago";\n        }\n\n        var days = (int)(delta.TotalDays);\n        if (days < 7)\n        {\n            return days == 1 ? "yesterday" : $"{days} days ago";\n        }\n\n        if (days < 30)\n        {\n            var weeks = days / 7;\n            return weeks == 1 ? "last week" : $"{weeks} weeks ago";\n        }\n\n        if (days < 365)\n        {\n            var months = days / 30;\n            return months == 1 ? "last month" : $"{months} months ago";\n        }\n\n        var years = days / 365;\n        return years == 1 ? "last year" : $"{years} years ago";\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Run and confirm PASS.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~RelativeTimeTests"\n```\n\nExpected: `Passed!  - Failed: 0, Passed: 13`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Wire `CommitRowViewModel.RelativeDate` to `RelativeTime`.** Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs` and ensure the `RelativeDate` property delegates to the formatter. The relevant region of the constructor body should read:\n\n```csharp\nRelativeDate = RelativeTime.Format(commit.AuthorDate);\n```\n\nAdd `using GitDelta.Core.Models;` at the top of the file if it is not already present.\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Build the UI project to confirm the wiring compiles.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [x] **Step 7: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.Core/Models/RelativeTime.cs tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/Models/RelativeTimeTests.cs src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/CommitRowViewModel.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(core): add RelativeTime formatter and use it for commit row dates\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 9.3: IFolderPicker abstraction + WPF-UI implementation\n\n`ShellViewModel`/`StartViewModel` need to open a folder picker. To keep the ViewModels unit-testable (no live dialogs), define an `IFolderPicker` abstraction. The interface lives in the UI layer (it is a UI concern), and the concrete implementation uses WPF-UI's `Wpf.Ui.Controls.OpenFolderDialog`. ViewModels receive `IFolderPicker` by constructor injection (this matches the `...` parameters in the `ShellViewModel`/`StartViewModel`/`MainWindowViewModel` backbone signatures).\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IFolderPicker.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/WpfFolderPicker.cs`\n\nThis is non-unit-testable UI glue (it shows an OS dialog), so we verify by build only; the picker is exercised manually in Task 9.9.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the interface.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/IFolderPicker.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\n/// <summary>Abstracts the OS "open folder" dialog so ViewModels stay unit-testable.</summary>\npublic interface IFolderPicker\n{\n    /// <summary>Shows a folder picker. Returns the selected absolute path, or null if cancelled.</summary>\n    string? PickFolder(string title);\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Create the WPF-UI implementation.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Services/WpfFolderPicker.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing Wpf.Ui.Controls;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Services;\n\npublic sealed class WpfFolderPicker : IFolderPicker\n{\n    public string? PickFolder(string title)\n    {\n        var dialog = new OpenFolderDialog\n        {\n            Title = title,\n            Multiselect = false,\n        };\n\n        if (dialog.ShowDialog() == true && !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(dialog.FolderName))\n        {\n            return dialog.FolderName;\n        }\n\n        return null;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Build to confirm the WPF-UI `OpenFolderDialog` API matches.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. These are tiny `IValueConverter`s used from XAML.\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/ChangeKindToBrushConverter.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/BoolToVisibilityConverter.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/NullToVisibilityConverter.cs`\n\nThese are UI-only; verify by build. (Glyph/counts text comes from `FileRowViewModel.StatusGlyph`/`Added`/`Deleted`, which were built in an earlier phase.)\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the change-kind brush converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/ChangeKindToBrushConverter.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Windows.Data;\nusing System.Windows.Media;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Models;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;\n\n/// <summary>Maps a ChangeKind to a status-glyph brush (green add / red delete / orange modify / blue rename).</summary>\npublic sealed class ChangeKindToBrushConverter : IValueConverter\n{\n    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n    {\n        var color = value is ChangeKind kind\n            ? kind switch\n            {\n                ChangeKind.Added or ChangeKind.Untracked or ChangeKind.Copied => Color.FromRgb(0x3F, 0xB9, 0x50),\n                ChangeKind.Deleted => Color.FromRgb(0xE5, 0x53, 0x4B),\n                ChangeKind.Renamed => Color.FromRgb(0x4F, 0x9C, 0xF5),\n                ChangeKind.Conflicted => Color.FromRgb(0xD2, 0x9A, 0x1F),\n                _ => Color.FromRgb(0xCC, 0x8E, 0x35),\n            }\n            : Color.FromRgb(0x80, 0x80, 0x80);\n\n        return new SolidColorBrush(color);\n    }\n\n    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n        => throw new NotSupportedException();\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Create the bool-to-visibility converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/BoolToVisibilityConverter.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Windows;\nusing System.Windows.Data;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;\n\n/// <summary>true => Visible, false => Collapsed. Set Invert=true to flip.</summary>\npublic sealed class BoolToVisibilityConverter : IValueConverter\n{\n    public bool Invert { get; set; }\n\n    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n    {\n        var flag = value is true;\n        if (Invert)\n        {\n            flag = !flag;\n        }\n\n        return flag ? Visibility.Visible : Visibility.Collapsed;\n    }\n\n    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n        => throw new NotSupportedException();\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the null-to-visibility converter.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/NullToVisibilityConverter.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Globalization;\nusing System.Windows;\nusing System.Windows.Data;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Converters;\n\n/// <summary>non-null => Visible, null => Collapsed. Set Invert=true to flip.</summary>\npublic sealed class NullToVisibilityConverter : IValueConverter\n{\n    public bool Invert { get; set; }\n\n    public object Convert(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n    {\n        var hasValue = value is not null;\n        if (Invert)\n        {\n            hasValue = !hasValue;\n        }\n\n        return hasValue ? Visibility.Visible : Visibility.Collapsed;\n    }\n\n    public object ConvertBack(object? value, Type targetType, object? parameter, CultureInfo culture)\n        => throw new NotSupportedException();\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Build to confirm the converters compile.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/Converters/\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): add change-kind brush + visibility value converters\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 9.5: ShellView — 3-pane workspace XAML\n\nBuild the `ShellView` UserControl: History (left, virtualized, pinned working-tree row on top), Changed files (middle, grouped-by-folder with a flat toggle), Diff (right, hosting `DiffView` + the diff toolbar). code-behind.** It owns the toolbar `Click` handlers (calling `DiffView` public methods), the infinite-scroll handler (calls `LoadMoreHistoryCommand` near the bottom), the multi-select bridge (pushes selection into `ShellViewModel.SelectedCommits` and triggers comparison), and the flat-toggle (clears/sets the folder grouping). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/ShellView.xaml.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Windows;\nusing System.Windows.Controls;\nusing System.Windows.Data;\nusing GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Views;\n\npublic partial class ShellView : UserControl\n{\n    public ShellView()\n    {\n        InitializeComponent();\n        Loaded += OnLoaded;\n    }\n\n    private ShellViewModel? ViewModel => DataContext as ShellViewModel;\n\n    private void OnLoaded(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)\n    {\n        FlatToggle.Checked += OnFlatToggleChanged;\n        FlatToggle.Unchecked += OnFlatToggleChanged;\n    }\n\n    private void OnFlatToggleChanged(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e)\n    {\n        if (Resources["GroupedFiles"] is not CollectionViewSource cvs)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        cvs.GroupDescriptions.Clear();\n        if (FlatToggle.IsChecked != true)\n        {\n            cvs.GroupDescriptions.Add(new PropertyGroupDescription("Folder"));\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void HistoryList_SelectionChanged(object sender, SelectionChangedEventArgs e)\n    {\n        if (ViewModel is null)\n        {\n            return;\n        }\n\n        ViewModel.SelectedCommits.Clear();\n        foreach (var item in HistoryList.SelectedItems)\n        {\n            if (item is CommitRowViewModel row)\n            {\n                ViewModel.SelectedCommits.Add(row);\n            }\n        }\n\n        ViewModel.OnHistorySelectionChanged();\n    }\n\n    private void HistoryList_ScrollChanged(object sender, ScrollChangedEventArgs e)\n    {\n        // Trigger paging when within ~3 rows of the bottom and there is more to scroll.\n        if (e.VerticalOffset > 0 && e.VerticalOffset >= e.ExtentHeight - e.ViewportHeight - 3\n            && ViewModel?.LoadMoreHistoryCommand.CanExecute(null) == true)\n        {\n            ViewModel.LoadMoreHistoryCommand.Execute(null);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void OnFind(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.ShowFind();\n\n    private void OnPreviousChange(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.GoToPreviousChange();\n\n    private void OnNextChange(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.GoToNextChange();\n\n    private void OnCopy(object sender, RoutedEventArgs e) => Diff.CopySelection();\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Add `OnHistorySelectionChanged` to `ShellViewModel`.** The code-behind needs a method to recompute the `DiffSpec` from the current selection (the backbone says: working-tree selected => `WorkingTreeVsHead`; 1 commit => `CommitVsParent`; 2 => `TwoCommits(older,newer)`). Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/ShellViewModel.cs` and add this method (it drives `SetComparisonAsync`):\n\n```csharp\npublic void OnHistorySelectionChanged()\n{\n    if (SelectedCommits.Count == 0)\n    {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    WorkingTreeRow.IsSelected = false;\n\n    DiffSpec spec = SelectedCommits.Count == 1\n        ? new DiffSpec.CommitVsParent(SelectedCommits[0].Sha)\n        : BuildTwoCommitSpec();\n\n    _ = SetComparisonAsync(spec, CancellationToken.None);\n}\n\nprivate DiffSpec BuildTwoCommitSpec()\n{\n    // History is newest-first; the lower index is the newer commit.\n    var first = SelectedCommits[0];\n    var second = SelectedCommits[1];\n    var firstIndex = History.IndexOf(first);\n    var secondIndex = History.IndexOf(second);\n    // older = larger index (further down history) => base; newer => target\n    return firstIndex > secondIndex\n        ? new DiffSpec.TwoCommits(first.Sha, second.Sha)\n        : new DiffSpec.TwoCommits(second.Sha, first.Sha);\n}\n```\n\nEnsure `using GitDelta.Core.Git;` and `using System.Threading;` are present at the top of `ShellViewModel.cs`.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Build to confirm the XAML, converters, and `DiffView` DP bindings all resolve.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Views/MainWindow.xaml.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing GitDelta.UI.ViewModels;\nusing Wpf.Ui;\nusing Wpf.Ui.Appearance;\nusing Wpf.Ui.Controls;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Views;\n\npublic partial class MainWindow : FluentWindow\n{\n    private readonly MainWindowViewModel _viewModel;\n\n    public MainWindow(MainWindowViewModel viewModel, IContentDialogService contentDialogService)\n    {\n        _viewModel = viewModel;\n        DataContext = viewModel;\n        InitializeComponent();\n\n        contentDialogService.SetDialogHost(RootContentDialogHost);\n        SystemThemeWatcher.Watch(this);\n    }\n\n    public MainWindowViewModel ViewModel => _viewModel;\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Add title-bar forwarding + persistence to `MainWindowViewModel`.** Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs`. Add observable `WindowWidth`/`WindowHeight` (seeded from settings, persisted on change) and the title-bar relay commands that forward to the active `ShellViewModel`:\n\n```csharp\n[ObservableProperty]\nprivate double _windowWidth = 1100;\n\n[ObservableProperty]\nprivate double _windowHeight = 720;\n\npublic string? RepoName => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.RepoName;\n\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate async Task OpenFolderAsync()\n{\n    switch (CurrentContent)\n    {\n        case ShellViewModel shell:\n            await shell.OpenFolderCommand.ExecuteAsync(null);\n            break;\n        case StartViewModel start:\n            await start.OpenFolderCommand.ExecuteAsync(null);\n            break;\n    }\n}\n\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate void ToggleTheme() => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.ToggleThemeCommand.Execute(null);\n\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate void OpenSettings() => (CurrentContent as ShellViewModel)?.OpenSettingsCommand.Execute(null);\n\npartial void OnCurrentContentChanged(ObservableObject? value) => OnPropertyChanged(nameof(RepoName));\n\npartial void OnWindowWidthChanged(double value) => PersistWindowSize();\n\npartial void OnWindowHeightChanged(double value) => PersistWindowSize();\n\nprivate void PersistWindowSize()\n{\n    var current = _settings.Load();\n    _settings.Save(current with { WindowWidth = WindowWidth, WindowHeight = WindowHeight });\n}\n```\n\nSeed `WindowWidth`/`WindowHeight` from `_settings.Load()` in the constructor, where `_settings` is the injected `ISettingsStore`. Ensure `using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.ComponentModel;`, `using CommunityToolkit.Mvvm.Input;`, and `using GitDelta.Core.Settings;` are present.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Implement `ShellViewModel.OpenSettings` + theme + folder picker + persistence.** Open `ShellViewModel.cs` and implement the relay-command bodies (these are the backbone commands `OpenSettings`, `ToggleTheme`, `OpenFolderAsync`). `OpenSettings` shows the `SettingsDialog`; on `Save`, it persists via `ISettingsStore` and re-applies theme + default diff view. Because the dialog and folder picker are UI, inject `IContentDialogService`, `IFolderPicker`, and a `Func<SettingsViewModel>` (these are the `...` constructor params in the backbone). Add:\n\n```csharp\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate async Task OpenSettingsAsync()\n{\n    var current = _settings.Load();\n    var vm = _settingsViewModelFactory();\n    var presenter = _contentDialogService.GetDialogHost();\n    var dialog = new SettingsDialog(presenter, vm);\n\n    var result = await dialog.ShowAsync(CancellationToken.None);\n    if (result != ContentDialogResult.Primary)\n    {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    vm.Save();\n    var updated = vm.Result;\n    _settings.Save(updated);\n\n    ApplyTheme(updated.Theme);\n    Diff.ViewMode = updated.DefaultDiffView;\n    Diff.TabSize = updated.TabSize;\n}\n\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate void ToggleTheme()\n{\n    var current = _settings.Load();\n    var next = current.Theme == AppTheme.Dark ? AppTheme.Light : AppTheme.Dark;\n    _settings.Save(current with { Theme = next });\n    ApplyTheme(next);\n}\n\n[RelayCommand]\nprivate async Task OpenFolderAsync()\n{\n    var folder = _folderPicker.PickFolder("Open a Git repository");\n    if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(folder))\n    {\n        return;\n    }\n\n    var root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(folder, CancellationToken.None);\n    if (root is not null)\n    {\n        await LoadRepositoryAsync(root, CancellationToken.None);\n    }\n    else\n    {\n        StatusMessage = "That folder is not inside a Git repository.";\n    }\n}\n\nprivate void ApplyTheme(AppTheme theme)\n{\n    switch (theme)\n    {\n        case AppTheme.Light:\n            ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Light);\n            Diff.IsDarkTheme = false;\n            break;\n        case AppTheme.Dark:\n            ApplicationThemeManager.Apply(ApplicationTheme.Dark);\n            Diff.IsDarkTheme = true;\n            break;\n        default:\n            ApplicationThemeManager.ApplySystemTheme();\n            Diff.IsDarkTheme = ApplicationThemeManager.GetAppTheme() == ApplicationTheme.Dark;\n            break;\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAdd the fields `_contentDialogService`, `_folderPicker`, This phase implements arg routing in App startup via `ArgRouter.Route`, the `AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS)` P/Invoke with a `GetFileType`-guarded `CONOUT$` reopen (so redirection/pipes still work), and passing the resolved `LaunchAction` into `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.\n\n`ArgRouter.Route` (pure logic) was built and unit-tested in an earlier Core phase per the backbone; this phase consumes it and adds the native console plumbing (P/Invoke; not unit-testable — verified by running the built exe from a terminal).\n\n### Task 10.1: NativeConsole P/Invoke helper\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/NativeConsole.cs`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/ConsoleOutput.cs`\n\nThese wrap unmanaged calls; not unit-testable. Verify by build now and by running from a terminal in Task 10.3.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the P/Invoke surface.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/NativeConsole.cs`. It exposes `TryAttachToParentConsole()` which attaches to the parent terminal and, only if stdout is a real char device (a console), reopens `CONOUT$` so writes appear in the terminal — while leaving redirected/piped stdout untouched so `gitdelta --version > out.txt` and `gitdelta --version | findstr` still work.\n\n```csharp\nusing System.IO;\nusing System.Runtime.InteropServices;\nusing Microsoft.Win32.SafeHandles;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Cli;\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Win32 console plumbing for a WinExe that must emit text to the launching terminal\n/// for --help/--version while preserving redirection and pipes.\n/// </summary>\ninternal static partial class NativeConsole\n{\n    private const int ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS = -1;\n\n    private const uint GENERIC_WRITE = 0x40000000;\n    private const uint FILE_SHARE_WRITE = 0x00000002;\n    private const uint OPEN_EXISTING = 3;\n\n    private const uint FILE_TYPE_UNKNOWN = 0x0000;\n    private const uint FILE_TYPE_CHAR = 0x0002;\n\n    private const int STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE = -11;\n\n    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]\n    [return: MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)]\n    private static partial bool AttachConsole(int dwProcessId);\n\n    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]\n    [return: MarshalAs(UnmanagedType.Bool)]\n    private static partial bool FreeConsole();\n\n    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]\n    private static partial nint GetStdHandle(int nStdHandle);\n\n    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", SetLastError = true)]\n    private static partial uint GetFileType(nint hFile);\n\n    [LibraryImport("kernel32.dll", EntryPoint = "CreateFileW", SetLastError = true, StringMarshalling = StringMarshalling.Utf16)]\n    private static partial SafeFileHandle CreateFile(\n        string lpFileName,\n        uint dwDesiredAccess,\n        uint dwShareMode,\n        nint lpSecurityAttributes,\n        uint dwCreationDisposition,\n        uint dwFlagsAndAttributes,\n        nint hTemplateFile);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Attaches to the parent console. Returns true if a console is now available\n    /// for writing (whether via an attached terminal or via redirection/pipe).\n    /// </summary>\n    public static bool TryAttachToParentConsole()\n    {\n        // If stdout is already redirected (file/pipe), the existing stream is valid —\n        // we must NOT replace it, or redirection breaks. Detect that first.\n        if (IsStdOutRedirected())\n        {\n            // Still attach so Console.Out flushes to the right place when not redirected,\n            // but the redirected handle already routes correctly; nothing more to do.\n            AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS);\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        if (!AttachConsole(ATTACH_PARENT_PROCESS))\n        {\n            // No parent console (e.g. launched from Explorer): nothing to write to.\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        return ReopenStdOutToConsole();\n    }\n\n    public static void Detach() => FreeConsole();\n\n    private static bool IsStdOutRedirected()\n    {\n        var handle = GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE);\n        if (handle == nint.Zero || handle == new nint(-1))\n        {\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        var type = GetFileType(handle);\n        // A char device is a console; disk/pipe means redirection is in effect.\n        return type is not FILE_TYPE_CHAR and not FILE_TYPE_UNKNOWN;\n    }\n\n    private static bool ReopenStdOutToConsole()\n    {\n        var handle = CreateFile(\n            "CONOUT$",\n            GENERIC_WRITE,\n            FILE_SHARE_WRITE,\n            nint.Zero,\n            OPEN_EXISTING,\n            0,\n            nint.Zero);\n\n        if (handle.IsInvalid)\n        {\n            handle.Dispose();\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        var stream = new FileStream(handle, FileAccess.Write);\n        var writer = new StreamWriter(stream, Console.OutputEncoding) { AutoFlush = true };\n        Console.SetOut(writer);\n        return true;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Create the help/version text writer.** Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/ConsoleOutput.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Reflection;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI.Cli;\n\n/// <summary>Renders --help / --version text to stdout.</summary>\ninternal static class ConsoleOutput\n{\n    public static void WriteHelp()\n    {\n        Console.WriteLine("GitDelta - a read-only Git diff and commit viewer.");\n        Console.WriteLine();\n        Console.WriteLine("Usage:");\n        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta                 Open the repository in the current directory.");\n        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta <path>          Open the repository at <path>.");\n        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta --help, -h, -?  Show this help.");\n        Console.WriteLine("  gitdelta --version, -v   Show the version.");\n        Console.WriteLine();\n        Console.WriteLine("With no repository context, GitDelta opens its start screen.");\n    }\n\n    public static void WriteVersion()\n    {\n        var version = Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly()\n            .GetCustomAttribute<AssemblyInformationalVersionAttribute>()?.InformationalVersion\n            ?? Assembly.GetExecutingAssembly().GetName().Version?.ToString()\n            ?? "0.0.0";\n\n        // Trim any build metadata suffix (e.g. "1.2.3+abcdef").\n        var plus = version.IndexOf('+');\n        if (plus >= 0)\n        {\n            version = version[..plus];\n        }\n\n        Console.WriteLine($"gitdelta {version}");\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Build to confirm the `LibraryImport` source generator and APIs compile.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`. (`LibraryImport` requires the partial class/methods exactly as written; if a `SYSLIB` analyzer error appears, it names the offending signature.)\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/NativeConsole.cs src/GitDelta.UI/Cli/ConsoleOutput.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): add native console attach plumbing and help/version output\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 10.2: App startup arg routing + LaunchAction handoff\n\nWire the App bootstrap to compute the `LaunchAction` via `ArgRouter.Route`, handle `PrintHelp`/`PrintVersion` on the console then shut down without showing a window, and for `OpenRepoWorkingTree`/`ShowStartScreen` build the host, resolve `MainWindow`, and pass the action into `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync`.\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`\n\nThese are bootstrap glue (not unit-testable — the routing decision itself is covered by `ArgRouter` tests in Core and the routing-to-content in `MainWindowViewModelTests`). Verify by build + terminal run.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create App.xaml.** It merges the WPF-UI themes/controls dictionaries (matching the org template) and sets no `StartupUri` (we create the window manually). Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml`:\n\n```xml\n<Application x:Class="GitDelta.UI.App"\n             xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml/presentation"\n             xmlns:x="http://schemas.microsoft.com/winfx/2006/xaml"\n             xmlns:ui="http://schemas.lepo.co/wpfui/2022/xaml">\n  <Application.Resources>\n    <ResourceDictionary>\n      <ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>\n        <ui:ThemesDictionary Theme="Dark" />\n        <ui:ControlsDictionary />\n      </ResourceDictionary.MergedDictionaries>\n    </ResourceDictionary>\n  </Application.Resources>\n</Application>\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Create App.xaml.cs.** This is the heart of dual-mode. It (a) routes args first; (b) for help/version attaches the console, writes, detaches, and `Shutdown()`s before any window; (c) otherwise builds the IHost (Autofac), installs the global exception handlers (per spec section 10), resolves `MainWindow`, sets its size, and calls `InitializeAsync` with the routed action. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs`:\n\n```csharp\nusing System.Windows;\nusing System.Windows.Threading;\nusing Autofac;\nusing Autofac.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\nusing GitDelta.Core.Cli;\nusing GitDelta.UI.Cli;\nusing GitDelta.UI.Views;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;\n\nnamespace GitDelta.UI;\n\npublic partial class App : Application\n{\n    private IHost? _host;\n\n    protected override void OnStartup(StartupEventArgs e)\n    {\n        base.OnStartup(e);\n\n        // e.Args already excludes the exe path. cwd is the launching directory.\n        var action = ArgRouter.Route(e.Args, Directory.GetCurrentDirectory());\n\n        // Console-only fast paths: write to the parent terminal and exit without a window.\n        if (action.Kind is LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp or LaunchActionKind.PrintVersion)\n        {\n            RunConsoleMode(action);\n            Shutdown();\n            return;\n        }\n\n        InstallGlobalExceptionHandlers();\n\n        _host = Host.CreateDefaultBuilder()\n            .UseServiceProviderFactory(new AutofacServiceProviderFactory())\n            .ConfigureContainer<ContainerBuilder>(builder => builder.RegisterModule<AppModule>())\n            .Build();\n\n        _host.Start();\n\n        var scope = _host.Services.GetRequiredService<ILifetimeScope>();\n        var window = scope.Resolve<MainWindow>();\n        window.Show();\n\n        // Kick off async initialization (routing to start screen vs working-tree).\n        _ = window.ViewModel.InitializeAsync(action, CancellationToken.None);\n    }\n\n    private static void RunConsoleMode(LaunchAction action)\n    {\n        var attached = NativeConsole.TryAttachToParentConsole();\n\n        if (action.Kind == LaunchActionKind.PrintHelp)\n        {\n            ConsoleOutput.WriteHelp();\n        }\n        else\n        {\n            ConsoleOutput.WriteVersion();\n        }\n\n        if (attached)\n        {\n            Console.Out.Flush();\n            NativeConsole.Detach();\n        }\n    }\n\n    private void InstallGlobalExceptionHandlers()\n    {\n        DispatcherUnhandledException += OnDispatcherUnhandledException;\n\n        AppDomain.CurrentDomain.UnhandledException += (_, args) =>\n        {\n            // Non-UI fatal path: log via Debug; structured logging added in the logging phase.\n            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[FATAL] {args.ExceptionObject}");\n        };\n\n        TaskScheduler.UnobservedTaskException += (_, args) =>\n        {\n            System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[UNOBSERVED] {args.Exception}");\n            args.SetObserved();\n        };\n    }\n\n    private void OnDispatcherUnhandledException(object sender, DispatcherUnhandledExceptionEventArgs e)\n    {\n        System.Diagnostics.Debug.WriteLine($"[UI] {e.Exception}");\n        MessageBox.Show(\n            $"An unexpected error occurred: {e.Exception.Message}",\n            "GitDelta",\n            MessageBoxButton.OK,\n            MessageBoxImage.Error);\n        e.Handled = e.Exception is not (OutOfMemoryException or StackOverflowException);\n    }\n\n    protected override async void OnExit(ExitEventArgs e)\n    {\n        if (_host is not null)\n        {\n            await _host.StopAsync();\n            _host.Dispose();\n        }\n\n        base.OnExit(e);\n    }\n}\n```\n\nAdd `using System.IO;` if the analyzer flags `Directory`/`File` (ImplicitUsings covers `System.IO` only via the SDK default set for some workloads — include it explicitly to be safe). Ensure the UI csproj from Phase 1 sets `<ApplicationDefinition Include="App.xaml" />` implicitly (default for WPF SDK) so this `App` is the entry point.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Confirm `MainWindowViewModel.InitializeAsync` honors all `LaunchActionKind`s.** Open `MainWindowViewModel.cs` and verify `InitializeAsync` matches the routing in the backbone: `ShowStartScreen` => `ShowStartAsync()`; `OpenRepoWorkingTree` => resolve via `IGitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(action.RepoPath!)`, on null fall back to `ShowStartAsync()`, otherwise `OpenRepositoryAsync(root)`. (`PrintHelp`/`PrintVersion` never reach here because App handled them.) If the body is not already present, implement:\n\n```csharp\npublic async Task InitializeAsync(LaunchAction action, CancellationToken ct)\n{\n    switch (action.Kind)\n    {\n        case LaunchActionKind.OpenRepoWorkingTree:\n            var root = await _gitReader.FindRepositoryRootAsync(action.RepoPath!, ct);\n            if (root is not null)\n            {\n                await OpenRepositoryAsync(root);\n            }\n            else\n            {\n                await ShowStartAsync();\n            }\n            break;\n\n        default:\n            await ShowStartAsync();\n            break;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Build the solution.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln\n```\n\nExpected: `Build succeeded. 0 Warning(s) 0 Error(s)`.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Run the existing routing tests to confirm nothing regressed.**\n\n```powershell\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests/GitDelta.Core.Tests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~ArgRouter"\ndotnet test C:/code/projects/GitDelta/tests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests/GitDelta.UI.UnitTests.csproj --filter "FullyQualifiedName~MainWindowViewModelTests"\n```\n\nExpected: both report `Passed!  - Failed: 0`.\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.**\n\n```powershell\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml src/GitDelta.UI/App.xaml.cs src/GitDelta.UI/ViewModels/MainWindowViewModel.cs\ngit -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\nfeat(ui): route CLI args at startup and hand LaunchAction to the shell\n\nCo-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n'@\n```\n\n### Task 10.3: Manual verification of dual-mode console behavior\n\nThe P/Invoke console attach cannot be unit-tested; it must be observed against a real terminal and against redirection/pipes. Run it with a non-repo path (`& ...gitdelta.exe C:/Windows`) and confirm the start screen appears. Double-click `gitdelta.exe` in Explorer (no parent console, no args) and confirm the start screen appears with no console flash.\n\n- [ ] **Step 7: No commit needed for verification-only.** If any step fails (e.g. redirection produces empty `ver.txt`), the most likely cause is the `IsStdOutRedirected` guard or `CONOUT$` reopen in `NativeConsole`; fix there, rebuild, re-run, then commit the fix with a `fix(ui): ...` message and the standard `Co-Authored-By` trailer.\n\n## Phase 11: Packaging & Distribution\n\nThis phase produces the Release publish configuration for `src/GitDelta.UI`, the Inno Setup installer (`installer/GitDelta.iss`), a README packaging/PATH section, and an end-to-end verification checklist. None of this phase is unit-testable (publish output, installer behavior, README prose), so every task uses **implementation steps with complete code/markup + a manual build/run verification step + a commit**. Verification steps are explicitly manual where noted.\n\nThis phase assumes the earlier phases already produced: `GitDelta.sln`, `src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` (WinExe, `net10.0-windows10.0.26100.0`, `UseWPF`, AssemblyName/output exe `gitdelta`), `Directory.Build.props`, `Directory.Packages.props`, `version.json`, and `CLAUDE.md`. This phase only adds publish properties, the installer folder, the runtime bootstrapper bundling, and docs — it does not redefine those projects.\n\n> **Prerequisites for the engineer's machine (one-time, manual):**\n> - .NET 10 SDK installed (`dotnet --version` reports `10.x`).\n> - Inno Setup 6.x installed (provides the compiler `ISCC.exe`, normally at `C:\Program Files (x86)\Inno Setup 6\ISCC.exe`). Install it from https://jrsoftware.org/isdl.php or via `winget install JRSoftware.InnoSetup`.\n\n---\n\n### Task 11.1: Add the Release single-file publish configuration to GitDelta.UI\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/Directory.Build.props.publish.notes.md` *(deleted before commit — scratch only; see Step 4)*\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Read the current GitDelta.UI.csproj.**\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj` and confirm it already contains `<OutputType>WinExe</OutputType>`, `<UseWPF>true</UseWPF>`, and `<AssemblyName>gitdelta</AssemblyName>` (so the produced exe is `gitdelta.exe`). If `<AssemblyName>gitdelta</AssemblyName>` is missing, that is a Phase 1 contract violation — add it now inside the first `<PropertyGroup>`. The publish properties below depend on the assembly name being `gitdelta`.\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Add the publish PropertyGroup to GitDelta.UI.csproj.**\n  These properties are scoped to `Configuration == Release` so debug builds stay fast and un-bundled. We set framework-dependent single-file (`SelfContained=false`), enable native-lib self-extract and compression, and explicitly turn **off** trimming (WPF trimming is SDK-disabled and would error). `RuntimeIdentifier` is set here so `dotnet build -c Release` and IDE publish both agree; the CLI command in Step 3 also passes `-r win-x64` for clarity.\n  Add this block to `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj`, immediately before the closing `</Project>` tag:\n\n  ```xml\n  <!-- Release single-file publish: framework-dependent (.NET 10 Desktop Runtime required on the\n       target machine). No trimming (WPF trimming is disabled by the SDK and would fail the build). -->\n  <PropertyGroup Condition="'$(Configuration)' == 'Release'">\n    <RuntimeIdentifier>win-x64</RuntimeIdentifier>\n    <PlatformTarget>x64</PlatformTarget>\n    <SelfContained>false</SelfContained>\n    <PublishSingleFile>true</PublishSingleFile>\n    <IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract>true</IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract>\n    <EnableCompressionInSingleFile>true</EnableCompressionInSingleFile>\n    <PublishTrimmed>false</PublishTrimmed>\n    <PublishReadyToRun>false</PublishReadyToRun>\n    <DebugType>embedded</DebugType>\n    <SatelliteResourceLanguages>en</SatelliteResourceLanguages>\n  </PropertyGroup>\n  ```\n\n  > Note: `IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract=true` makes the single exe self-extract the few unmanaged WPF helper DLLs at first run; without it WPF apps refuse to publish as a true single file. `DebugType=embedded` keeps the PDB inside the exe so we ship one file. `SatelliteResourceLanguages=en` drops localized resource folders (smaller, single-file-friendly).\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the publish helper script.**\n  This script centralizes the exact publish command so the installer build (Task 11.2) and humans use the same output path. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1`:\n\n  ```powershell\n  #Requires -Version 7.0\n  <#\n  .SYNOPSIS\n    Publishes GitDelta.UI as a framework-dependent, compressed, single-file gitdelta.exe.\n  .DESCRIPTION\n    Output: <repo>\publish\gitdelta.exe  (plus gitdelta.pdb is embedded, so one file).\n    Framework-dependent: the target machine needs the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime (the installer\n    in Task 11.2 detects and installs it).\n  #>\n  [CmdletBinding()]\n  param(\n      [string] $Configuration = 'Release',\n      [string] $Runtime       = 'win-x64'\n  )\n\n  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'\n\n  $repoRoot   = Split-Path -Parent $PSScriptRoot\n  $project    = Join-Path $repoRoot 'src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj'\n  $outDir     = Join-Path $repoRoot 'publish'\n\n  if (Test-Path $outDir) {\n      Remove-Item -Recurse -Force $outDir\n  }\n\n  Write-Host "Publishing GitDelta.UI ($Configuration / $Runtime) -> $outDir" -ForegroundColor Cyan\n\n  dotnet publish $project `\n      -c $Configuration `\n      -r $Runtime `\n      --self-contained false `\n      -p:PublishSingleFile=true `\n      -p:IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract=true `\n      -p:EnableCompressionInSingleFile=true `\n      -p:PublishTrimmed=false `\n      -o $outDir\n\n  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {\n      throw "dotnet publish failed with exit code $LASTEXITCODE"\n  }\n\n  $exe = Join-Path $outDir 'gitdelta.exe'\n  if (-not (Test-Path $exe)) {\n      throw "Expected output not found: $exe"\n  }\n\n  $sizeMb = [math]::Round((Get-Item $exe).Length / 1MB, 1)\n  Write-Host "OK: $exe ($sizeMb MB)" -ForegroundColor Green\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Build-verify the publish (MANUAL).**\n  Run the exact framework-dependent single-file publish command (this is the canonical command the spec requires). From the repo root `C:/code/projects/GitDelta`:\n\n  ```powershell\n  dotnet publish src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj -c Release -r win-x64 --self-contained false -p:PublishSingleFile=true -p:IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract=true -p:EnableCompressionInSingleFile=true -p:PublishTrimmed=false -o publish\n  ```\n\n  **Expected:** the command ends with `Build succeeded` / no errors, and `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish/gitdelta.exe` exists. Verify the single-file shape and that no trimming was applied:\n\n  ```powershell\n  Get-ChildItem C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish | Select-Object Name, Length\n  ```\n\n  **Expected to observe:** `gitdelta.exe` present, size roughly **5–15 MB** (compressed single file). There should be **no** `*.dll` next to it for the managed app assemblies (framework-dependent + single-file bundles them inside the exe). A `gitdelta.exe` plus possibly a couple of `*.json` config files is fine; a folder full of dozens of DLLs means single-file was NOT applied — re-check Step 2.\n\n  Smoke-run the version path against the built exe (this is the same `--version` path Phase 0/CLI implemented):\n\n  ```powershell\n  & C:/code/projects/GitDelta/publish/gitdelta.exe --version\n  ```\n\n  **Expected:** the version string (e.g. `gitdelta 1.0.0`) prints to the terminal and the process exits without launching a window. Now delete the scratch notes file if you created one and remove the throwaway `publish/` output from source control consideration (it must be gitignored — see Step 5):\n\n  ```powershell\n  Remove-Item -Force C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/Directory.Build.props.publish.notes.md -ErrorAction SilentlyContinue\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Ensure publish output is gitignored.**\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/.gitignore` and confirm it ignores build artifacts. If a `publish/` ignore line is absent, add these lines at the end:\n\n  ```gitignore\n  # Publish output and installer artifacts\n  /publish/\n  /installer/Output/\n  /installer/runtime/*.exe\n  ```\n\n  > The `/installer/runtime/*.exe` line keeps the large bundled .NET runtime installer (added in Task 11.2) out of git — it is fetched at build time, not committed.\n\n- [x] **Step 6: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add src/GitDelta.UI/GitDelta.UI.csproj build/publish.ps1 .gitignore\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  build: add framework-dependent single-file Release publish for gitdelta.exe\n\n  - Scope PublishSingleFile / IncludeNativeLibrariesForSelfExtract /\n    EnableCompressionInSingleFile / SelfContained=false to Release (no trimming).\n  - Add build/publish.ps1 wrapper producing publish/gitdelta.exe.\n  - Gitignore publish/ and installer artifacts.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Task 11.2: Author the Inno Setup installer (per-user, PATH, runtime detection)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/GitDelta.iss`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/runtime/.gitkeep`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/fetch-runtime.ps1`\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Create the runtime bundle folder and fetch script.**\n  The installer bundles the .NET 10 **Desktop** Runtime offline installer so users without it get a one-click experience. The exe itself is not committed (it is large and license-redistributed via Microsoft's CDN); this script downloads it into `installer/runtime/` before compiling the installer.\n  First create the placeholder so the folder exists in git: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/runtime/.gitkeep` with a single line:\n\n  ```text\n  Bundled .NET Desktop Runtime installer is fetched here by build/../installer/fetch-runtime.ps1 (gitignored).\n  ```\n\n  Then create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/fetch-runtime.ps1`:\n\n  ```powershell\n  #Requires -Version 7.0\n  <#\n  .SYNOPSIS\n    Downloads the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime (x64) offline installer into installer/runtime/.\n  .DESCRIPTION\n    The file is bundled by GitDelta.iss and run silently on the target machine only when the\n    runtime is missing. The exe is gitignored (fetched at build time, never committed).\n  #>\n  [CmdletBinding()]\n  param(\n      # Pinned to a known .NET 10 Desktop Runtime build. Update when bumping the runtime.\n      [string] $Version  = '10.0.0',\n      [string] $FileName = 'windowsdesktop-runtime-10.0.0-win-x64.exe'\n  )\n\n  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'\n  $runtimeDir = $PSScriptRoot\n  $target     = Join-Path $runtimeDir $FileName\n\n  if (Test-Path $target) {\n      Write-Host "Already present: $target" -ForegroundColor Green\n      return\n  }\n\n  # Microsoft's stable aka.ms redirector for the .NET Desktop Runtime offline installer.\n  $url = "https://aka.ms/dotnet/$Version/windowsdesktop-runtime-win-x64.exe"\n  Write-Host "Downloading .NET Desktop Runtime $Version -> $target" -ForegroundColor Cyan\n  Invoke-WebRequest -Uri $url -OutFile $target -UseBasicParsing\n\n  if (-not (Test-Path $target) -or (Get-Item $target).Length -lt 10MB) {\n      throw "Runtime download failed or file too small: $target"\n  }\n  Write-Host "OK: $target" -ForegroundColor Green\n  ```\n\n  > If the pinned `aka.ms` link or filename changes for the final 10.x build, update the `-Version`/`-FileName` defaults here and the `RuntimeInstaller` constant in `GitDelta.iss` (Step 2) to match.\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Write the full Inno Setup script.**\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/GitDelta.iss` with the complete script below. It is per-user (`PrivilegesRequired=lowest`), installs to `{localappdata}\Programs\GitDelta`, idempotently appends the install dir to `HKCU\Environment\Path` as `REG_EXPAND_SZ` via Pascal scripting (never `setx`), removes that PATH entry on uninstall, creates a Start Menu shortcut, gets an automatic Add/Remove Programs entry, and detects the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime — running the bundled silent installer if missing, or opening the download page if the bundle is absent.\n\n  ```ini\n  ; GitDelta installer (Inno Setup 6.x)\n  ; Per-user, no admin. Installs gitdelta.exe to %LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta,\n  ; puts the install dir on the per-user PATH, and ensures the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime.\n\n  #define AppName        "GitDelta"\n  #define AppExeName     "gitdelta.exe"\n  #define AppPublisher   "Morten Brudvik"\n  #define AppUrl         "https://github.com/mortenbrudvik/GitDelta"\n  #define AppVersion     "1.0.0"\n  ; The exe produced by build/publish.ps1\n  #define PublishDir     "..\publish"\n  ; Bundled .NET Desktop Runtime installer (fetched by installer\fetch-runtime.ps1).\n  #define RuntimeInstaller "windowsdesktop-runtime-10.0.0-win-x64.exe"\n  #define RuntimeDownloadUrl "https://dotnet.microsoft.com/download/dotnet/10.0/runtime"\n\n  [Setup]\n  AppId={{6D2B6F2E-7C2C-4F4E-9D3B-7A2E2C9A1F10}\n  AppName={#AppName}\n  AppVersion={#AppVersion}\n  AppPublisher={#AppPublisher}\n  AppPublisherURL={#AppUrl}\n  AppSupportURL={#AppUrl}\n  AppUpdatesURL={#AppUrl}/releases\n  ; Per-user install: no UAC elevation, lands in %LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta.\n  PrivilegesRequired=lowest\n  PrivilegesRequiredOverridesAllowed=dialog\n  DefaultDirName={localappdata}\Programs\{#AppName}\n  DisableProgramGroupPage=yes\n  DefaultGroupName={#AppName}\n  ; Required so Inno broadcasts WM_SETTINGCHANGE after we touch PATH (new terminals pick it up).\n  ChangesEnvironment=yes\n  ; Per-user uninstaller / Add-Remove-Programs registration (HKCU).\n  UninstallDisplayName={#AppName}\n  UninstallDisplayIcon={app}\{#AppExeName}\n  Compression=lzma2/max\n  SolidCompression=yes\n  WizardStyle=modern\n  ArchitecturesAllowed=x64compatible\n  ArchitecturesInstallIn64BitMode=x64compatible\n  OutputDir=Output\n  OutputBaseFilename=GitDelta-{#AppVersion}-setup\n  SetupIconFile=..\src\GitDelta.UI\Assets\gitdelta.ico\n\n  [Languages]\n  Name: "english"; MessagesFile: "compiler:Default.isl"\n\n  [Tasks]\n  Name: "addtopath"; Description: "Add GitDelta to the PATH (run 'gitdelta' from any terminal)"; GroupDescription: "Integration:"\n  Name: "startmenu"; Description: "Create a Start Menu shortcut"; GroupDescription: "Shortcuts:"\n\n  [Files]\n  ; The single-file framework-dependent exe.\n  Source: "{#PublishDir}\{#AppExeName}"; DestDir: "{app}"; Flags: ignoreversion\n  ; Bundle the runtime installer ONLY if it was fetched; runs silently on demand (see [Run]).\n  Source: "runtime\{#RuntimeInstaller}"; DestDir: "{tmp}"; Flags: deleteafterinstall external skipifsourcedoesntexist; Check: NeedsDotNetRuntime\n\n  [Icons]\n  Name: "{group}\{#AppName}"; Filename: "{app}\{#AppExeName}"; Tasks: startmenu\n  Name: "{group}\Uninstall {#AppName}"; Filename: "{uninstallexe}"; Tasks: startmenu\n\n  [Run]\n  ; Install the .NET Desktop Runtime silently if missing AND we bundled it.\n  Filename: "{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}"; Parameters: "/install /quiet /norestart"; \\n      StatusMsg: "Installing the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime..."; \\n      Flags: waituntilterminated; Check: ShouldRunBundledRuntime\n  ; If the runtime is missing and was NOT bundled, open the download page after install.\n  Filename: "{#RuntimeDownloadUrl}"; Description: "Download the required .NET 10 Desktop Runtime"; \\n      Flags: shellexec postinstall skipifsilent; Check: NeedsRuntimeButNotBundled\n\n  [Code]\n  const\n    EnvironmentKey = 'Environment';\n\n  var\n    GBundledRuntimePresent: Boolean;\n\n  { ---- PATH helpers (HKCU\Environment, REG_EXPAND_SZ, idempotent, never setx) ---- }\n\n  function GetPathValue(var Value: string): Boolean;\n  begin\n    Result := RegQueryStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', Value);\n    if not Result then\n      Value := '';\n  end;\n\n  { Returns True if Dir already appears as a whole entry in the ';'-delimited PathList. }\n  function PathContainsDir(const PathList, Dir: string): Boolean;\n  var\n    Hay, Needle: string;\n  begin\n    Hay    := ';' + Uppercase(Trim(PathList)) + ';';\n    Needle := ';' + Uppercase(Trim(Dir)) + ';';\n    Result := Pos(Needle, Hay) > 0;\n  end;\n\n  procedure AddDirToPath(const Dir: string);\n  var\n    PathList, NewPath: string;\n  begin\n    GetPathValue(PathList);\n    if PathContainsDir(PathList, Dir) then\n      exit; { idempotent: already present, do nothing }\n\n    if (PathList = '') then\n      NewPath := Dir\n    else if (Copy(PathList, Length(PathList), 1) = ';') then\n      NewPath := PathList + Dir\n    else\n      NewPath := PathList + ';' + Dir;\n\n    { REG_EXPAND_SZ so other entries with %VAR% keep expanding. Inno broadcasts\n      WM_SETTINGCHANGE on completion because ChangesEnvironment=yes. }\n    RegWriteExpandStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', NewPath);\n  end;\n\n  procedure RemoveDirFromPath(const Dir: string);\n  var\n    PathList, Rebuilt, Part: string;\n    P: Integer;\n  begin\n    if not GetPathValue(PathList) then\n      exit;\n\n    Rebuilt := '';\n    PathList := PathList + ';';\n    repeat\n      P := Pos(';', PathList);\n      Part := Trim(Copy(PathList, 1, P - 1));\n      PathList := Copy(PathList, P + 1, Length(PathList));\n      if (Part <> '') and (Uppercase(Part) <> Uppercase(Trim(Dir))) then\n      begin\n        if Rebuilt = '' then\n          Rebuilt := Part\n        else\n          Rebuilt := Rebuilt + ';' + Part;\n      end;\n    until PathList = '';\n\n    RegWriteExpandStringValue(HKEY_CURRENT_USER, EnvironmentKey, 'Path', Rebuilt);\n  end;\n\n  { ---- .NET 10 Desktop Runtime detection ---- }\n\n  { True if a Microsoft.WindowsDesktop.App 10.x shared framework folder exists. }\n  function IsDotNet10DesktopRuntimeInstalled(): Boolean;\n  var\n    FindRec: TFindRec;\n    BaseDir: string;\n  begin\n    Result := False;\n    { Per-machine x64 install location. dotnet.exe also resolves it via PATH, but the\n      shared framework folder is the reliable, no-process probe. }\n    BaseDir := ExpandConstant('{commonpf64}\dotnet\shared\Microsoft.WindowsDesktop.App');\n    if not DirExists(BaseDir) then\n      exit;\n\n    if FindFirst(BaseDir + '\10.*', FindRec) then\n    try\n      repeat\n        if (FindRec.Attributes and FILE_ATTRIBUTE_DIRECTORY) <> 0 then\n        begin\n          Result := True;\n          break;\n        end;\n      until not FindNext(FindRec);\n    finally\n      FindClose(FindRec);\n    end;\n  end;\n\n  function NeedsDotNetRuntime(): Boolean;\n  begin\n    Result := not IsDotNet10DesktopRuntimeInstalled();\n  end;\n\n  { True only when the runtime is missing AND the bundled installer made it onto disk. }\n  function ShouldRunBundledRuntime(): Boolean;\n  begin\n    Result := NeedsDotNetRuntime() and GBundledRuntimePresent;\n  end;\n\n  { True when the runtime is missing but no bundle was shipped (open download page). }\n  function NeedsRuntimeButNotBundled(): Boolean;\n  begin\n    Result := NeedsDotNetRuntime() and (not GBundledRuntimePresent);\n  end;\n\n  { ---- Wizard wiring ---- }\n\n  procedure InitializeWizard();\n  begin\n    { Record whether the bundle was compiled into this setup (source existed at compile time\n      AND extracted to {tmp}). We approximate "shipped" by checking the source file existed;\n      the [Files] 'skipifsourcedoesntexist' flag handles the compile-time-absent case. }\n    GBundledRuntimePresent := FileExists(ExpandConstant('{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}'));\n  end;\n\n  procedure CurStepChanged(CurStep: TSetupStep);\n  begin\n    if CurStep = ssPostInstall then\n    begin\n      { Re-evaluate after [Files] extraction so the {tmp} probe is accurate. }\n      GBundledRuntimePresent := FileExists(ExpandConstant('{tmp}\{#RuntimeInstaller}'));\n      if WizardIsTaskSelected('addtopath') then\n        AddDirToPath(ExpandConstant('{app}'));\n    end;\n  end;\n\n  procedure CurUninstallStepChanged(CurUninstallStep: TUninstallStep);\n  begin\n    if CurUninstallStep = usUninstall then\n      RemoveDirFromPath(ExpandConstant('{app}'));\n  end;\n  ```\n\n  > Notes for the engineer:\n  > - The `[Files]` line for the runtime uses `skipifsourcedoesntexist`, so the installer still compiles even when `installer/runtime/` is empty (CI without the bundle). In that case `GBundledRuntimePresent` is false and, if the runtime is missing, the post-install step opens the Microsoft download page.\n  > - `RegWriteExpandStringValue` writes `REG_EXPAND_SZ` — the correct PATH type. We never call `setx` (which truncates at 1024 chars).\n  > - `ChangesEnvironment=yes` is what makes Inno broadcast `WM_SETTINGCHANGE`, so freshly opened terminals see the new PATH without a logoff.\n  > - `SetupIconFile` points at `src/GitDelta.UI/Assets/gitdelta.ico`. If the icon asset does not yet exist from an earlier UI phase, either add a 256x256 `gitdelta.ico` there or temporarily comment out the `SetupIconFile` and `UninstallDisplayIcon` lines to compile — but the icon is expected to exist before release.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Create the installer build script.**\n  This orchestrates: publish → fetch runtime → compile installer. Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`:\n\n  ```powershell\n  #Requires -Version 7.0\n  <#\n  .SYNOPSIS\n    End-to-end installer build: publish gitdelta.exe, fetch the bundled runtime, compile GitDelta.iss.\n  .DESCRIPTION\n    Output: installer\Output\GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe\n  #>\n  [CmdletBinding()]\n  param(\n      [switch] $SkipRuntimeBundle,\n      [string] $IsccPath = 'C:\Program Files (x86)\Inno Setup 6\ISCC.exe'\n  )\n\n  $ErrorActionPreference = 'Stop'\n  $repoRoot   = Split-Path -Parent $PSScriptRoot\n  $issFile    = Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/GitDelta.iss'\n\n  # 1) Publish the single-file exe.\n  & (Join-Path $PSScriptRoot 'publish.ps1')\n\n  # 2) Fetch the bundled .NET Desktop Runtime (unless skipped, e.g. CI that relies on download page).\n  if (-not $SkipRuntimeBundle) {\n      & (Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/fetch-runtime.ps1')\n  }\n  else {\n      Write-Host "Skipping runtime bundle (installer will open the download page if runtime is missing)." -ForegroundColor Yellow\n  }\n\n  # 3) Compile the installer.\n  if (-not (Test-Path $IsccPath)) {\n      throw "Inno Setup compiler not found at '$IsccPath'. Install Inno Setup 6 or pass -IsccPath."\n  }\n  Write-Host "Compiling installer: $issFile" -ForegroundColor Cyan\n  & $IsccPath $issFile\n  if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) {\n      throw "ISCC.exe failed with exit code $LASTEXITCODE"\n  }\n\n  $out = Get-ChildItem (Join-Path $repoRoot 'installer/Output') -Filter '*-setup.exe' |\n         Sort-Object LastWriteTime -Descending | Select-Object -First 1\n  Write-Host "OK: $($out.FullName) ($([math]::Round($out.Length/1MB,1)) MB)" -ForegroundColor Green\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Compile-verify the installer (MANUAL).**\n  This is a manual verification — installer compilation cannot be unit-tested. From the repo root:\n\n  ```powershell\n  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1\n  ```\n\n  **Expected:** publish succeeds, the runtime download completes (or is skipped), and `ISCC.exe` prints `Successful compile` ending with the output path. Confirm the artifact:\n\n  ```powershell\n  Get-ChildItem C:/code/projects/GitDelta/installer/Output | Select-Object Name, Length\n  ```\n\n  **Expected to observe:** `GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe` exists. If you bundled the runtime its size will be large (~50–70 MB); without the bundle (`-SkipRuntimeBundle`) it will be ~5–15 MB. If `ISCC.exe` reports a missing `SetupIconFile`, address the icon per the Step 2 note before continuing.\n\n- [x] **Step 5: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add installer/GitDelta.iss installer/runtime/.gitkeep installer/fetch-runtime.ps1 build/make-installer.ps1\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  build: add Inno Setup per-user installer with PATH + .NET runtime detection\n\n  - installer/GitDelta.iss: PrivilegesRequired=lowest, install to\n    {localappdata}\Programs\GitDelta, ChangesEnvironment=yes.\n  - Idempotent HKCU\Environment\Path append (REG_EXPAND_SZ) via Pascal, removed on\n    uninstall; never uses setx.\n  - Start Menu shortcut + automatic Add/Remove Programs entry.\n  - Detect .NET 10 Desktop Runtime; run bundled silent installer or open download page.\n  - fetch-runtime.ps1 + make-installer.ps1 orchestration.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Task 11.3: Document distribution, SmartScreen, and PATH usage in the README\n\n**Files:**\n- Modify (or Create if absent): `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md`\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Read the existing README (if any).**\n  Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md`. If it does not exist, create it with the full content in Step 2. If it exists, append the `## Installation` and `## Using the `gitdelta` command` sections from Step 2 after the project intro (do not duplicate an existing title).\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Write the Installation & usage documentation.**\n  Put this content into `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md` (full file shown; if the file already exists, merge the two new `##` sections in rather than overwriting your existing intro):\n\n  ```markdown\n  # GitDelta\n\n  GitDelta is a lightweight, native Windows 11 **read-only** Git diff and commit viewer.\n  Inspect uncommitted changes, what a single commit introduced, or the diff between any two\n  commits — in a modern Fluent UI. It is not a full Git client (no staging, committing, or\n  pushing); it only visualizes.\n\n  ## Installation\n\n  GitDelta is distributed as a **per-user installer** via\n  [GitHub Releases](https://github.com/mortenbrudvik/GitDelta/releases). Download\n  `GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe` and run it. No administrator rights are required — GitDelta\n  installs to `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` for the current user only.\n\n  The installer will:\n\n  - Install `gitdelta.exe`.\n  - Add the install folder to your **per-user PATH** so you can run `gitdelta` from any terminal.\n  - Create a Start Menu shortcut and an entry in **Settings → Apps → Installed apps** (for clean uninstall).\n  - Detect the **.NET 10 Desktop Runtime** and, if it is missing, either install the bundled\n    runtime silently or open the Microsoft download page.\n\n  ### "Windows protected your PC" / SmartScreen warning\n\n  GitDelta v1 is **not code-signed**. When you run the installer, Microsoft Defender SmartScreen\n  may show **"Windows protected your PC — Unknown publisher"**. This is expected for unsigned\n  software and does not indicate a problem with the download.\n\n  To proceed:\n\n  1. Click **More info**.\n  2. Click **Run anyway**.\n\n  If you prefer, verify the download first: each GitHub Release lists the SHA-256 checksum of the\n  installer. Compare it with:\n\n  ```powershell\n  Get-FileHash .\GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe -Algorithm SHA256\n  ```\n\n  ### Prerequisites\n\n  - **Windows 11** (x64).\n  - **.NET 10 Desktop Runtime** — the installer adds it for you if missing.\n  - **Git for Windows ≥ 2.30** on your PATH. GitDelta shells out to the `git` CLI; if git is not\n    found it shows an actionable screen linking the Git for Windows download. Install via\n    `winget install Git.Git` or from https://git-scm.com/download/win.\n\n  ## Using the `gitdelta` command\n\n  After installing (and **opening a new terminal** so the updated PATH takes effect), run:\n\n  | Command | What it does |\n  |---|---|\n  | `gitdelta` | Opens the repository in the current folder at the **working-tree-vs-HEAD** view. |\n  | `gitdelta <path>` | Opens the repository at `<path>` at the working-tree-vs-HEAD view. |\n  | `gitdelta` (outside a repo) | Opens the **start screen** with an "Open folder" picker. |\n  | `gitdelta --version` | Prints the version to the terminal and exits. |\n  | `gitdelta --help` | Prints usage to the terminal and exits. |\n\n  > **New PATH not picked up?** The installer broadcasts a system message so freshly opened\n  > terminals see the updated PATH immediately. Terminals that were already open before installing\n  > will **not** see `gitdelta` until you open a new one. (Bare `gitdelta` resolves via PATH;\n  > `cmd` and PowerShell do not consult Windows "App Paths", which is why the installer edits PATH.)\n\n  ## Uninstalling\n\n  Uninstall from **Settings → Apps → Installed apps → GitDelta → Uninstall**, or via the\n  "Uninstall GitDelta" Start Menu shortcut. Uninstalling removes the install folder **and** the\n  PATH entry it added.\n\n  ## Building from source\n\n  ```powershell\n  # Restore, build (zero warnings — TreatWarningsAsErrors), and test.\n  dotnet build C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln -c Release\n  dotnet test  C:/code/projects/GitDelta/GitDelta.sln\n\n  # Produce the single-file gitdelta.exe in .\publish\\n  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/publish.ps1\n\n  # Build the full installer (publish + bundle runtime + compile Inno Setup)\n  pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1\n  ```\n\n  Building the installer requires [Inno Setup 6](https://jrsoftware.org/isdl.php)\n  (`winget install JRSoftware.InnoSetup`).\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Verify the README renders (MANUAL).**\n  This is a manual prose verification. Open `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/README.md` in a Markdown previewer (VS Code: `Ctrl+Shift+V`). **Confirm:** the SmartScreen "More info → Run anyway" steps are present, the `gitdelta` command table renders, the "open a new terminal" note is present, and all fenced code blocks have language hints and close correctly.\n\n- [x] **Step 4: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add README.md\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  docs: document installation, SmartScreen note, and gitdelta PATH usage\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### Task 11.4: End-to-end packaging verification checklist (clean Win11)\n\n**Files:**\n- Create: `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/docs/release-verification.md`\n\nThis task is entirely **manual verification** — there is nothing to unit-test. It produces a repeatable checklist used before publishing each GitHub Release, ideally run on a clean Windows 11 VM (or a freshly-reset user profile) that does **not** already have the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime or `gitdelta` on PATH.\n\n- [x] **Step 1: Write the release verification checklist.**\n  Create `C:/code/projects/GitDelta/docs/release-verification.md`:\n\n  ```markdown\n  # GitDelta — Release Verification Checklist\n\n  Run this before publishing a GitHub Release. Prefer a **clean Windows 11 x64 VM** (or a fresh\n  user profile) so runtime detection and the PATH broadcast are genuinely exercised.\n\n  ## A. Build artifacts (build machine)\n\n  - [ ] `pwsh -File build/publish.ps1` succeeds; `publish/gitdelta.exe` exists and is ~5–15 MB.\n  - [ ] `publish/` contains no per-app managed `*.dll` siblings (single-file bundling confirmed).\n  - [ ] `& publish/gitdelta.exe --version` prints the expected version and exits without a window.\n  - [ ] `pwsh -File build/make-installer.ps1` produces `installer/Output/GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe`.\n\n  ## B. Clean-machine install (test VM WITHOUT .NET 10 runtime and WITHOUT gitdelta on PATH)\n\n  - [ ] Copy `GitDelta-<version>-setup.exe` to the clean VM and run it (standard, non-admin user).\n  - [ ] SmartScreen shows "Unknown publisher"; **More info → Run anyway** proceeds (matches README).\n  - [ ] Installer runs **without a UAC elevation prompt** (per-user install).\n  - [ ] If the bundled runtime is present: installer shows "Installing the .NET 10 Desktop Runtime..."\n        and completes; if not bundled: the .NET download page opens at the end.\n  - [ ] App installs to `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` and `gitdelta.exe` is present there.\n  - [ ] A **Start Menu** "GitDelta" shortcut exists and launches the app to the start screen.\n  - [ ] **Settings → Apps → Installed apps** lists "GitDelta" with the correct version/publisher.\n\n  ## C. PATH integration (test VM)\n\n  - [ ] Open a **brand-new** PowerShell window after install (do not reuse a pre-install terminal).\n  - [ ] `gitdelta --version` prints the version (resolves via PATH).\n  - [ ] `gitdelta --help` prints usage to the terminal.\n  - [ ] `gitdelta --version > out.txt` writes the version to the file (redirection works).\n  - [ ] In a folder that IS a git repo, run `gitdelta` → app opens to **working-tree-vs-HEAD**.\n  - [ ] In a folder that is NOT a git repo, run `gitdelta` → app opens to the **start screen**.\n  - [ ] `gitdelta <path-to-repo>` opens that repo's working-tree view.\n  - [ ] Inspect the PATH entry is a single, non-duplicated value:\n        `(Get-ItemProperty 'HKCU:\Environment' Path).Path` contains `...\Programs\GitDelta` exactly once.\n\n  ## D. Idempotent re-install (test VM)\n\n  - [ ] Run the installer a second time over the existing install; it completes cleanly.\n  - [ ] PATH still contains `...\Programs\GitDelta` **exactly once** (no duplicate appended).\n\n  ## E. Uninstall (test VM)\n\n  - [ ] Uninstall via Settings → Apps (or the Start Menu "Uninstall GitDelta" shortcut).\n  - [ ] `%LOCALAPPDATA%\Programs\GitDelta` is removed.\n  - [ ] Open a new terminal: `gitdelta` is no longer found (PATH entry removed).\n        Confirm: `(Get-ItemProperty 'HKCU:\Environment' Path).Path` no longer contains the GitDelta dir.\n\n  ## F. Git-missing path (optional, test VM without Git for Windows)\n\n  - [ ] Launch GitDelta with git absent → the actionable "Git not installed" screen appears with a\n        link to Git for Windows (per the spec's startup git detection).\n\n  Only publish the release once every box in A–E passes.\n  ```\n\n- [x] **Step 2: Execute the checklist once (MANUAL) and record results.**\n  Spin up (or reset) a clean Windows 11 x64 VM. Build the installer on your dev machine with `pwsh -File C:/code/projects/GitDelta/build/make-installer.ps1`, copy `installer/Output/GitDelta-1.0.0-setup.exe` to the VM, and walk through sections **A–E** of `docs/release-verification.md`, ticking each box. **Expected:** every box in A–E passes. Pay special attention to:\n  - **C — new terminal:** the most common failure is testing PATH in a terminal opened *before* install; always open a fresh one.\n  - **D — idempotency:** re-running the installer must not add a second `...\Programs\GitDelta` to PATH (this validates the `PathContainsDir` guard in `GitDelta.iss`).\n  - **E — uninstall:** the PATH entry must be gone afterward (validates `RemoveDirFromPath`).\n\n  If any box fails, fix the relevant script/`GitDelta.iss` from Task 11.1/11.2, rebuild, and re-run the affected section before committing.\n\n- [x] **Step 3: Commit.**\n\n  ```powershell\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta add docs/release-verification.md\n  git -C C:/code/projects/GitDelta commit -m @'\n  docs: add clean-Win11 release verification checklist for packaging\n\n  Covers single-file publish, per-user install without admin, SmartScreen flow,\n  .NET 10 runtime detection, PATH add (new-terminal) / idempotent re-install / removal\n  on uninstall, and the gitdelta CLI fast-paths.\n\n  Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.8 (1M context) <noreply@anthropic.com>\n  '@\n  ```\n```\n\n
